 yad pada ambhoruha dhyāna vidhvasta aśeṣa kalmaṣaḥ vastu tām upayātaḥ aham yāmunā iyam namāmi tam śriyaḥ patiḥ nikhila pratyanīka kalyāṇa tānaḥ samasta vastu ananta jñana svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya balāi śvarya vīrya prabhṛti saṃkhyeya kalyāṇa gaṇa mahā udadhiḥ abhim ata acintya divya adbhuta niravadya niratiśayāujjvalya saundarya saugandhya saukumārī lāvaṇya yauvana ucita vividha vicitra ananta āścarya niravadya parimita divya bhūṣaṇaḥ rūpā saṃkhyeya acintya niravadya niratiśaya kalyāṇa divya āyudhaḥ abhim ata anurūpa niravadya vibhavāi śvarya śīla ana vadhika atiśaya saṃkhyeya kalyāṇa gaṇa śr saṅkalpa vidhāyi pravṛtti aśeṣa seṣatā rati niravadya niratiśaya kriyāiśvarya anavarata abhiṣṭuta yugalaḥ manasā paricchedya svabhāvaḥ ucita vividha vicitra ananta bhogya upakaraṇa samṛddha ananta āḥ caryā ananta mahā vibhava ananta parimāṇa nity vividha vicitra ananta bhogya varga paripūrṇa nikhila udaya vibhava laya līlaḥ puruṣottamaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ sthāvara antam akhilam sṛṣṭvā rūpeṇa avasthitaḥ manuṣyāṇām dhyāna ārādhana gocaraḥ apāra ka aruṇya sauśīlya vātsalī auu dārya mahā udadhiḥ svam rūpam sajātīya saṃsthānam svabhāvam ajahad kurvan teṣu teṣu iṣu avatīrya avatīrya taiḥ taiḥ ārādhitaḥ anurūpam ākhyam prayacchan bhāra ava tāraṇa apadeśena asmad ādīnām samāśrayaṇīya tvāya avatīrya urvyām sakalam anuja nayana viṣaya tām gataḥ parāvara nikhila jana nayana hāri divya ceṣṭitāni kurvan pūta nāśa kaṭaya mala arjuna ariṣṭa pralamba dhenu ka kāli ya keśi kuvalaya āpīḍa cāṇūra muṣṭika tosala kaṃsa ādīn nihatya anavadhika dayā sauhārda anurāga garbha avalokana ālāpa mṛtaiḥ viśvam āpyāyayan niratiśaya saundarya sauśīlya gaṇa viṣkāreṇa akrūra mālā ākāra ādīn parama bhāgavatān kṛtvā pāṇḍu tanaya yuddha protsāhana vyājena parama sādhana uditam viṣayam anugṛhītam bhakti avatārayām āsa pāṇḍavānām kurūṇām yuddhe prārabdhe bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ īśvara īśvaraḥ upakṛti martyaḥ vātsalya vivaśaḥ pārtham rathinam ātmānam sārathim sākṣikam cakāra jñātvā andhaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ suyodhana vijaya bubhutsayā sañjayam papraccha duryodhanaḥ svayam bhīma abhirakṣitam pāṇḍavānām balam ātmīyam bhīṣma abhirakṣitam balam avalokya vijaye balasya paryāpta tām ātmīyasya balasya vijaye parya āpta tām ācāryāya nivedya viṣaṇṇaḥ abhavat viṣādam ālakṣya bhīṣmaḥ harṣam janayitum siṃhanādam śaṅkha dhmānam kṛtvā śaṅkha bherī ninādaiḥ vijaya abhiśaṃsinam ghoṣam akārayat tataḥ tam ghoṣam ākarṇya īśvara īśvaraḥ pārtha sārathī rathī pāṇḍu tanayaḥ trailokya vijaya upakaraṇa bhūte mahati syandane sthitau trailokyam kampayantau śrīmat pāñcajanya devadattau divyau śaṅkhau pradadhmatuḥ tataḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vṛkodara svakīyān śaṅkhān pradadhmuḥ ghoṣaḥ duryodhana pramukhānām bhavat putrāṇām hṛdayāni bibheda adya iva naṣṭam kurūṇām balam dhārtarāṣṭrā menire vijayā abhikāṅkṣiṇe dhṛtarāṣṭrāya sañjayaḥ akathayat yuyutsūn avasthitān dhārtarāṣṭrān dṛṣṭvā laṅkā dahana vānara dhvajaḥ pāṇḍu tanayaḥ balāi śvarya vīrya tejasām nidhim saṅkalpa udaya vibhava laya līlam hṛṣīkeśam parāvara nikhila jana bāhya karaṇānām prakāra niyamane avasthitam vātsalī vivaśa sārathye avasthitam yuyutsūn yathāvat avekṣitum īkṣana kṣame sthāne ratham sthāpaya acodayat tena coditaḥ kṣaṇāt bhhīṣma ḍroṇa ādīnām mahīkṣitām paśyatām coditam akarot īdṛśī bhavadīyānām vijaya sthitiḥ avocat pārthaḥ mahāmanāḥ parama kāruṇikaḥ bandhuḥ parama dhārmikaḥ bhrātṛkaḥ bhavadbhiḥ ghoraiḥ māraṇaiḥ jatu gṛha dāha ādibhiḥ vañcitaḥ parama sahāyena haniṣya māṇān bhavadīyān vilokya bandhu snehena parayā kṛpayā bhayena sanna gātraḥ aham yotsyāmi uktvā bandhu viśleṣa janita śoka saṃvigna mānasaḥ śaram cāpam visṛjya rathopastha upāviśat upaviṣṭe pārthe kutaḥ ayam asthāne samupasthitaḥ śoka ākṣipya tam imam viṣama stham śokam avidvat sevitam virodhinam akīrti karam kṣudram hṛdaya daurbalya kṛtam parityajya yuddhāya uttiṣṭha śrī bhagavān uvāca punar pārthaḥ sneha kāruṇya bhaya ākulaḥ bhagavat hitatamam ajānan idam uvāca bhīṣma droṇa ādikān gurūn bahu mantavyān katham aham haniṣyāmi kathaṃtarām iṣu atimātra saktān tān hatvā taiḥ bhujyamānān tān bhogān rudhireṇa upasicya teṣu āsaneṣu upaviśya bhuñjīya yuddham ārabhya nivṛtta vyāpārān bhavataḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ prasahya hanyuḥ vadha labdha vijayāt adharmyāt asmākam adharmau ajānadbhiḥ taiḥ hananam garīya me pratibhāti uktvā yad mahyam śreya niścitam śaraṇa āgatāya tava śiṣyāya me brūhi atimātra kṛpaṇaḥ bhagavat pādau upasasāda asthāne samupasthita sneha kāruṇyābhyām aprakṛtim gatam kṣatriyāṇām yuddham parama adharmam manvānam bubhutsayā śaraṇa āgatam pārtham uddiśya yāthātmya jñānena yuddhasya abhisandhirahitasya prāpti upāyatā jñānena vinā mohaḥ śāmyati matvā bhagavatā parama puruṣeṇa avataraṇam kṛtam sneha kāruṇya dhiyā ākulam pārtham prapannam uddiśya avataraṇam kṛtam ūr yāthātmya ajñāna śoka āviṣṭam atirikta nimittam bhāṣamāṇam paraspara viruddha anvitam senayoḥ yuddhāya udyuktayoḥ madhye akasmāt nirudyogam pārtham ālokya parama puruṣaḥ prahasan iva idam uvāca parihāsa vākyam vadan iva paramātma yāthātmya prāpti upāya yoga yoga bhakti yoga gocaram aham jātu sam ārabhya aham tvā pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ etad antam vacanam uvāca aśocyān anuśocasi patanti pitaraḥ eṣām lupta piṇḍa uda ka kriyāḥ ādikān svabhāva vāda bhāṣase svabhāva jñānavatām atra kiṃcid choka nimittam gatāsūn dehān agatāsūn svabhāva yāthātmya śocanti ataḥ tvayi vipratiṣiddham idam yad etān haniṣyāmi anuśocanam yad atirikta kṛtam adharma bhāṣaṇam ataḥ svabhāvam jānāsi atiriktam ātmānam prāpti upāya yuddha ādikam idam yuddham abhisandhi rahitam ātmayāthātmya avāpti upāya sadbhāvaḥ maraṇa vināśa ḥ maraṇayoḥ ataḥ śoka sthānam dehaḥ acetanaḥ pariṇāma svabhāvaḥ vināśa svābhāvika śoka sthānam abhiprāyaḥ prathamam tāvat ātmanām svabhāvam śṛṇu aham īśvara ḥ tāvat ataḥ vartamānāt pūrvasmin anādau kāle nāsam āsam tvad mukhāḥ īśitavyāḥ kṣetrajñāḥ nāsam āsan aham yūyam vayam ataḥ parasmin anante kāle iva bhaviṣyāmaḥ bhaviṣyāma aham īśvaraḥ paramātmā atra saṃśayaḥ bhavantaḥ kṣetrajñā ātmānaḥ nityā mantavyāḥ bhagavataḥ īśvara āt atmanām parasparam bhedaḥ pāramārthika bhagavatā pratīyate ajñāna mohitam nivṛttaye pārma arthika samaye aham vayam aupacārika vāde bhedasya tāttvika tattva samaye nirdeśaḥ saṃgacchate bhagavat ukta bhedaḥ svābhāvika śrutiḥ nityaḥ nityānām cetanaḥ cetanānām ekaḥ bahūnām yaḥ vidadhāti kāmān nityānām bahūnām cetanānām ya ekaḥ nityaḥ cetanaḥ san kāmān vidadhāti ajñāna vāde parama puruṣasya parama dṛṣteḥ nirviśeṣa kūṭa caitanya yāthātmya sākṣātkārān nivṛtta ajñāna ajñāna vyavahārāḥ saṃgacchante parama puruṣasya adhigata at va eta jñānasya bādhita anuvṛtti rūpam idam jñānam dagdha van bandhakam ucyate etad marīcikā jala ādikam bādhitam anuvartamānam jala āharaṇa pravṛtti hetuḥ atra advaita jñānena bādhitam jñānam anuvartamānam mithyā viṣaya niścayān pravṛtti hetuḥ bhavati īśvarasya ajñasya adhigata tattva bādhita anuvṛttiḥ śakyate vaktum yaḥ sarvajñaḥ vit parāsya śaktiḥ vividhā śrūyate svābhāvikī bala veda aham samatītāni vartamānāni arjuna bhaviṣyāṇi bhūtāni mām veda kaścana kim parama puruṣaḥ idānīṃtana guru paramparā advitīya niścaye anuvartamāne jñāne niścaya anurūpam advitīya jñānam kasmā upadiśati vaktavyam pratibimbavat pratīyamānebhyaḥ arjuna ādibhya etad anunmattaḥ kaḥ maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa pratīyamāneṣu pratibimbeṣu jānan tebhyaḥ kim upadiśati bādhita anuvṛttiḥ taiḥ śakyate vaktum bādhakena dvitīya jñānena vyatirikta kāraṇasya ana ādeḥ vinaṣṭa dvi candra ādau candra jñānena pāramārthika timira doṣasya dvi candra hetoḥ avinaṣṭa bādhita anuvṛttiḥ yuktā anuvartamānam prabala pramāṇa bādhita akiṃcitkaram jñānasya viṣayasya kāraṇasya pāramārthika vastu yāthātmya vinaṣṭa kathañcid bādhita anuvṛttiḥ saṃbhavati ataḥ īśvarasya idānīṃtana guru paramparāya āḥ tattva jñānam darśana saṃbhavaḥ ajñānasya hetoḥ sthita ena ajña sutarām saṃbhavati kim guroḥ advitīya vijñānāt ajñānasya kāryasya vinaṣṭa śiṣyam praty niṣprayojanaḥ guruḥ jñānam kalpitam śiṣya jñānayoḥ kalpita anivartakam kalpita tve virodhi nivartakam acārya jñāne samānam nivartakam bhavati kṛtam asamīcīnavādaiḥ dehe vartamānasya dehinaḥ kaumāra avasthām vihāya yauvana prāptau sthira buddhyā naṣṭa śocati dehāt prāptau sthira buddhimān śocati ata ātmanām śoka sthānam atra kartavyam ātmanām nityānām ana vaśya ucita saṃsṛṣṭānām taiḥ dehaiḥ nivṛttaye śāstrī iyam varṇa ucitam yuddha ādikam anabhisaṃhita kurvatām avarjanīya indriyaiḥ indriya sparśāḥ śīta uṣṇa prayukta duḥkha dā bhavanti yāvat śāstrī ya samāpti kṣantavyā imam anantaram sparśa rasa gandhāḥ āśrayāḥ tanmātrā mātrā ucyante śrotra ādibhiḥ sparśāḥ śīta uṣṇa mṛdu paruṣa duḥkha dāḥ bhavanti śīta uṣṇa pradarśana tān dhairyeṇa yāvat yuddha śa astrī ya samāpti titikṣasva āgama pāyi dhairyavatām kṣantum yogyāḥ anityāḥ nāśe āgama apāyi vartante kṣamā kimartha atra yam dhairya yuktam avarjanīya duḥkham sukhavan manyamānam sādhana varṇa ucitam yuddha anabhisaṃhita kurvāṇam antargatāḥ śastra pāta mṛdu krūra sparśāḥ vyathayanti sādhayati tvādṛśaḥ duḥkha sahiṣṇuḥ ātmanām atra kartavyam yad ātmanām dehānām svābhāvikam nāśi śoka nimittam gata asūn agatāsu un ḥ anuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ upapādayitum ārabhate dehasya sadbhāvaḥ vidyate sadbhāvaḥ ūr upalabhyamānayoḥ tattva darśibhiḥ antaḥ nirṇaya tvān nirūpaṇasya nirṇaya śabdena ucyate dehasya acit vastunaḥ asattvam svarūpam cetanasya sattvam svarūpam nirṇayaḥ vināśa svabhāvaḥ asattvam avināśa svabhāva ḥ sattvam bhagavatā parāśareṇa tasmāt vijñānam ṛte kiṃcid kvacid kadācid dvija vastu jātam sadbhāva bhavataḥ mayā uktaḥ jñānam satyam asatyam anyat anāśī parama ḥ prājñaiḥ abhyupagamyate nāśi saṃdehaḥ nāśidra vya upapāditam yad kāla saṃjñām upaiti vai pariṇāma saṃbhūtām vastu nṛpa kim atra antavanta dehāḥ avināśi viddhi ucyate sattva asattva hetuḥ gamyate atra satkārya vādasya prastuta tvān ayam ślokaḥ svabhāva ajñāna mohitasya moha śāntaye nāśi tvā nāśi svabhāva viveka vaktavyaḥ gata asūn agatāsūn prastutaḥ avināśi viddhi antavanta dehāḥ anantaram upapādyate ataḥ ukta avināśi katham avagamyata atra atma tattvam avināśī viddhi yena tattvena cetanena vyatiriktam idam acetana tattvam sarvam tatam vyāptam vyāpaka niratiśaya sūkṣma vināśān arhasya vyatiriktaḥ kaścid padārthaḥ vināśam kartum arhati vyāpi tasmāt sthūla nāśakam śastra jala vāyu ādikam nāśyam vyāpya śithilīkaroti mudrā vegavat saṃyogena utpādya dvāreṇa nāśayanti ata tattvam avināśi dehānām vināśi svabhāva diha upacaye rūpā dehā antavantaḥ vināśa svabhāvāḥ ātmakā ghaṭa antavantaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ nityasya śarīriṇaḥ saṃghāta rūpā dehāḥ puṇyaḥ puṇyena ityādi śāstraiḥ uktāḥ avasāna vināśinaḥ avināśī kutaḥ aprameya prameya pramātṛ vakṣyate etad yaḥ vetti tam prāhuḥ kṣetrajña upalabhayate dehe aham idam jānāmi dehasya anyasya pramātṛ rūpeṇa ādeḥ iva pramātuḥ ākāra ata anupacaya pramātṛ vyāpaka nityaḥ dehaḥ śarīriṇaḥ vyāpya vināśī tasmāt dehasya vināśa svabhāva atmanaḥ ubhayau śoka sthānam śastra pāta sparśān avarjanīyān gatān gatān ghairyeṇa soḍhvā prāptaye anabhisaṃhita yuddha ākhyam ārabhasva ukta svabhāvam ātmānam hantāram hanana hetum kam yaḥ manyate yaḥ kena hetunā hatam manyate tau ubhau vijānītaḥ uktaiḥ hetubhiḥ ayam hanti ayam hanana hetuḥ bhavati ata ayam hanyate hantidhātuḥ karmakaḥ viyoga karaṇa vācī hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtāni brāhmaṇaḥ hantavyaḥ ityādīni śāstrāṇi avihita viyoga karaṇa viṣayāṇi uktaiḥ hetubhiḥ pariṇāmi janana maraṇa cetana dharmā santi ucyate jāyate mriyate vartamāna sarveṣu deheṣu sarvaiḥ anubhūyamāne janana maraṇe kadācid ātmānam spṛśataḥ ayam bhūtvā bhavitā ayam kalpa ādau bhūtvā kalpa ante bhavitā keṣucid prajāpati prabhṛti iṣu āgamena upalabhyamānam kalpa ādau jananam kalpa ante maraṇam ātmānam spṛśati ataḥ gata ajaḥ ata nityaḥ śāśvataḥ prakṛtivat viśada satata pariṇāmaiḥ anvīyate purāṇaḥ purā navaḥ sarvadā apūrvavat anubhāvya ataḥ hanyamāne hanyate ayam avināśi aja vyayān ātmānam yaḥ puruṣaḥ veda puruṣaḥ tiryak sthāvara avasthiteṣu ātmasu kam ātmānam katham ghātayati kam katham hanti katham nāśayati katham prayojakaḥ bhavati etān ghātayāmi hanmi anuśocanam yāthātmya ajñāna mūlam abhiprāyaḥ yadi nityānām ātmanām viśleṣa kriyate ramaṇīya sādhaneṣu śarīreṣu naśyatsu viyoga rūpam śoka nimittam atra yuddhe tyajatām tyakta śarīrāt adhikatara kalyāṇa grahaṇam ād avagamyata jīrṇāni vāsāṃsi vihāya navāni kalyāṇāni vāsāṃsi gṛhṇatām iva harṣa nimittam atra punar avināśi viddhi yena sarvam idam tatam avināśi grahaṇāya vyañjayan draḍhayati śastra vāyavaḥ chedana dahana kleda śoṣaṇāni ātmānam kartum śaknuvanti gata tattva vyāpana svabhāvatayā sarvebhyaḥ tattvebhyaḥ sūkṣma taiḥ anarha vyāpya kartavya chedana dahana kleda śoṣaṇānām ata nityaḥ sthāṇuḥ acalaḥ ayam sanātanaḥ sthira svabhāvaḥ aprakampyaḥ purātanaḥ chedana yogyāni vastūni yaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ vyajyante taiḥ ayam vyajyata avyaktaḥ ataḥ chedya visajātīyaḥ acintya ḥ vastu vijātīya svabhāva yukta cintayitum arhaḥ ataḥ vikāryaḥ vikārān arhaḥ tasmāt ukta lakṣaṇam ātmānam viditvā kṛte śocitum arhasi jātam mṛtam deham ātmānam manuṣe atiriktam ukta lakṣaṇam atimātram śocitum arhasi pariṇāma svabhāvasya dehasya vināśayoḥ avarjanīya utpannasya vināśaḥ dhruvaḥ avarjanīya vinaṣṭasya avarjanīyam katham idam vinaṣṭasya utpattiḥ sata vināśa dravyasya viśeṣāḥ tantu prabhṛtīni dravyāṇi santi yuktāni ādīni ucyante vādinā tantu saṃsthāna atirekeṇa dravya antaram pratīyate kāraka bhajana vyavahāra viśeṣāṇām etāvatā dravya yuktā ataḥ vināśa dravyasya viśeṣāḥ ākhyām avasthām upayātasya dravyasya virodhi vināśa ucyate mṛd dravyasya piṇḍa ghaṭa kapāla cūrṇa ādivat pariṇāmi dravyasya pariṇāma paramparā avarjanīyā avasthasya dravyasya vināśaḥ iva avasthasya utpattiḥ vināśa ākhya pariṇāma paramparā pariṇāminaḥ dravyasya parihārya śocitum arhasi dravyasya virodhi prāpti darśanena yaḥ alpīyān śokaḥ saṃbhavati ādīni bhūtāni santi dravyāṇi anupalabdha avasthāni upalabdha madhyama avasthāni anupalabdha avasthāni sveṣu svabhāveṣu vartanta paridevanā nimittam vāde śoka nimittam uktvā atirikte āścarya svarūpe draṣṭā vaktā āyatta niścayaḥ durlabha ukta svabhāvam samasta vastu visajātīya āścaryavat asthitam ananteṣu jantuṣu mahatā tapasā kṣīṇa pāpaḥ upacita puṇyaḥ kaścid paśyati tathāvidhaḥ kaścid parasmai kaścid śṛṇoti śrutvā yathāvat avasthitam tattvataḥ kaścid veda cakāra at draṣṭṛ vaktṛ śrotṛṣv tattvataḥ tattvataḥ vacanam tattvata ḥ śravaṇam durlabham bhavati sarvasya dehinaḥ dehe vadhyamāne ayam dehī avadhyaḥ mantavyaḥ tasmāt sthāvara antāni bhūtāni viṣama ākārāṇi uktena svabhāvena svarūpataḥ samānāni nityāni gatam vaiṣamyam anitya tataḥ ādīni bhūtāni uddiśya śocitum arhasi kevalam bhīṣma ādīn idam prārabdham yuddham prāṇi māraṇam agnīṣomīya ādivat svadharmam avekṣya vikampitum arhasi dharmyān nyāyataḥ pravṛttāt yuddhāt anyan kṣatriyasya śreyaḥ vidyate śauryam dhṛtiḥ dākṣyam yuddhe apalāyanam dānam īśvara kṣātram svabhāva jam vakṣyate agnīṣomīya hiṃsā paśoḥ nihīna tara chāga parityāga kalyāṇatara svarga prāpaka saṃjñapanasya etad mriyase riṣyasi devām ideṣi pathibhiḥ surebhiḥ yanti sukṛtaḥ duṣkṛtaḥ tvā devaḥ savitā dadhātu śrūyate yuddhe mṛtānām kalyāṇatara uktā vāsāṃsi jīrṇāni vihāya navāni gṛhṇāti ityādinā ataḥ cikitsaka śalya āturasya iva rakṣaṇam agnīṣomīya saṃjñapanam ayatna upanatam idam niratiśaya upāya nirvighnam īdṛśam yuddham sukhinaḥ puṇyavantaḥ kṣatriyā labhante kṣatriyasya svadharma imam ārabdham saṃgrāmam mohān kariṣyasi tataḥ prārabdhasya dharmasya akaraṇāt svadharma niratiśaya sukham vijayena niratiśayām kīrtim hitvā pāpam niratiśayam avāpsyasi kevalam niratiśaya kīrti hāni pārthaḥ yuddhe prārabdhe palāyitaḥ avyayām deśa kāla vyāpinīm akīrtim samarthāni asamarthāni bhūtāni kathayiṣyanti tataḥ kim śairya vīrya parākrama ādibhiḥ saṃbhāvitasya viparyaya jā akīrtiḥ maraṇāt atiricyate evaṃvidhāyā akīrteḥ maraṇam tava śreya bandhu snehāt kāruṇyāt yuddhān nivṛttasya śūrasya mama kīrtiḥ katham āgamiṣyati atra yeṣām karṇa duryodhana ādīnām mahā rathānām itaḥ śūraḥ vairī bahu mataḥ bhūtvā idānīm yuddhe samupasthite nivṛtta lāghavam sugraha tām yāsyasi mahā ratha aḥ tvām bhayāt yuddhāt uparatam maṃsyante śūrāṇām vairiṇām śatru bhayāt rte bandhu sneha yuddhāt uparatiḥ kim śūrāṇām asmākam sannidhau katham ayam pārthaḥ kṣaṇam sthātum śaknuyāt asmad sannidhānāt sāmarthyam tava sāmarthyam nindantaḥ śūrāṇām avācya vādān bahūn vadiṣyanti tava śatravaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ tataḥ adhikataram duḥkham kim tava evaṃvidha avācya śravaṇān maraṇam śreya maṃsyase ataḥ śūrasya pareṣām hananam paraiḥ hananam ubhayam śreyase bhavati yuddhe paraiḥ hata ḥ tataḥ parama niḥśreyasam prāpsyasi parān hatvā akaṇṭakam rājyam bhokṣyase anabhisaṃhita phalasya yuddha ākhyasya dharmasya parama niḥśreyasa upāya parama niḥśreyasam prāpsyasi tasmāt yuddhāya udyogaḥ parama sādhanam niścitya uttiṣṭha kuntī putrasya tava etad yuktam abhiprāyaḥ mumukṣoḥ yuddha anuṣṭhāna prakāram atiriktam aspṛṣṭa samasta svabhāvam ātmānam jñātvā yuddhe auvarjanīya śastra pāta duḥkha lābha ālābha jaya parājayeṣu avikṛta buddhiḥ svarga abhisandhi rahitaḥ kevala buddhyā yuddham ārabhasva kurvāṇaḥ pāpam avāpsyasi pāpam duḥkha rūpam saṃsāram vāpsyasi bandhān mokṣyase yāthātmya jñānam upadiśya pūrvakam sādhana vaktum ārabhate saṅkhyā buddhiḥ buddhyā avadhāraṇīyam tattvam sāṅkhyam jñātavye tattve jñānāya yā buddhiḥ abhidheyā aham ārabhya tasmāt bhūtāni śocitum arhasi eṣā abhihitā sādhana anuṣṭhāne yaḥ vaktavyaḥ yoga śabdena ucyate dūreṇa avaram vakṣyate yoge yā buddhiḥ vaktavyā tām imām abhidhīyamānām śṛṇu yayā buddhyā yuktaḥ bandham prahāsyasi karmaṇā bandhaḥ bandhaḥ vakṣyamāṇa yuktasya karmaṇaḥ māhātmyam yoge abhikrama nāśaḥ abhikramaḥ ārambhaḥ nāśaḥ sādhana nāśaḥ ārabdhasya samāptasya vicchinnasya niṣphala ārabdhasya vicchede pratyavāyaḥ vidyate yoga ākhyasya dharmasya su aṃśa mahataḥ bhayāt bhayāt trāyate ayam pārtha mutra vināśa ḥ vidyate prapañcayiṣyate anyāni laukikāni vaidikāni sādhanāni vicchinnāni phalāya bhavanti pratyavāyāya bhavanti kāmya viṣayāyā buddheḥ sādhana viṣayām buddhim viśinaṣṭi śāstrīye sarvasmin vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ ekā mumukṣuṇā anuṣṭheye buddhiḥ vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ vyavasāyaḥ niścayaḥ buddhiḥ yāthātmya niścaya pūrvikā kāmya viṣayā buddhiḥ avyavasāya ātmikā adhikāre atirikta astitva apekṣitam yāthātmya niścayaḥ yāthātmyā niścaye svarga arthi sādhana anuṣṭhāna anubhavānām iyam vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ sādhana viṣaya ekā ekasmai ākhya phalāya mumukṣoḥ karmāṇi vidhīyante ataḥ arthasya viṣayā buddhiḥ ekā sādhana āgneya ādīnām ṣaṇṇām kartavya tākānām viṣayā buddhiḥ ekā avyavasāyinām svarga paśu anna sādhana adhikṛtānām buddhayaḥ ānantyāt anantāḥ bahu śākhāḥ ekasmai phalāya codite darśa pūrṇam āsa ādau karmaṇiāyuḥ āśāḥ avagata auvāntara bahu śākha vidyate ataḥ avyavasāyinām buddhayaḥ anantā bahu śākhāḥ etad bhavati nityeṣu naimittikeṣu karmasu phalāni avāntara phalāni yāni śrūyamāṇāni parityajya karmāṇi anuṣṭheyāni kāmyāni varṇa āśrama ucitāni phalāni parityajya sādhana naimittikaiḥ ekīkṛtya yathābalam anuṣṭheyāni kāmya adhikṛtān nindati yām imām puṣpitām puṣpa phalām āpāta ramaṇīyām vācam avipaścitaḥ jñāḥ bhogāi śvarya gatim vartamānām pravadanti veda vāda ratāḥ vedeṣu ye svarga vādāḥ teṣu saktāḥ anyat vādinaḥ saṅga atirekeṇa svarga ādeḥ anyat vadantaḥ kām ātmānaḥ kām apravaṇa manasaḥ svarga parāḥ svarga parāyaṇāḥ svarga avasāne punar ākhya pradām bahulām tattva rahita pracurām bhogāi śvarya gatim vartamānām yām imām puṣpitām vācam ye pravadanti saṃbandhaḥ bhogāi śvarya prasaktānām vācā bhogāi śvarya viṣayayā apahṛta jñānānām udita vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ samādhau vidhīyate utpadyate samādhīyate jñānam samādhiḥ yāthātmya niścaya sādhana viṣayā buddhiḥ kadācid utpadyate ataḥ kāmyeṣu karmasu mumukṣuṇā saṅgaḥ kartavyaḥ phalāni punar prasavāni karmāṇi mātā pitṛ sahasrebhyaḥ vatsalatara ujjīvane pravṛttā vedāḥ kim vadanti katham veda uditam tyājya ucyate ata trayaḥ aḥ traiguṇyam sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi sattva rajaḥ tamaḥ pracurāḥ puruṣāḥ traiguṇya śabdena ucyante viṣayā vedāḥ tamaḥ pracurāṇām rajaḥ pracurāṇām sattva pracurāṇām vatsalatara hitam avabodhayanti vedāḥ yadi eṣām anuguṇyena svarga sādhanam hitam avabodhayanti rajaḥ tamaḥ pracura sāttvika vimukhāḥ svāpekṣita sādhanam ajānantaḥ prāvaṇya vivaśā anupādeyeṣu upādeya bhrāntyā praviṣṭāḥ pranaṣṭā bhaveyuḥ ataḥ traiguṇya viṣayā vedāḥ nistraiguṇyaḥ bhava idānīm sattva pracuraḥ vardhaya anyonya saṅkīrṇa traya pracuraḥ bhava prācuryam vardhaya nirdvandvaḥ nirgata sakala sāṃsārika svabhāvaḥ sattva sthaḥ dvaya rahita pravṛddha sattva sthaḥ bhava katham niryogakṣemaḥ prāpti upāya bahi ḥ bhūtānām arthānām prāptānām kṣemam parityajya ātmavān bhava svarūpān veṣaṇa bhava aprāptasya prāptasya parikṣaṇam kṣemaḥ vartamānasya rajaḥ tamaḥ pracura naśyati sattvam vardhate veda uditam sarvam sarvasya upādeyam parikalpite sarvataḥ saṃpluta udake udapāne pipāsoḥ yāvān yāvat prayojanam tāvat tena upādīyate sarvam sarveṣu vedeṣu brāhmaṇasya vijānataḥ vaidikasya mumukṣoḥ yad sādhanam pādeyam anyat ataḥ sattva sthasya mumukṣoḥ upādeyam nitye naimittike kāmye kenacid viśeṣeṇa saṃbandhi śrūyamāṇe sattva sthasya mumukṣoḥ mātre adhikāraḥ saṃbandhi avagateṣu phaleṣu kadācid adhikāraḥ saphalasya rahitasya kevalasya mad ārādhana rūpasya tvāc mā phalayoḥ bhūḥ tvayā anuṣṭhīyamāne sattva sthasya mumukṣoḥ tava akartṛ anusandheyam phalasya kṣut nivṛtti ādeḥ hetuḥ anusandheyam bhayam guṇeṣu īśvare mayi anusandheyam vakṣyate anusandhāya kuru akarmaṇi ananuṣṭhāne yotsyāmi yad tvayā abhihitam saṅgaḥ uktena prakāreṇa yuddha saṅgaḥ etad sphuṭīkaroti rājya bandhu prabhṛtiṣu saṅgam tyaktvā yuddha ādīni karmāṇi yoga sthaḥ kuru antarbhūta vijaya siddhi siddhyoḥ samaḥ bhūtvā kuru idam siddhi asiddhyoḥ sama yoga atra yoga śabdena ucyate siddhi asiddhiyoḥ sama rūpam citta samādhānam kim idam ucyata ata yaḥ ayam tyāga viṣayaḥ avāntara siddhi siddhyoḥ sama viṣaya ḥ yuktāt karmaṇa dūreṇa avaram idam dvayoḥ utkarṣa apakarṣa rūpam vairūpyam ukta yoga yuktam nikhila sāṃsārika duḥkham vinivartya parama lakṣaṇam mokṣam prāpayati aparimita duḥkha rūpam saṃsāram ataḥ kriyamāṇe uktāyām buddhau śaraṇam anviccha śaraṇam vāsasthānam tasyām buddhau vartasva kṛpaṇāḥ hetavaḥ saṅga kurvāṇāḥ kṛpaṇāḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ bhaveyuḥ yoga yukta ḥ kurvāṇaḥ ubhe kāla sañcite anante bhūte jahāti tasmāt uktāya yogāya yujyasva karmasu kauśalam karmasu kriyamāṇa iṣu ayam kauśalam sāmarthyam sāmarthī sādhya yoga yuktāḥ jam tyaktvā kurvantaḥ tasmāt vinirmuktāḥ anāmayam padam gacchanti prasiddham etad asu upaniṣatsu ukta prakāreṇa vartamānasya vṛttyā nirdhūta kalmaṣasya buddhiḥ yadā moha kalilam saṅga moha rūpam kaluṣam vyatitariṣyati asmattaḥ itaḥ tyājya śrutasya ādeḥ itaḥ paścāt śrotavyasya kṛte svayam nirvedam gantāsi gamiṣyasi yoge imām śṛṇu ityādinā uktasya yāthātmya pūrvakasya saṃskṛtasya anuṣṭhānasya lakṣa yoga ākhyam śrutiḥ śravaṇam asmattaḥ śravaṇena viśeṣataḥ pratipannā sakala visajātīya niratiśaya sūkṣma tattva viṣayā svayam acalā rūpā buddhiḥ asaṅga anuṣṭhānena nirmalīkṛte yadā niścalā sthāsyati ava lokanam avāpsyasi etad bhavati janya ka sthita prajña ākhya niṣṭhām āpādayati niṣṭhā rūpā sthita prajña yoga ākhyam ava lokanam sādhayati etad uktaḥ pārthaḥ asaṅga anuṣṭhāna yoga sādhya sthita prajña tāyāḥ yoga sādhana bhūtāyāḥ svarūpam sthita prajñasya anuṣṭhāna prakāram pṛcchati sthasya sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣā kaḥ vācakaḥ svarūpam kīdṛśam sthita prajñaḥ kim bhāṣā ādikam karoti vṛtti kathanena svarūpam bhavati vṛtti ucyate manasā avalambanena tuṣṭaḥ tena toṣeṇa vyatiriktān gatān kāmān yadā prakarṣeṇa jahāti ayam sthita prajña ucyate niṣṭhā kāṣṭheyam anantaram tataḥ arvācī nādūra viprakṛṣṭa ucyate viśleṣa duḥ kha nimitteṣu upasthiteṣu anudvigna manāḥ duḥkhī bhavati sukheṣu vigata spṛhaḥ priyeṣu sannihita iṣu vigata spṛhaḥ vīta rāga bhaya krodhaḥ anāgateṣu spṛhā rāgaḥ rahitaḥ viśleṣa āgamana darśana nimittam duḥkham bhayam rahitaḥ viśleṣa āgamana cetana gata duḥkha vikāraḥ krodhaḥ rahitaḥ evaṃbhūtaḥ muniḥ manana śīlaḥ sthita dhīḥ ucyate tataḥ arvā cīnadaśā procyate yaḥ priyeṣu anabhisnehaḥ udāsīnaḥ saṃśleṣa viśleṣa rūpam śubha aśubham prāpya abhinandana dveṣa rahitaḥ sthita prajñaḥ tataḥ arvā cīna daśām yadā indriya arthān spṛṣṭum udyuktāni kūrmaḥ aṅgāni iva indriya arthebhyaḥ śaḥ pratisaṃhṛtya mana avasthāpayati sthita prajñaḥ caturvidhā niṣṭhā pūrvā uttarottra niṣpādyā idānīm niṣṭhāyāḥ duṣprāpatām prāpti upāyam indriyāṇām āhārā viṣayāḥ nirāhārasya viṣayebhyaḥ pratyāhṛta indriyasya dehinaḥ viṣayā vinivartamānā rasa vinivartante rasaḥ rāgaḥ viṣaya rāgaḥ nivartata rāgaḥ svarūpam viṣayebhyaḥ sukhataram dṛṣṭvā nivartate darśanena vinā viṣaya rāgaḥ nivartate anivṛtte viṣaya rāge vipaścitaḥ yatamānasya puruṣasya pramāthīni balavanti prasahya haranti indriya jayaḥ darśana adhīnaḥ indriya jaya adhīnam niṣṭhā duṣprāpā sarvasya parijihīrṣayā viṣaya anurāga yukta durjaya ani saṃyamya cetasaḥ śubha bhūte mayi avasthāpya samāhita āsīta mad viṣaye nirdagdha aśeṣa kalmaṣa nirmalīkṛtam viṣaya anurāga rahitam mana vaśāni karoti tataḥ vaśya indriyam mana darśanāya prabhavati agniḥ uddhata śikhaḥ kakṣam dahati anilaḥ citta sthitaḥ viṣṇuḥ yoginām kilbiṣam vaśe yasya pratiṣṭhitā mayi aniveśya yatna gauraveṇa indriya jaye pravṛttaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati anirasta viṣaya anurāgasya mayi aniveśita manasa saṃyamya avasthitasya pāpa vāsanayā viṣaya dhyānam avarjanīyam dhyāyataḥ viṣayān puṃsaḥ punar saṅgaḥ atipravṛddhaḥ jāyate saṅgāt saṃjāte kāmaḥ kāmaḥ saṅgasya vipāka daśā puruṣaḥ yām daśām āpannaḥ viṣayān abhuktvā sthātum śaknoti kāmaḥ krodhaḥ abhijāyate kāme vartamāne viṣaye āsat nihite sannihitān puruṣān ebhiḥ asmat iṣṭam vihitam krodhaḥ bhavati krodhāt bhavati saṃmohaḥ saṃmohaḥ kṛtyā kṛtya viveka śūnyatā sarvam karoti tataḥ prārabdhe indriya jaya ādike prayatne bhraṃśaḥ bhavati bhraṃśāt nāśaḥ jñāne yaḥ vyavasāyaḥ kṛtaḥ nāśaḥ nāśāt punar saṃsāre nimagnaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati uktena prakāreṇa mayi īśvare cetasaḥ śubha bhūte nyasta manāḥ nirdagdha aśeṣa kalmaṣa rāga dveṣa viyuktaiḥ vaśyaiḥ indriyaiḥ viṣayāṃ caran viṣayān tiraskṛtya vartamānaḥ vidheya vidheya manāḥ prasādam adhigacchati nirmala antaḥkaraṇaḥ bhavati puruṣasya prasāde prakṛti saṃsarga prayukta duḥkhānām hāniḥ upajāyate prasanna cetasaḥ ava lokana virodhi rahita manasaḥ tadānīm vivikta viṣayā buddhiḥ paryavatiṣṭhate ataḥ prasāde duḥkhānām hāniḥ bhavati mayi sannyaḥ ta manorahitasya yatnena indriya niyamane pravṛttasya kadācid vivikta viṣayā buddhiḥ setsyati ata bhāvanā saṃbhavati vivikta ātmānam abhāvayataḥ viṣaya spṛhā śāntiḥ bhavati aśāntasya viṣaya spṛhā yuktasya kutaḥ niratiśaya punar uktena prakāreṇa indriya niyamanam akurvataḥ anartham indriyāṇām viṣayeṣu caratām vartamānānām vartanam yad vidhīyate puruṣeṇa anuvartyate vivikta pravaṇām prajñām harati viṣaya pravaṇām karoti ambhasi nīyamānām nāvam pratikūlaḥ vāyuḥ prasahya harati tasmāt uktena prakāreṇa śubha āśraye mayi niviṣṭa manasaḥ yasya indriya arthebhyaḥ śaḥ nigṛhītāni pratiṣṭhitā bhavati niyata indriyasya prasanna manasaḥ siddhim yā viṣayā buddhiḥ bhūtānām niśā niśā i va prakāśā tasyām viṣayāyām buddhau indriya saṃyamī prasanna manāḥ jāgarti ātmānam avalokayan āsta yasyām viṣayāyām buddhau bhūtāni jāgrati prabuddhāni bhavanti viṣayā buddhiḥ ātmānam paśyataḥ muneḥ niśā i va prakāśā bhavati āpūryamāṇam rūpam samudram nādeyya praviśanti āsām apām praveśe apraveśe samudraḥ kañcana āpadyate kāmāḥ viṣayāḥ yam saṃyaminam praviśanti indriya gocara tām yānti śāntim āpnoti indriya gocara tām āpanneṣu anāpanneṣu avalokana tṛptyā yaḥ vikāram āpnoti śāntim āpnoti kāmī yaḥ ādibhiḥ vikriyate kadācid śāntim āpnoti kāmyanta kāmāḥ yaḥ pumān ādīn viṣayān vihāya nisspṛhaḥ mamatā rahita ḥ anātmani dehe abhimāna rahita ḥ carati ātmānam dṛṣṭvā śāntim adhigacchati eṣā pūrvikā asaṅga sthitiḥ sthita dhīlakṣā brāhmī brahmaprāpikā īdṛśīm prāpya vimuhyati punar saṃsāram āpnoti asyāḥ sthityām antime vayasi sthitvā nirvāṇam ṛcchati nirvāṇa mayam gacchati tānam ātmānam avāpnoti ātmayāthātmyam yuddha ākhyasya karmaṇaḥ prāpti sādhana tām ajānataḥ jñānena mohitasya tena mohena yuddhān nivṛttasya moha śāntaye viṣayā sāṅkhya buddhiḥ pūrvikā asaṅga anuṣṭhāna yoga viṣayā buddhiḥ sthita prajña yoga sādhana bhūtāḥ dvitīye adhyāye proktā saṅga gocarā sāṅkhya yoga dhīḥ dvitīye sthita dhīlakṣā proktā moha śāntaye mumukṣubhiḥ prāpyatayā udita nirasta nikhila avidyā gandhāna vadhika atiśaya saṃkhyeya kalyāṇa gaṇa uttama prāpt vaktum ya apahata pāpmā ityādi prajāpati uditam prāptuḥ yāthātmya kāsaṅga niṣpādya yoga sādhyam prajāpati vākye dahara udita aśeṣa prāptuḥ yaḥ tam ātmānam anuvidya vijānāti uktvā jāgarita atītam pratyak svarūpam aśarīram pratipādya eṣa saṃprasādaḥ asmāc śarīrāt samutthāya upasaṃpadya rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate dahara phalena upasaṃhṛtam yoga adhigamena devam matvā dhīraḥ harṣa śokau jahāti devam matvā vidhīyamāna yoga adhigamena pratyak jñānam vidhāya jāyate mriyate vipaścit ityādinā pratyak svarūpam viśodhya aṇoḥ aṇīyān ārabhya mahāntam vibhum ātmānam matvā dhīraḥ śocati ayam pravacanena labhyaḥ medhayā bahunā śrutena yam eṣa vṛṇute tena labhya ḥ eṣa vivṛṇute tanūm svām ityādibhiḥ svarūpam upāsanam upāsanasya bhakti tām pratipādya sārathiḥ yaḥ pragrahavān naraḥ adhvanaḥ pāram āpnoti viṣṇoḥ paramam padam phalena upasaṃhṛtam ataḥ adhyāya catuṣṭayena idam prāptuḥ pratyak sādhanam prapañcayati yadi karmaṇaḥ buddhiḥ jyāyasi matā kim tarhi ghore mām niyojayasi etad bhavati niṣṭhā ava lokana sādhanam niṣṭhā tasyāḥ niṣpādikā avalokana sādhana bhūtāḥ niṣṭhā sakala indriya manasām viṣaya uparati niṣpādya abhihitā indriya uparati niṣpādyam ava lokanam siṣā dhayiṣitam sakala nivṛtti ka niṣṭhāyām aham niyojayitavyaḥ kim ghore indriya rūpe avalokana virodhini mām niyojayasi ataḥ miśra vākyena mām mohayasi iva pratibhāti avalokana sādhana bhūtāyāḥ indriya uparati rūpāyāḥ niṣṭhāyāḥ viparyaya rūpam sādhanam kurv vākyam viruddham vyāmiśram tasmāt ekam amiśra rūpam vākyam vada yena vākyena aham rūpam niścitya śreyaḥ prāpnuyām samyak avadhṛtam tvayā purā vicitra adhikāri pūrṇe dvividhā niṣṭhā viṣayā adhikāram asaṅkīrṇā mayā uktā sarvaḥ laukikaḥ puruṣaḥ saṃjāta abhilāṣaḥ tadānīm yoga adhikāre prabhavati anabhisaṃhita phalena kevala parama ārādhana veṣeṇa anuṣṭhitena karmaṇā vidhvasta malaḥ avyākula indriyaḥ niṣṭhāyām adhikaroti yataḥ pravṛttiḥ bhūtānām yena sarvam idam tatam karmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mānavaḥ parama ārādhana veṣa karmaṇām vakṣyate ḥ ityādinā anabhisaṃhita vidhāya tena viṣaya vyākula moha at uttīrṇa buddheḥ prajahāti yadā kāmān ityādinā yoga uditaḥ ataḥ sāṅkhyānām yogena sthitiḥ uktā yoginām yogena saṅkhyā buddhiḥ yuktāḥ sāṅkhyāḥ viṣayayā buddhyā saṃbandhinaḥ sāṅkhyāḥ atadarhāḥ yoga adhikāriṇaḥ viṣaya vyākula yuktānām yoge adhikāraḥ avyākula buddhīnām yoge ukta kiṃcid viruddham vyāmiśram abhihitam sarvasya laukikasya puruṣasya icchāyām jātāyām sahasā duṣkara śāstrīyāṇām karmaṇām anārambhāt puruṣaḥ naiṣkarmyam niṣṭhām prāpnoti ārabdhasya śāstrīyasya tyāgāt yataḥ anabhisaṃhita phalasya parama ārādhana veṣasya karmaṇaḥ ataḥ tena vinā tām prāpnoti anabhisaṃhita phalaiḥ karmabhiḥ anārādhita govindaiḥ avinaṣṭa ana kāla pravṛtta ananta pāpa sañcayaiḥ avyākula indriya tāpūrvikā niṣṭhā dussaṃpādā etad upapādayati vartamānaḥ puruṣaḥ kaścid kadācid akurvāṇa ḥ tiṣṭhati kiṃcid karomi vyavasitaḥ sarvaḥ puruṣaḥ prakṛti saṃbhavaiḥ sattva rajaḥ tamobhiḥ prācīna anuguṇam pravṛddhaiḥ guṇaiḥ ucitam avaśaḥ kāryate pravartyate ata ukta lakṣaṇena yogena prācīnam pāpa saṃcayam nāśayitvā anḥ sattva ādīn vaśe kṛtvā nirmala antaḥkaraṇena saṃpādyaḥ yogāya pravṛttaḥ mithyā ācāraḥ bhavati avinaṣṭa pāpa ajita antaḥkaraṇaḥ jñānāya pravṛttaḥ viṣaya pravaṇa vimukhīkṛta manāḥ viṣayān smaran ya āste saṃkalpya carati mithyā ucyate jñānāya udyuktaḥ viparītaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati ataḥ abhyasta viṣaya sajātīye śāstrīye ava lokana pravṛttena manasā niyamya taiḥ svata pravaṇaiḥ indriyaiḥ asaṅga pūrvakam yaḥ ārabhate asaṃbhāvyamāna pramāda niṣṭhād puruṣāt viśiṣyate niyatam vyāptam prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭena vyāptam vāsanayā prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭa ḥ niyata suśaka asaṃbhāvita pramāda karmaṇaḥ kuru akarmaṇaḥ niṣṭhāyāḥ naiṣkarmyam puruṣaḥ aśunute prakramāt akarma śabdena niṣṭhā ucyate niṣṭha adhikāriṇaḥ anabhyasta aniyata duḥśaka pramāda niṣṭhāyāḥ niṣṭhā jyāyasī kriyamāṇe ātmayāthātmya jñānena akartṛ sandhānam anantaram vakṣyate ata jñānasya yoga antargata jyāyān karmaṇaḥ niṣṭhāyāḥ vacanam niṣṭhāyām adhikāre yadi sarvam parityajya kevalam niṣṭhāyām adhikāraḥ tarhi akarmaṇaḥ niṣṭhā upakāriṇī yātrā setsyati yāvat sādhana samāpti dhāraṇam vaśyam nyāya arjita dhanena mahāyajña ādikam kṛtvā aśanena dhāraṇam kāryamāhāra śuddhau sattva śuddhiḥ sattva śuddhau dhrutvā smṛtiḥ ityādi agham bhuñjate pāpā ye pacanti kāraṇāt vakṣyate ataḥ akurvataḥ yātrā setsyati yataḥ dhriyamāṇa śarīrasya yāvat sādhana samāpti mahāyajña naimittikam avaśyam kartavyam yataḥ yoge akartṛ bhāvanayā yāthātmya anusandhānam antarbhūtam yataḥ prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya suśakaḥ apramādaḥ ataḥ niṣṭhā yogyasya jyāyān tasmāt kurv abhiprāyaḥ tarhi dravya arjana ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ ahaṅkāram amakāra indriya vyakula garbha puruṣasya vāsanayā bandhanam bhaviṣyati atra śāstrī ya bhūtāt dravya arjana ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ ātmīya bhūte kriyamāṇe ayam lokaḥ bandhanaḥ bhavati ataḥ dravya arjana ādikam samācara sādhana yaḥ saṅgaḥ tasmāt saṅgān ḥ tam samācara saṅgena kriyamāṇe ādibhiḥ karmabhiḥ ārādhitaḥ parama puruṣaḥ ana kāla pravṛtta vāsanām ucchidya avyākula avalokanam dadāti śiṣṭena iva sādhana niṣṭhānām kartavyatām ayajña śiṣṭena dhāraṇam kurvatām doṣam patim viśvasya ityādi nirupādhikaḥ prajāpati sarveśvaram viśvasya sraṣṭāram viśvātmānam parāyaṇam nārāyaṇam purā sarga kāle bhagavān prajāpatiḥ kāla pravṛtta acit saṃsarga vivaśāḥ upasaṃhṛta vibhāgāḥ svasmin pralīnāḥ sakala arthān arhāḥ cetanā kalpāḥ prajāḥ samīkṣya parama kāruṇikaḥ ujjīvayiṣayā ārādhana nirvṛttaye yajñaiḥ sṛṣṭvā uvāca yajñena prasaviṣyadhvam vṛddhim kurudhvam eṣa vaḥ yajñaḥ parama ākhyasya kāmasya anuguṇānāam kāmānām prapūrayitā bhavatu katham ārādhana bhūtena devān mad bhūtān mad ātmakān ārādhayata aham yajñānām bhoktā prabhuḥ vakṣyate yajñena ārādhitāḥ devāḥ mad ātmakāḥ ārādhana apekṣita anna pāna ādikaiḥ yuṣmān puṣṇantu parasparam bhāvayantaḥ śreyaḥ ākhyam avāpsyatha bhāvitāḥ yajñena ārādhitāḥ mad ātmakā devāḥ iṣṭān vaḥ dāsyante uttama lakṣaṇam mokṣam sādhayatām ye iṣṭā bhogāḥ tān bhāvitā devāḥ dāsyante ārādhana upekṣitān bhogān vaḥ dāsyante ārādhana taiḥ dattān bhogān tebhyaḥ apradāya yaḥ bhuṅkte cora couryam anyadīye prayojanāya parikḷpte vastuni kīyatā buddhim kṛtvā tena poṣaṇam ataḥ parama arthān niraya gāmi bhaviṣyati abhiprāyaḥ vivṛṇoti indra avasthita parama ārādhana dravyāṇi upādāya vipacya taiḥ avasthitam parama ārādhya aśanena ye yātrām kurvate kāla upārjitaiḥ kilbiṣaiḥ yāthātmya avalokana virodhibhiḥ sarvaiḥ mucyante ye parama puruṣeṇa indra ādiātmanā ārādhanāya dattāni arthati upādāya vipacya aśnanti pāpa agham bhuñjate agha pariṇāmi agham ucyate avalokana vimukhāḥ narakāya pacante punar sarvasya darśayitvā anuvartanasya tām ananuvartane doṣam annāt bhūtāni bhavanti parjanyāc anna saṃbhavaḥ sākṣikam yajñāt parjanyaḥ bhavati śāstreṇa avagamyate agnau prāsta āhutiḥ samyak ādityam upatiṣṭhate at jāyate vṛṣṭiḥ ityādinā yajñaḥ dravya arjana samudbhavaḥ udbhavam atra nirdiṣṭam prakṛti pariṇāma rūpam tasmāt etad rūpam annam jāyate śabdena prakṛti nirdiṣṭā mama vakṣyate ataḥ udbhavam prakṛti pariṇāma udbhavam bhavati samudbhavam atra nirdiṣṭaḥ jīvātmā anna pāna tṛpta adhiṣṭhitam karmaṇe prabhavati sādhana samudbhavam tasmāt gatam adhi kāri gatam yajñe pratiṣṭhitam mūlam parama puruṣeṇa pravartitam idam cakram anna ād nirdiṣṭāni jīvāni śarīrāṇi paryjanyāt annam yajñāt parjanyaḥ yajñaḥ rūpāt karmaṇaḥ jīvā c śarīrāt jīvam punar anna ād anyonya bhāvena cakravat parivartamānam sādhane vartamānaḥ yaḥ yoga adhikārī yoga adhikārī anuvartayati pravartayati śiṣṭena dhāraṇam akurvan aghāyuḥ bhavati agha ārambhāya yasya āyuḥ agha pariṇatam rūpam aghāyuḥ ata indriya ārāmaḥ bhavati ārāmaḥ udyānāni bhavanti ayajña vardhita ena udrikta rajaḥ tamaskaḥ avalokana vimukha viṣaya ratiḥ bhavati ataḥ yoga ādau yatamānaḥ niṣphala mogham pārtha jīvati asādhana āyatta darśanasya muktasya iva mahāyajña varṇa āśrama ucita anārambha yaḥ yoga yoga sādhana nirapekṣaḥ svata ratiḥ abhimukhaḥ tṛptaḥ anna pāna ādibhiḥ vyatiriktaiḥ santuṣṭaḥ udyāna sraj gīta vāditra nṛtta ādau poṣaṇa bhogya ādikam sarvam atmā yasya darśanāya kartavyam vidyate svata sarvadā ata darśanāya kṛtena sādhanena kiṃcid prayojanam akṛtena darśana sādhanena kaścid anarthaḥ asādhana āyatta darśana svata vyatirikta sakala ācit vastu vimukhasya sarveṣu prakṛti pariṇāma viśeṣeṣu kāryeṣu kaścid sādhana yataḥ vimukhīkaraṇāya sādhana ārambhaḥ yasmāt asādhana āyatta darśanasya sādhana pravṛttiḥ yasmāt sādhane pravṛttasya suśaka apramāda antargata yāthātmya anusandhāna mātrayā anuvṛtti yoga darśana nirvṛttau śreyān tasmāt asaṅga pūrvakam satatam yāvat prāpti samācara asaktaḥ vakṣyamāṇa ākartṛ sandhāna pūrvakam ācaran puruṣaḥ yogena āpnoti ātmānam prāpnoti yataḥ yoga adhikāriṇaḥ yoga darśane śreyān ata janaka rājarṣayaḥ jñāninām agresarāḥ yogena saṃsiddhim āsthitāḥ ātmānam prāptavantaḥ prathamam mumukṣoḥ yogān yoga adhikāriṇaḥ yoga uktvā yoga adhikāriṇaḥ yoga śreyān hetukam idānīm vyapadeśyasya yoga ucyate saṃgraham paśyan kartum arhasi jñātayā anuṣṭhātṛ prathitaḥ yad yad ācarati akṛt sna vij janaḥ ācarati anuṣṭhīyamānam yad pramāṇam yad yuktam anutiṣṭhati yuktam ākṛtsna lokaḥ anutiṣṭhati ataḥ rakṣā prathitena śreṣṭhena varṇa āśrama ucitam sakalam sarvadā nāśa janitam pāpam pracyāvayet me īśvarasi āpta kāmasya sarvajñasya saṅkalpasya triṣu lokeṣu rūpeṇa svacchandataḥ vartamānasya kiṃcid kartavyam yataḥ anavāptam karmaṇā avāptavyam kiṃcid rakṣāyai varte aham īśvaraḥ saṅkalpaḥ saṅkalpa udaya vibhava laya līlaḥ chandataḥ upakṛti martyaḥ jātaḥ manuṣyeṣu jana gresara vasudeva gṛhe avatīrṇa ḥ kula ucite atandrita ḥ sarvadā yadi varteya mama jana gresara vasudeva sūnoḥ vartma akṛt sna śiṣṭāḥ prakāreṇa ayam anuvartante kartavyān anuṣṭhānena akaraṇe pratyavāyena ātmānam alabdhvā niraya gāminaḥ bhaveyuḥ aham kula ucitam kuryām lokā madācara āyatta niścayāḥ akaraṇāt utsīdeyuḥ naṣṭā bhaveyuḥ śāstrīyācārān anupālanāt kulānām saṃkarasya syām ata imāḥ prajāḥ upahanyām jana agresara pāṇḍu tanayaḥ yudhiṣṭhira anujaḥ arjuna ḥ san yadi niṣṭhāyām adhikaroṣi tataḥ tvad anuvartinaḥ akṛt sna śiṣṭā mumukṣavaḥ adhikāram ajānantaḥ niṣṭhāyām adhikurvantaḥ vinaśyeyuḥ ataḥ vyapadeśyena viduṣā kartavyam avidvāṃsaḥ akṛt sna saktāḥ avarjanīya saṃbandhāḥ akṛt sna vittayā abhyāsa yoge anadhikṛtāḥ yoga adhikāriṇaḥ darśanāya kurvate vittayā asaktaḥ yoga yogyaḥ vyapadeśyaḥ śiṣṭaḥ rakṣā su ācāreṇa lokānām niścayam cikīrṣuḥ kuryāt ajñānām akṛt sna vittayā yoga upādāna śaktānām mumukṣūṇām saṅginām vāsanayā niyata yoga adhikāriṇām anyat ava lokana sādhanam bhedam janayet kim tarhi vittayā yoga śaktaḥ ukta rītyā yoga yoga nirapekṣaḥ ava lokana sādhanam buddhyā yuktaḥ ācaran sakala karmasu akṛt sna vidām prītim janayet anutiṣṭhataḥ viduṣaḥ aviduṣaḥ pradarśayan yoga apekṣitam akartṛ sandhāna prakāram upadiśati prakṛteḥ guṇaiḥ sattva ādibhiḥ rūpam kriyamāṇāni karmāṇi ahaṅkāra vimūḍha aham manyate ahaṅkāreṇa vimūḍha yasya asau ahaṅkāra vimūḍha ahaṅkāraḥ anaham arthe prakṛtau aham abhimānaḥ tena ajñāta karmasu aham manyata vibhāgayoḥ sattva vibhāge vibhāge tattva aḥ sattva guṇeṣu sveṣu kāryeṣu vartanta matvā karmasu aham sajjate akṛt sna darśanāya pravṛttāḥ prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭa prakṛteḥ guṇaiḥ avasthita saṃmūḍhāḥ karmasu kriyāsu sajjante vivikta svarūpe ataḥ yogāya prabhavanti yoga adhikāraḥ evaṃbhūtān tān mandān akṛt sna svayam yoga avasthānena vicālayet kila mandāḥ śreṣṭha jana anuvartinaḥ utthitam dṛṣṭvā pracalita manasaḥ bhaveyuḥ ataḥ svayam yoge tiṣṭhan ātmayāthātmya jñānena akartṛ anusandhānaḥ yoga avalokane nirapekṣa sādhanam darśayitvā tān akṛt sna joṣayet yoga adhikāriṇaḥ ataḥ vyapadeśyaḥ saṃgrahāya etam kuryāt prakṛti vivikta svabhāva nirūpaṇena guṇeṣu āropya anuṣṭhāna prakāra uktaḥ guṇeṣu sandhānam idam prayuktam idam samparka kṛtam prāpta prāpta vivekena kṛtam anusandhānam idānīm ātmanām parama niyāmya nirūpaṇena bhagavati puruṣottame bhūte kṛtam āropya kartavya ucyate mayi īśvare bhūte karmāṇi cetasā saṃnyasya nirāśīḥ nirmamaḥ vigata jvaraḥ yuddha ādikam sarvam coditam kuruṣva yad viṣayeṇa śata siddhena jñānena antaḥ praviṣṭaḥ śāstā janānām praviṣṭam kartāram etam tiṣṭhan antaraḥ yam veda yasya ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati ta antaryāmī amṛtaḥ ādyāḥ śrutayaḥ parama pravartyam ātmānam parama pravartayitāram smṛtayaḥ praśāsitāram ityādyāḥ sarvasya aham sanniviṣṭaḥ mattaḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam apohanam īśvaraḥ bhūtānām hṛd deśe arjuna tiṣṭhati bhrāmayan bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā vakṣyate ataḥ mad mad pravarti anusandhānena karmāṇi mayā kriyamāṇā ani mayi parama puruṣe saṃnyasya kevalam mad ārādhanāni kṛtvā phale nirāśīḥ tataḥ mamatā rahitaḥ bhūtvā vigata jvaraḥ yuddha ādikam kuruṣva svakīyena kartrā svakīyaiḥ upakaraṇaiḥ suārādhana prayojanāya parama puruṣaḥ śeṣī īśvaraḥ svayam karmāṇi kārayati anusandhāya ḥ mamatā rahitaḥ prācīnena kāla pravṛtta ananta pāpa sañcayena katham aham bhaviṣyāmi evaṃbhūta jvara vinirmuktaḥ parama karmabhiḥ ārādhitaḥ bandhān mocayiṣyati sukhena kuruṣv tam īśvarāṇām paramam maheśvaram tam daivatānām paramam daivatam patim viśvasya patim patīnām ityādi siddhim īśvara śeṣi īśvara niyantṛ śeṣi ayam upaniṣad bhūtaḥ ye mānavāḥ adhikāriṇaḥ ayam etad me matam niścitya anutiṣṭhanti ye ana nutiṣṭhantaḥ arthe śraddadhānā bhavanti ye śraddadhānā saṃbhavati abhyasūyanti mahā guṇe arthe doṣam anāviṣkurvantaḥ bhavanti hetubhiḥ kāla ārabdhaiḥ sarvaiḥ karmabhiḥ mucyante eṣām idānīm ananutiṣṭhantaḥ arthe śraddadhānā anabhyasūyavaḥ śraddhayā ana sūyayā kṣīṇa pāpāḥ acireṇa imam anuṣṭhāya mucyanta bhagavat abhimatam aupaniṣadam ananutiṣṭhatām aśraddadhānānām abhyasūyatām doṣam ye etad sarvam vastu mad madādhāram mad mad pravartyam me matam anutiṣṭhanti anusandhāya karmāṇi kurvate ye śraddadhate ye abhya sūyantaḥ vartante tān sarveṣu jñāneṣu viśeṣeṇa mūḍhān tataḥ naṣṭān acetasaḥ viddhi vastu yāthātmya niścayaḥ acetasaḥ viparīta jñānāḥ vimūḍhāḥ prakṛti saṃsargiṇa ḥ udreka kṛtam parama āyattam anusandhāya yoga yogyena yoga yogyena yogasya suśaka apramāda antargata nirapekṣa duśśaka pramāda yoga kartavyaḥ vyapadeśyasya viśeṣataḥ kartavyaḥ ataḥ adhyāya śeṣeṇa yogasya duśśaka pramādatā ucyate prakṛti viviktam īdṛśam svarūpam sarvadā sandhā iyam śāstrāṇi pratipādayanti jñānavān svasyāḥ prakṛteḥ prācīna vāsana āya aḥ sadṛśam prākṛta viṣayeṣu ceṣṭate kutaḥ prakṛtim yānti bhūtāni acit saṃsṛṣṭā jantavaḥ kāla pravṛtta vāsanām anuyānti vāsanā anuyāyīni bhūtāni kṛtaḥ nigrahaḥ kim kariṣyati prakṛti anuyāyi prakāram śrotra indriyasya arthe ādau indriyasya arthe vacana ādau prācīna vāsanā janita anububhūṣā rūpaḥ yaḥ rāgaḥ avarjanīyaḥ vyavasthitaḥ anubhave pratihate āvarjanīyaḥ yaḥ dveṣaḥ vyavasthitaḥ tau yogāya yatamānam niyamita indriyam vaśe kṛtvā prasahya kāryeṣu saṃyojayataḥ tataḥ ayam anubhava vimukhaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati yoga ārambheṇa rāga dveṣa vaśam āgamya vinaśyet tau rāga dveṣau durjayau śatrū abhyāsam vārayataḥ ataḥ suśaka svadharma bhūtaḥ viguṇaḥ apramāda garbhaḥ prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya duśśaka bhūtāj kiṃcid kālam anuṣṭhitāt pramādāt chreyān upādātum yogyatayā svadharma bhūte yoge vartamānasya janmani aprāpta nidhanam śreyaḥ anantarāya hata ananta ra jan mani avyākula yoga ārambha prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya upādātum aśakya bhūtaḥ pramāda garbha bhaya āvahaḥ ayam yogāya pravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ svayam viṣayān anubhavitum anicchan kena prayuktaḥ viṣaya anubhava rūpam pāpam balān niyojita iva carati udbhava abhibhava rūpeṇa vartamāna maya prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya aya ārabdhasya rajaḥ samudbhavaḥ prācīnavāsanā janitaḥ viṣayaḥ kāmaḥ mahā aśanaḥ śatruḥ viṣayeṣu ākarṣati eṣa pratihata gatiḥ pratihati cetanān krodha rūpeṇa pariṇataḥ mahā pāpmā hiṃsā pravartayati rajaḥ samudbhavam sahajam yoga virodhinam vairiṇam viddhi dhūmena vahniḥ āvriyate ādarśaḥ malena ulbena āvṛtaḥ garbhaḥ tena kāmena idam jantu jātam āvṛtam āvaraṇa prakāram jantoḥ jñāninaḥ svabhāvasya viṣayam jñānam viṣaya vyāmoha jananena vairiṇā āvṛtam duṣpūreṇa prāpti anarha viṣayeṇa analena paryāpti rahitena kaiḥ upakaraṇaiḥ ayam ātmānam adhiṣṭhiti atra adhitiṣṭhati ebhiḥ ayam ātmānam buddhiḥ etaiḥ indriya buddhibhiḥ kāmaḥ bhūtaiḥ viṣaya pravaṇaiḥ dehinam prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭam jñānam āvṛtya vimohayati vividham mohayati vimukham viṣaya anubhava karoti yasmāt indriya uparati rūpe yoge pravṛttasya ayam kāmarūpaḥ śatruḥ viṣaya abhimukhya karaṇena vaimukhyam karoti tasmāt prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭa indriya pravaṇaḥ ādau upāya ārambha samaya indriya rūpe yoge niyamya nāśanam viṣayasya jñānasya viveka viṣayasya nāśanam pāpmānam kāmarūpam vairiṇam prajahi nāśaya virodhiṣu pradhānam virodhe pradhānā ni āhuḥ yata indriyeṣu viṣaya vyāpṛteṣu jñānam pravartate indriyebhyaḥ indriyeṣu uparata iṣu viṣaya pravaṇe jñānam saṃbhavati manasaḥ parā buddhiḥ vṛtti vimukhe viparīta adhyavasāya pravṛttau satyām jñānam pravartate sarveṣu paryanteṣu uparata iṣu icchā aparyāyaḥ kāmaḥ rajassamudbhavaḥ vartate etāni indriya ādīni viṣaye vartayitvā jñānam niruṇaddhi idam ucyate yaḥ buddheḥ ḥ buddheḥ yaḥ ḥ buddheḥ kāmam yoga virodhinam vairiṇam buddhvā ātmānam buddhyā yoge avasthāpya kāmarūpam durāsadam śatrum jahi nāśaya adhyāye prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya mumukṣoḥ sahasā yoge anadhikārāt yoga kāryaḥ yoga adhikāriṇaḥ akartṛ sandhāna ka yoga śreyān hetukam vyapadeśyasya viśeṣataḥ yoga caturthena idānīm yogasya nikhila uddharaṇāya manvantara ādau upadiṣṭa kartavyatām draḍhayitvā antargata yoga ākara tām pradarśya yoga svarūpam bhedāḥ yoge aṃśasya prādhānyam ucyate prasaṅga āt bhagavat avatāra yāthātmyam ucyate śrī bhagavān uvāca yaḥ ayam tava uditaḥ kevalam yuddha protsāhanāya idānīm udita mantavyam manvantara ādau nikhila uddharaṇāya parama sādhana imam aham vivasvate proktavān vivasvān manave manuḥ ikṣu akave saṃpradāya paramparayā prāptam imam rājarṣayaḥ aviduḥ mahatā kālena śrotṛ māndya at vinaṣṭa prāyaḥ abhūt ayam askhalita purātanaḥ sakhyena bhaktyā mām prapannāya mayā proktaḥ parikaraḥ vistaram ukta mad anyena kena jñātum vaktum aśakyam yata idam uditam uttamam rahasyam jñānam prasaṅge bhagavat avatāra yāthātmyam yathāvaj jñātum arjuna uvāca kāla saṅkhyayā avaram asmat sama kālam bhavataḥ vivasvataḥ kāla saṅkhyayā aṣṭāviṃśati caturyuga saṅkhyā saṅkhyātam ādau proktavān katham etad asaṃbhāvanīyam yathārtham jānīyām nanu vaktum śakyam kṛtasya mahatām smṛtiḥ yujyata atra kaścid asau vaktāram vasudeva tanayam sarveśvaram jānāti yata vakṣyati dhāma pavitram paramam bhavān śāśvatam divyam ādidevam ajam vibhum āhuḥ tvām ṛṣayaḥ devarṣiḥ nārada ḥ asitaḥ devalaḥ vyāsaḥ svayam iva bravīṣi me yudhiṣṭhira rājasūya bhīṣma asa kṛt kṛṣṇa lokānām utpattiḥ apyayaḥ kṛṣṇasya kṛte idam viśvam carācaram evamādiṣu kṛṣṇasya kṛte kṛṣṇasya idam kṛtsnam jagad atra ucyate jānāti ayam bhagavantam vasudeva sūnam pārthaḥ jānataḥ ajānata iva pṛcchataḥ ayam āśayaḥ nikhila pratyanīka kalyāṇa tānasya īśvarasya sarvajñasya saṅkalpasya avāpta samasta kāmasya vaśa sajātīyam kim indrajāla van mithyā uta satyam tve katham prakāraḥ kim ātmakaḥ ayam dehaḥ kaḥ hetuḥ kadā kim parihāra prakāreṇa vijñāyate janmanaḥ bahūni me vyatītāni ani tava upādāna āt avatāra prakāram yāthātmyam hetum aja tvā avyaya īśvara sarvam pārameśvaram prakāram ajahad svām prakṛtim adhiṣṭhāya māyayā saṃbhavāmi svabhāvaḥ svam svabhāvam adhiṣṭhāya rūpeṇa icchayā saṃbhavāmi svarūpam hiāditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt kṣayantam rajasaḥ parāke ya eṣaḥ antarāditye hiraṇya puruṣaḥ tasmin ayam puruṣaḥ amṛtaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ nimeṣā jajñire vidyutaḥ puruṣāt adhi bhā ru upaḥ saṅkalpa kāmā ḥ ḥ rasaḥ mā āhāra janam vāsaḥ ityādi siddham māyayā ātmīyayā māyayā vayunam jñānam paryāyaḥ atra abhi yukta prayogaḥ māyayā satatam vetti prāṇinām śubha aśubham ātmīyena jñānena saṅkalpena ataḥ apahata pāpma samasta kalyāṇa sarvam aiśam svabhāvam ajahat svam rūpam sajātīya saṃsthānam kurvan saṅkalpena rūpaḥ saṃbhavāmi idam ajāyamānaḥ bahudhā vijāyate śrutiḥ sādhāraṇam akurvan rūpeṇa saṅkalpena ukta prakriyayā jāyata bahūni me vyatītāni janmāni tava arjuna aham veda ātmānam sṛjāmi aham me divyam yaḥ vetti tattvataḥ apara kālam kāla asmad saṃbhavasya yadā yadā dharmasya veda uditasya cāturvarṇya cāturāśramya vyavasthayā avasthitasya kartavyayasya glāniḥ bhavati yadā yadā viparyayasya dharmasya abhyutthānam aham saṅkalpena ukta prakāreṇa ātmānam sṛjāmi janmanaḥ prayojanam sādhavaḥ ukta śīlāḥ vaiṣṇava agra īsarā mad samāśrayaṇe pravṛttā mad svarūpāṇām manasā agocara mad darśanena vinā poṣaṇa km alabhamānāḥ kṣaṇa kālam kalpa sahasram manvānāḥ pratiśithila gātrā bhaveyuḥ mad ceṣṭita ava lokanālāpa dānena paritrāṇāya viparītānām vināśāya kṣīṇasya vaidikasya dharmasya mad ārādhana rūpasya rādhya pradarśanena sthāpanāya rūpeṇa yuge yuge saṃbhavāmi tretā yuga triguṇa prakṛti saṃsarga rahitasya sarvesvara sāru ajñi saṅkalpa samasta kalyāṇa upetasya sādhu paritrāṇa mad samāśrayaṇa prayojanam divyam aprākṛtam mad sādhāraṇam mama ceṣṭitam tattvataḥ yaḥ vetti vartamānam deham parityajya punarjanma mām prāpnoti madīya divya ceṣṭita yāthātmya vijñānena vidhvasta samasta mad samāśryaṇa virodhi pāpaḥ janmani udita prakāreṇa mām āśritya mad priyaḥ mad cittaḥ mām prāpnoti madīya tattva ākhyena tapasā pūtā bahava saṃvṛttāḥ śrutiḥ dhīrāḥ parijānanti yonim dhīrāḥ dhīmatām agresarā prakāram jānanti kevalam rūpeṇa avatīrya mad samāśrayaṇa apekṣāṇām paritrāṇam karomi ye mad samāśrayaṇa yena prakāreṇa anurūpam mām saṃkalpya prapadyante samāśrayante tān manīṣita prakāreṇa bhajāmi mām darśayāmi kim atra bahunā manuṣyāḥ mad anuvartana manorathā mama vartma mad svabhāvam sarvam yoginām manasā agocaram svakīyāiḥ karaṇaiḥ śaḥ svāpekṣitaiḥ prakāraiḥ anuvartnte idānīm prāsaṅgikam parisamāpya prakṛtasya yogasya ākāra prakāram vaktum tathāvidha yoga adhikāriṇaḥ durlabha puruṣāḥ karmaṇām kāṅkṣamāṇāḥ indra yajante ārādhayanti kaścid anabhisaṃhita phalaḥ indra yajñānām bhoktāram mām yajate kuta etad yataḥ kṣiprasmin mānuṣe jā paśu anna bhavati svarga ādīnām pradarśana sarvam laukikāḥ puruṣā akṣīṇa ana kāla pravṛtta ananta pāpa saṃcaya avivekinaḥ kṣipra ākāṅkṣiṇaḥ paśu annādya svarga aṇi indra ārādhana mātrāṇi kurvate kaścid udvigna hṛdayaḥ mumukṣuḥ ukta lakṣaṇam mad ārādhana ārabhata ukta yoga ārambha virodhi pāpa kṣaya hetum cāturvarṇya pramukham stamba paryantam kṛtsnam sattva vibhāgena anuguṇa vibhāgena vibhaktam mayā sṛṣṭam sṛṣṭi grahaṇam pradarśana mayā rakṣyante mayā upasaṃhriyate vicitra sṛṣti ādeḥ kartāram akartāram mām viddhi katham atra yata imāni vicitra sṛṣṭi ādīni karmāṇi mām limpanti mām saṃbadhnanti mad prayuktāni vaicitryāṇi sṛjyānām puṇya pāpa prayuktā ni ataḥ prāpta prāpta vivekena vicitra sṛṣṭi ādeḥ aham yataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ kṣetrajñāḥ sṛṣṭi labdha karaṇa kalebarāḥ sṛṣṭi labdham bhogya jātam saṅga anuguṇam bhuṅjate sṛṣṭyāt phale spṛhā ne me spṛhā sūtra kāraḥ naiḥ ghṛṇye bhagavān parāśaraḥ asau sṛjyānām sarga kāraṇībhūtā yataḥ vai sṛjya śaktayaḥ muktvā idam anyat kiṃcid apekṣate nīyate tapatām śreṣṭha śaktyā vastu vastu tām sṛjyānām ādīnām kṣetrajñānām sṛṣṭeḥ ayam parama puruṣaḥ vaicitrye kāraṇam sṛjya kṣetrajñānām prācīna śaktaya ataḥ muktvā sṛṣṭeḥ kartāram parama muktvā idam kṣetrajña vastu vicitra anyat apekṣate gata prācīnakarma śaktyā vastu nīyata uktena prakāreṇa sṛṣti ādeḥ kartāram akartāram sṛṣṭi saṅga rahitam yaḥ mām abhijānāti yoga ārambha virodhibhiḥ saṅga hetubhiḥ prācīna karmabhiḥ saṃbadhyate mucyata mām jñātvā vimukta pāpaiḥ pūrvaiḥ mumukṣubhiḥ ukta lakṣaṇam kṛtam tasmāt ukta prakāra mad viṣaya vidhūta pāpaḥ pūrvaiḥ vivasvatm ādibhiḥ kṛtam pūrvataram purātanam tadānīm mayā vakṣyamāṇa ākāram karva kuru vakṣyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥ durjñāna tām mumukṣuṇā kiṃrūpam akarma kim akarma yāthātmya jñānam ucyate antargatam jñānam kiṃrūpam ubhayatra kavayaḥ vidvāṃsaḥ mohitāḥ yathāvan jānanti antargata jñānam yad pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvā anuṣṭhāya aśubhāt bandhān mokṣyase kartavya jñānam anuṣṭhāna kutaḥ durjñāna yasmān sādhana bhūte svarūpe boddhavyam vikarmaṇi naimittika kāmya rūpeṇa sādhana dravya arjana ākāreṇa vividha āpannam vikarma akarmaṇi jñāne boddhavyam gahanā durvijñānā mumukṣoḥ karmaṇaḥ gatiḥ vikarmaṇi boddhavyam naimittika kāmya dravya arjana ādau kṛtam vaividhyam parityajya sandhānam etad vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ ekā atra prapañcyate akarmaṇoḥ boddhavyam akarma śabdena atra itarāt prastutam jñānam ucyate kriyamāṇa jñānam yaḥ paśyet akarmaṇi jñāne vartamāna yaḥ paśyet kim bhavati kriyamāṇam yāthātmya anusandhānena ākāram yaḥ paśyet jñānam yoga gata ākāram yaḥ paśyet bhavati kriyamāṇe yāthātmya anusandhāne bhayam saṃpannam bhavati yāthātmya anusandhāna garbham yaḥ paśyet buddhimān manuṣyeṣu yuktaḥ mokṣāya arhaḥ kṛt kṛt pratyakṣeṇa kriyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥ ākāra katham upapadyata atra yasya mumukṣoḥ dravya arjana laukika naimittika kāmya samārambhāḥ arjitāḥ saṅga rahitāḥ saṅkalpa varjitāḥ prakṛtyā guṇaiḥ ātmānam ekīkṛtya anusandhānam saṅkalpaḥ prakṛti viyukta anusandhāna yukta rahitāḥ tam kurvāṇam paṇḍitam antargata yāthātmya agninā dagdha prācīna karmāṇam āhuḥ tattva jñāḥ ataḥ karmaṇaḥ ākāra etad vivṛṇoti saṅgam tyaktvā tṛptaḥ nitye ātmni tṛptaḥ nirāśrayaḥ asthira prakṛtau rahitaḥ yaḥ karmāṇi karoti ābhimukhyena pravṛttaḥ iva kiṃcid karoti apadeśena abhyāsam karoti punar karmaṇaḥ ākāra iva viśodhyate nirāśīḥ nirgata abhisandhiḥ yata citta yata citta manāḥ tyakta parigrahaḥ prakṛti prākṛta vastuni mamatā rahitaḥ yāvat jīvam kevalam śārīram kurvan kilbiṣam saṃsāram āpnoti niṣṭhā vyavadhāna rahita kevala yogena evaṃrūpeṇa ātmānam paśyati yadṛcchā upanata vastu santuṣṭaḥ dvandva atītaḥ yāvat sādhana samāpti varjanī ya śīta uṣṇa sahaḥ vimatsaraḥ upanipāta nirūpaṇena pareṣu vigata matsaraḥ samaḥ siddhau asiddau yuddha karmasu jaya siddhi asiddhyoḥ sama cittaḥ kṛtvā niṣṭhām vinā nibadhyate saṃsāram pratipadyate viṣaya ava sthita nirgata saṅgasya tataḥ nikhila parigraha vinirmuktasya ukta nirvṛttaye vartamānasya puruṣasya prācīnam samagram pravilīyate niśśeṣam kṣīyate prakṛti viyukta anusandhāna yukta karmaṇaḥ ākāra idānīm sarvasya parikarasya karmaṇaḥ parama sandhāna yukta ākāra arpaṇam havir viśeṣyate arpyate arpaṇam srucādi yasya haviṣaḥ arpaṇam arpaṇam haviḥ arpaṇam haviḥ svayam agnau bhūte agnau brahmaṇā kartrā hutam sarvam mayam yaḥ samādhatte samādhiḥ tena samādhinā brahmā gantavyam svarūpam gantavyam mumukṣuṇā kriyamāṇam ātmakam anusandhāna yukta ākāram avalokana sādhanam niṣṭhā vi adhānena karmaṇaḥ ākāra tām pratipādya yoga bhedān bhhu daivam arcana rūpam yajñam apare paryupāsate sevante niṣṭhām kurvanti apare agnau yajñam yajñena upajuhvati atra haviḥ srucādi sādhane vartate arpaṇam haviḥ nyāyena yāga homayoḥ niṣṭhām kurvanti bhhu śrotra ādīnām indriyāṇām prayatante indriyāṇām pravaṇa nivāraṇe prayatante bhhu dīpite manassaṃyana yoga agnau aṇi indriya karmāṇi karmāṇi juhvati manasa indriya prvaṇa nivāraṇe prayatanta bhhu kecid dravya yajñāḥ nyāyataḥ dravyāṇi upādāya arcane prayatante kecid dāneṣu kecid yāgeṣu kecid homeṣu dravya yajñāḥ kecid tapaḥ yajñāḥ kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa upavāsa niṣṭhām kurvanti yoga yajñāḥ puṇya tīrtha puṇya prāptiṣu niṣṭhām kurvanti yoga niṣṭha at viṣayaḥ kecid svādhyāya abhyāsa parāḥ kecid abhyāsa parāḥ yatayaḥ śīlāḥ saṃśita vratāḥ dṛḍha saṅkalpāḥ bhhu apare prāṇāyāmeṣu niṣṭhām kurvanti trividhāḥ pūraka recaka kumbhaka apāne juhvati prāṇam pūrakaḥ prāṇe apānam recakaḥ apāna gatī ruddhvā prāṇān prāṇeṣu juhvati kumbhakaḥ prāṇāyāma pareṣu triṣu anuṣajyate niyata āhārā bhhu daiva prabhṛti prāṇāyāma paryanteṣu yoga bhedeṣu samīhiteṣu pravṛttā yajñaiḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā abhihita mahā ya naimittika niṣṭhāḥ tataḥ kṣapita kalmaṣāḥ amṛtena dhāraṇam kurvanta yoga vyāpṛtāḥ sanātanam yānti bhhu ayajñasya mahāyajña maimittika rahitasya ayam lokaḥ prākṛta lokaḥ prākṛta saṃbandhi ākhyaḥ sidhyati kuta itaḥ ākhyaḥ parama mokṣasya prastuta ayam lokaḥ nirdiśyate prākṛtaḥ bhhu bahu prakārāḥ yogāḥ brahmaṇaḥ mukhe vitatāḥ yāthātmya avāpti sādhana sthitāḥ tān ukta lakṣaṇān ukta bhedān yogān jān viddhi aharahar anuṣṭhīyamāna naimittika jān viddhi jñātvā ukta prakāreṇa anuṣṭhāya mokṣyase antargata karmaṇaḥ ākāra antargata jñāne aṃśasya prādhānyam bhhu ākāre dravya mayād aṃśāj maya śreyān sarvasya karmaṇaḥ akhilasya upādeyasya jñāne parisamāpteḥ sarvaiḥ sādhanaiḥ prāpya jñānam antargata abhyasyate abhyasyamānam prāpya daśām pratipadyate bhhu atma viṣayam jñānam avināśi viddhi ārabhya eṣā abhihitā mayā upadiṣṭam yukta vartamāna vipāka anuguṇam kāle kāle praṇipāta paripraśna sevā ādibhiḥ viśada ākāram jñānibhyaḥ viddhi sākṣātkṛtātma svarūpā aḥ jñāninaḥ praṇipāta sevitāḥ bubhutsayā paritaḥ pṛcchataḥ tava āśayam ālakṣya jñānam upadekṣyanti yāthātmya viṣayasya jñānasya sākṣātkāra rūpasya lakṣaṇam bhhu yaj jñānam jñātvā punar abhimāna rūpam kṛtam mamatā adi āspadam moham yāsyasi yena ākāreṇa anusanhitāni bhūtāni drakṣyasi yataḥ tava anyeṣām bhūtānām prakṛti viyuktānām ākāra sāmyam prakṛti saṃsarga vinirmuktam rūpam sarvam samam vakṣyate nirdoṣam samam tasmāt brahmaṇi sthitāḥ athaḥ mayi bhūtāni aśeṣeṇa drakṣyasi mad pariśuddhasya sarvasya vastunaḥ idam jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ vakṣyate vidvān puṇya pāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti evamādiṣu vinirmuktasya vastunaḥ sāmyam avagamyate ataḥ prakṛti vinirmuktam sarvam vastu parasparam samam īśvareṇa samam bhhu yadi sarvebhyaḥ pāpebhyaḥ pāpa kṛttamaḥ asi sarvam arjitam vṛjina rūpam samudram viṣaya plavena saṃtariṣyasi bhhu samyak pravṛddhaḥ agniḥ sañcayam iva yāthātmya rūpaḥ agniḥ jīvātma gatam kāla pravṛtta ananta sañcayam bhasmīkaroti bhhu yasmāt jñānena sadṛśam pavitram śuddhi karam jagati vastu antaram vidyate tasmāt jñānam pāpam nāśayati tathāvidham jñānam upadeśam aharahar anuṣṭhīyamāna ākāra yoga saṃsiddhaḥ kālena svayam labhate vispaṣṭam bhhu aj jñānam labdhvā upadiṣṭa vṛddhau śraddhāvān niyata manāḥ viṣayāt saṃyata indriyaḥ acireṇa kālena ukta vipāka daśā āpannam jñānam labhate tathāvidham jñānam labdhvā parām śāntim acireṇa adhigacchati nirvāṇam āpnoti bhhu ajñaḥ labdha rahitaḥ upadiṣṭa upāye śraddhadhānaḥ atvaramāṇaḥ upadiṣṭe jñāne saṃśaya saṃśaya manāḥ vinaśyati vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati upadiṣṭe yāthātmya viṣaye jñāne saṃśaya ayam prākṛtaḥ lokaḥ sidhyanti kutaḥ śāstrī ya siddhi arthānām śāstrīya janya atirikta niścaya ataḥ lava bhāgi saṃśaya saṃbhavati bhhu upadiṣṭa yogena saṃnyasta karmāṇam ākāra āpanna karmāṇam upadiṣṭena jñānena saṃcchinna saṃśayam ātmavantam manasvinam upadiṣṭa arthe dṛḍha ava sthita manasam prācīna ananta karmāṇi nibadhnanti bhhu tasmāt anādya saṃbhūtam hṛd stham viṣayam saṃśayam mayā upadiṣṭena asinā chittvā mayā upadiṣṭam ātiṣṭha uttiṣṭha bhārata caturthe adhyāye yogasya ākāra bhedaḥ aṃśasya prādhānyam yoga adhikāriṇaḥ yogasya antargata apramāda sukara tvān nirapekṣa idānīm yoga prāpti sādhana tve niṣṭhāya āḥ śaighryam yoga antargata ākarṭrtvā sandhāna prakāram pratipādya mūlam jñānam viśodhyate karmaṇām saṃnyāsam punar śaṃsasi etad bhavati dvitīye adhyāye mumukṣoḥ prathamam yoga kāryaḥ yogena mṛdita antaḥkaraṇa kaṣāyasya yogena pratipādya punar caturthayoḥ yoga daśā āpannasya niṣṭhā jyāyasī iva niṣṭhā niḥ prāptau sādhanam niṣṭhām praśaṃśasi etayoḥ yoga yogayoḥ prāpti sādhana yad ekam saukārya c chaighryāt śreyaḥ śreṣṭham su niścitam me brūhi bhhu saṃnyāsaḥ yoga śaktasya ubhau nirapekṣau niśśreyasa karau tayoḥ saṃnyāsā j yoga viśiṣyate kuta atra bhhu yaḥ yogī antargata anubhava tṛpta ḥ vyatiriktam kim kāṅkṣati tataḥ kim dveṣṭi tataḥ dvandva sahaḥ saṃnyāsī niṣṭha jñeyaḥ sukara yoga niṣṭhatayā sukham bandhāt pramucyate yoga yogayoḥ prāpti sādhana anyonyanaiḥ apekṣyam bhhu yoga yogau bhūtau ye pravadanti bālāḥ aniṣpanna jñānāḥ paṇḍitāḥ akṛt sna sādhayati yoga ḥ ava lokanam sādhayati tayoḥ pṛthaktvam vadantaḥ paṇḍitā avalokana phalayoḥ ekam āsthita ḥ labhate etad vivṛṇoti bhhu sāṃkhyaiḥ niṣṭhaiḥ yad atma avalokana rūpam prāpyate yoga niṣṭhaiḥ prāpyate ekam vaikalpikam sāṃkhyam yaḥ paśyati paśyati paṇḍita iyān āhā bhhu saṃnyāsaḥ yoga ḥ ayogataḥ rte prāptum aśakyaḥ yoga yuktaḥ yoga yuktaḥ svayam muniḥ manana śīlaḥ sukhena sādhayitvā alpena kālena adhigacchati ātmānam prāpnoti yoga yukta ḥ mahatā duḥkhena sādhayati duḥkha sādhya ātmānam prāpnoti bhhu yoga yukta ḥ śāstrīye parama ārādhana rūpe viśuddhe vartamānaḥ tena viśuddha manāḥ vijita svābhyaste vyāpṛta sukhena vijita manāḥ tataḥ jitendiyaḥ yāthātmya anusandhān niṣṭhatayā bhūtānām yasya asau ātmayāthātmyam anusandhānasya ādīnām svasya ākāra bhedānām prakṛti pariṇāma ākāra prakṛti viyuktaḥ deheṣu ākāra ākāra nirdoṣam samam anantaram vakṣyate evaṃbhūtaḥ kurvan anātmani abhimānena lipyate saṃbadhyate ataḥ acireṇa ātmānam prāpnoti yataḥ saukaryāt chaighryāt yoga śreyān ataḥ apekṣitam śṛṇu bhhu bhhu tattva śrotra ādīni ādīni karmendriyāṇi praṇāḥ viṣayeṣu vartanta dhārayan anusandhānaḥ aham kiṃcid karomi manyeta svabhāvasya mama indriya kṛtam īdṛśam prayuktam manyeta bhhu śabdena ucyate mama vakṣyate indriyāṇām prakṛti pariṇāma indriya kāreṇa avasthitāyām prakṛtau paśyan chṛṇvan ityādi ukta prakāreṇa karmāṇi ādhāya saṅgam tyaktvā iva kiṃcid karomi yaḥ karmāṇi karoti prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭa vartamānaḥ prakṛti abhimāna rūpeṇa hetunā pāpena lipyate padma patram iva ambhasā padma patram ambhasā saṃsṛṣṭam lipyate lipyata bhhu kāya indriya sādhyam svarga saṅgam tyaktvā yogina viśuddhaye kuranti gata prācīna vināśāya kurvanti bhhu bhhu tiryak sthāvara prakṛti saṃsargeṇa vartamānasya lokasya asādhāraṇam asādhāraṇāni karmāṇi janya saṃyogam ayam prabhuḥ akarma vaśyaḥ svābhāvika svarūpeṇa avasthita sṛjati utpādayati kaḥ tarhi svabhāvaḥ pravartate svabhāvaḥ prakṛti vāsanā kāla pravṛtta janita ākāra prakṛti saṃsarga abhimāna janita vāsanā akṛtam īdṛśam ādikam sarvam prayuktam bhhu kasyacid saṃbandhi abhimatasya ādeḥ pāpam duḥkham ādatte panudati kasyacid pratikūla abhimatasya sukṛtam sukham ādatte panudati yataḥ ayam vibhuḥ kvācid kaḥ ādya deśaḥ ata kasyacid saṃbandhī kasyacid pratikūlaḥ sarvam idam vāsanā kṛtam evaṃsvabhāvasya katham iyam viparīta vāsanā utpadyate ajñānena āvṛtam jñānam virodhinā karmaṇā anubhava yogya tvāya jñānam āvṛtam saṃkucitam tena āvaraṇa rūpeṇa karmaṇā saṃyoga ḥ abhimāna moha ḥ jāyate tataḥ tathāvidha abhimāna vāsanā ucita vāsanā vāsanātaḥ viparīta abhimānaḥ ārambhaḥ sarvam plavena vṛjinam saṃtariṣyati agniḥ karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute jñānena sadṛśam pavitram kāle saṃgamayati bhhu vartamāneṣu sarveṣu ātmasu yeṣām ātmanām ukta lakṣaṇena yāthātmya janitena viṣayeṇa aharahar abhyāsa ādheya atiśayena niratiśaya pavitreṇa jñānena āvaraṇam kāla pravṛtta ananta saṃcaya rūpam ajñānam nāśitam svābhāvikam jñānam aparimitam asaṃkucitam ādityavat sarvam avasthitam prakāśayati vinaṣṭa jñānānām bahu abhimānāt bahu aham jātu sam upakrama avagatam atra spaṣṭataram idam bahu upādhikṛtam vinaṣṭa jñānānām upādhi vaj jñānam āt jñānasya anubandhi dṛṣṭāntena jñātṛ jñānayoḥ prabhā prabhāvatoḥ iva avasthānam tataḥ daśāyām jñānasya karmaṇā saṃkocaḥ daśāyām vikāsaḥ bhhu buddhayaḥ tathāvidha darśana adhyavasāyāḥ ātmānaḥ viṣaya manasaḥ niṣṭhāḥ abhyāsa niratāḥ parāyaṇāḥ parama prayojanam manvānāḥ abhyasyamānena jñānena nirdhūta prācīna kalmaṣāḥ tathāvidham ātmanam apunarāvṛttim gacchanti yad avasthād punarāvṛttiḥ vidyate apunarāvṛttiḥ rūpeṇa avasthitam ātmānam gacchanti bhhu vinaya saṃpanne kevala brāhmaṇe gaḥ hasti śva śva paca atyanta viṣama ākāra pratīyamāneṣu ātmasu paṇḍitāḥ yāthātmya ākāra sama darśinaḥ viṣama ākāra ḥ prakṛteḥ ākāra sama paśyanti taiḥ jitaḥ svargaḥ yeṣām sāmye sthitam nirdoṣam samam tasmāt brahmaṇi sthitāḥ sādhana anuṣṭhāna daśāyām taiḥ sargaḥ jitaḥ saṃsāraḥ jitaḥ yeṣām ukta rītyā sarveṣu ātmasu sāmye sthitam nirdoṣam samam prakṛti saṃsarga viyukta samam vastu bramha sāmye sthitāḥ brahmaṇi sthitā brahmaṇi sthitiḥ sṃsāra jayaḥ ātmasu ākāra sāmyam anusandhānā muktā yena prakāreṇa avathitasya sama darśana rūpaḥ jñana vipākaḥ bhavati tam prakāram upadiśati yādṛśa sthasya yad avasthasya prācīna vāsanayā yad priyam bhavati yad priyam bhayam prāpya harṣa udvegau kuryāt katham sthira buddhiḥ sthire buddhiḥ yasya sthira buddhiḥ asaṃmūḍhaḥ asthieṇa śarīreṇa sthiram ātmānam ekīkṛtya mohaḥ saṃmohaḥ rahitaḥ katham brahmaṇi sthitaḥ upadeśena san tasmin brahmaṇi abhyāsa yuktaḥ etad bhavati tattva vidām upadeśena yāthātmya bhūtvā yatamānaḥ abhimānam parityajya sthira ava lokana anubhave vyavasthitaḥ asthire prākṛte apriye prāpya harṣa udevegau kuryāt uktena prakāreṇa bāhya sparśeṣu vyatirikta viṣaya anubhaveṣu asakta asakta manāḥ antarātmani yaḥ sukham vindati labhate prakṛti abhyāsam vihāya yoga yukta abhyāsa yukta manāḥ anubhava rūpam akṣayam sukham prāpnoti viṣaya indriya sparśa jāḥ ye bhogāḥ duḥkha yonayaḥ duḥkha ud arkāḥ antavantaḥ kāla vartinaḥ upalabhyante teṣu yāthātmya ramate vimokṣaṇāt ih sādhana anuṣṭhāna daśā ayam bhava prītyā krodha udbhavam vegam soḍhum niroddhum yaḥ śaknoti yuktaḥ anubhavāya arhaḥ vimokṣa kālam bhava ḥ saṃpatsyate yaḥ bāhya viṣaya anubhavam sarvam vihāya antassukhaḥ bhava sukhaḥ ārāmaḥ udyānaḥ guṇaiḥ vardhakaḥ yasya uktaḥ jñānaḥ yaḥ vartate bhūtaḥ yogī nirvāṇam bhava sukham prāpnoti cchinna dvaidhāḥ śīta uṣṇa dvandvaiḥ vimuktāḥ yata ātmānaḥ niyamita manasaḥ hite ratāḥ ātmavat bhūtānām hita iṣu niratāḥ ṛṣayaḥ draṣṭāraḥ ava lokana parāḥ ya evambhūtāḥ kṣīṇa aśeṣa prāpti virodhi kalmaṣāḥ nirvāṇam labhante krodhviyuktānām yatīnām śīlānām yata cetasām niyamita manasām vijita ātmanām vijita manasām nirvāṇam abhitaḥ vartate evaṃbhūtānām stham nirvāṇam yata indriya buddhiḥ muniḥ parāyaṇaḥ vigata icchā bhaya krodhaḥ yaḥ sadā bāhyān viṣaya sparśān bahiḥ kṛtvā bāhya indriya vyāpāram sarvam upasaṃhṛtya yoga yogya āsane ṛjukāya upaviśya cakṣuṣī bhruvoḥ nāsā agre vinyasya nāsā abhyantara cāriṇau pānau samau kṛtvā ucchvāsa niśvāsau sama gatī kṛtvā ava lokanāt pravṛtti anarha indriya buddhiḥ tataḥ vigata icchā bhaya krodhaḥ parāyaṇaḥ prayojanaḥ muniḥ ava lokana śīlaḥ yaḥ sadā sādhya daśāyām iva sādhana daśāyām tapasām bhoktāram maheśvaram bhūtānām suhṛdam mām jñātvā śāntim ṛcchati yoga karaṇa sukham ṛcchati maheśvaram īśvarāṇām īśvaram tam īśvarāṇām paramam maheśvaram śrūyate mām maheśvaram suhṛdam jñātvā mad ārādhana rūpaḥ yoga sukhena pravartata suhṛda ārādhanāya pravartante uktaḥ parikaraḥ idānīm yoga yoga sādhya avalokana yoga abhyāsa ucyate yogasya nirapekṣa yoga sādhana draḍhayitum ākāraḥ yoga śiraskaḥ anūdyate svarga ādikam anāśritaḥ anuṣṭhānam asmad suhṛd parama ārādhana mama prayojanam sādhyam kiṃcid yaḥ karoti saṃnyāsī yoga niṣṭhaḥ yogī yoga niṣṭhaḥ avalokana yoga sādhana bhaya niṣṭha niragniḥ kriyaḥ codita karmasu apravṛttaḥ kevala niṣṭhaḥ niṣṭhā yoga bhayam abhiprāyaḥ yam saṃnyāsa yoga yāthātmya jñānam prāhuḥ tam viddhi upapādayati asaṃnyasta saṃkalpaḥ yogī bhavati kaścana yāthātmya anusandhānena anātmani prakṛtau saṅkalpaḥ saṃnyastaḥ parityaktaḥ yena saṃnyasta saṅkalpaḥ anevaṃbhūtaḥ asaṃnyasta saṅkalpaḥ ukteṣu yogiṣu anevaṃbhūtaḥ kaścana yogī bhavati yasya samārambhāḥ saṅkalpa varjitāḥ ava lokanam prāptum icchā ūḥ mumukṣoḥ yoga kāraṇam ucyate yoga ārūḍhasya pratiṣṭhita yogasya śamaḥ nivṛttiḥ kāraṇam ucyate yāvat ava lokana avāpti yadā ayam yogī anubhava svabhāva indriya artheṣu vyatirikta prākṛta viṣayeṣu saṃbandhiṣu karmasu anuṣajjate saṅgam arhati saṅkalpa samnyāsī yoga ārūḍha ucyate tasmāt ārurukṣoḥ viṣaya anubhava ananuṣaṅga abhyāsa rūpaḥ yoga yoga niṣpatti kāraṇam ataḥ viṣayān anuṣaṅga abhyāsa rūpam ārurukṣuḥ kuryāt manasā viṣayān anuṣaktena ātmānam uddharet viparītena manasā ātmānam avasādayet mana bandhuḥ ripuḥ yena puruṣeṇa viṣayebhyaḥ jitam bandhuḥ anātmanaḥ ajita manasaḥ svakīyam svasya śatruvat śatru tve varteta niśśreyasa viparīte varteta bhagavatā parāśareṇa mana manuṣyāṇām kāraṇam mokṣayoḥ bandhāya viṣaya āsaṅgi muktyā nirviṣayam śīta uṣṇa duḥkheṣu māna avamānayoḥ jita jita manasaḥ rahita manasaḥ praśāntasya paramātmā samāhitaḥ samyak āhitaḥ rūpeṇa avasthitaḥ pratyagātmā atra paramātmā ucyate paramātma samāhita anvayaḥ tṛpta viṣayeṇa jñānena prakṛti visajātīya ākāra viṣayeṇa jñānena tṛpta manāḥ kūṭasthaḥ avasthāsu anuvartamāna ākāra sthitaḥ tataḥ vijita indriyaḥ sama loṣṭa kāñcanaḥ prakṛti vivikta niṣṭhatayā prākṛta vastu viśeṣeṣu bhogya abhāvāl loṣṭa kāñcaneṣu sama prayojanaḥ yaḥ yogī yukta ucyate ava lokana yoga abhyāsa ucyate vayaḥ anaṅgīkāreṇa hita eṣiṇaḥ suhṛdaḥ savayasaḥ hita eṣiṇaḥ mitrāṇi arayaḥ nimittataḥ anartha icchavaḥ rahitā udāsīnāḥ janmata rahitā madhyasthāḥ janmata nicchā i chavaḥ dveṣyāḥ janmata hita eṣiṇaḥ bandhavaḥ sādhavaḥ śīlāḥ pāpāḥ pāpa śīlāḥ suhṛd mitra ādibhiḥ virodha teṣu sama buddhiḥ yoga abhyāsa tve viśiṣyate yogī ukta prakāra yoga niṣṭhaḥ satatam aharahar yoga kāle ātmānam yuñjīta ātmānam yuktam kurvīta darśana niṣṭham kurvīta rahasi jana varjite niśśabde deśe sthitaḥ ekākī dvitīyaḥ yata citta yata citta manaskaḥ nirāśīḥ vyatirikte kṛtsne vastuni nirapekṣaḥ aparigrahaḥ vyatirikte kasmiṃścid mamatā rahitaḥ ekāgram kṛtvā yata citta indriya kriyaḥ upaviśya āsane yuñjyāt viśuddhaye śucau deśe aśucibhiḥ puruṣaiḥ anadhiṣṭhite aparigṛhīte aśucibhiḥ vastubhiḥ aspṛṣṭe pavitra bhūte deśe dārva nirmitam ucchritam nīcam cela ajina kuśa uttaram āsanam pratiṣṭhāpya tasmin prasāda kare apa āśraye upaviśya yoga ekāgram kṛtvā yata citta indriya kriyaḥ upasaṃhṛta citta indriya kriyaḥ viśuddhaye nivṛttaye yuñjyāt atma avalokanam kurvīta praśānta vigata bhīḥ brahmacāri vrate sthitaḥ saṃyamya mad cittaḥ yukta āsīta mad kāya grīvam samam acalam apāśraya sthiram dhārayan diśaḥ anavaloakayan nāsikā agram saṃprekṣya praśānta atyanta nirvṛta manāḥ vigata bhīr brahmacarya yuktaḥ saṃyamya mad cittaḥ yuktaḥ avahitaḥ mad āsīta mām cintyan āsīta mayi parasmin brahmaṇi puruṣottame manasaḥ śubha āśraye sadā ātmānam yuñjan niyata mānasaḥ mad sparśa vitrīkṛta niścala mānasaḥ mām cintayan mad saṃsthām nirvāṇa paramām śāntim adhigacchati nirvāṇa kāṣṭhā rūpām mad saṃsthām mayi saṃsthitām śāntim adhigacchati yukta āhāra vihārasya yukta ceṣṭasya karmasu yukta ava bodhasya bhavati duḥkha hā anaśane yoga virodhinī vihārau atimātra jāgarye āyāsa anāyāsau mita āhāra vihārasya mita āyāsasya mita ava bodhasya sakala duḥkha hā nāśanaḥ saṃpannaḥ bhavati yadā viṣayam cittam viniyatam viśeṣeṇa niyatam niratiśaya niyatam niścalam avatiṣṭhate kāmebhyaḥ nisspṛhaḥ san yukta ucyate yoga ucyate nivāta sthaḥ dīpaḥ iṅgate calati acalaḥ prabhaḥ tiṣṭhati yata cittasya nivṛtta sakala vṛtteḥ yuñjataḥ
