arcitum icchati ajānataḥ mad viṣaya eṣā śraddhā anusandhāya tām acalām nirvighnām vidadhāmi aham nirvighnayā śraddhayā yukta ḥ indra ādeḥ ārādhanam pratīhate tataḥ mad indra ārādhanāt tān abhilaṣitān kāmān mayā vihitān labhate yadi ārādhana kāleārādhya indra āt ayaḥ madīyāḥ tanavaḥ tataḥ arcanam mad ārādhanam jānāti vastunaḥ mad ārādhana ārādhaka abhilaṣitam aham vidadhāmi medhasām alpabuddhīnām indra yājinām ārādhana alpam bhavati kutaḥ devān devayajaḥ yānti yata indra ādīn devān yājinaḥ yānti indra paricchinna bhogāḥ parimita kāla vartinaḥ tataḥ sāyujyam prāptāḥ taiḥ pracyavante mad bhaktā karmaṇām mad ārādhana tām jñātvā paricchinna saṅgam tyaktvā mad prīṇa prayojanāḥ mām prāpnuvanti punar nivartante mām upetya kaunteya punar vidyate vakṣyate sarvaiḥ karmabhiḥ ārādhyaḥ aham īśvaraḥ manasā paricchedya svabhāvaḥ parama kāruṇyāt aśriti vātsalī āt samāśrayaṇīya tvāya ajahatsvabhāva vasudeva sūnuḥ avarīrṇa mama avyayam anuttamam ajānantaḥ prākṛta rāja sūnu samānam itaḥ anabhivyaktam idānīm vaśā j prāpya vyaktim āpannam prāptam mām buddhayaḥ manyante ataḥ mām āśrayante karmabhiḥ ārādhayanti kṣetrajñā saṃsthāna yoga ākhya māyayā samāvṛtaḥ aham sarvasya mayi saṃsthāna darśana mātreṇa mūḍhaḥ ayam lokaḥ mām ativāyu indra karmāṇam sūrya tejasam upalabhyamānam ajam avyayam nikhila kāraṇam sarveśvaram mām samāśrayaṇīya tvāya saṃsthānam āsthitam abhijānāti atītāni vartamānāni anāgatāni bhūtāni aham veda jānāmi mām veda kaścana mayā anusaṃdhīyamāneṣu kāla traya vartiṣu mām evaṃvidham vāsudevam samāśrayṇī ya tvā aya avatīrṇam viditvā mām samāśrayan kaścid upalabhyata ataḥ jñānī su durlabha icchā dveṣābhyām samutthitena śīta uṣṇa dvandva ākhyena mohena bhūtāni sarge kāla saṃmoham yānti etad bhavati mayeṣu duḥkha dvandveṣu janmani yad viṣayau icchā dveṣau abhyastau vāsanayā punar kāla dvandva ākhyam icchā dveṣa viṣaya samutthitam bhūtānām mohanam bhavati tena mohena bhūtāni saṃmoham yānti viṣaya icchā dveṣa svabhāvāni bhavanti mad samśleṣa viyoga duḥkha svabhāvāni jñānī mad saṃśleṣa viyoga duḥkha svabhāvaḥ svabhāvam kim jāyate yeṣām arjitena utkṛṣṭa puṇya saṃcayena maya dvandveccchā dveṣa mada aunmukhya virodhi kāla pravṛttam pāpam gatam kṣīṇam uktena tāratamyena mām śaraṇam anuprapadya mayān mohāt vinirmuktāḥ jarā maraṇa mokṣāya mahate aiśvaryāya mad prāptaye dṛḍha vratāḥ dṛḍha saṅkalpāḥ mām bhajante jarā maraṇa mokṣāya prakṛti viyukta darśanāya mām āśritya ye yatante viduḥ adhyātmam kṛtsnam viduḥ akhilam viduḥ atra ya punar nirdiṣṭa vyaḥ adhikāriṇaḥ jñāyante adhibhūtam adhidaivam mām aiśvarya arthinaḥ ye viduḥ etad anuvāda sarūpam aprāpta vidhāyakam adhiyajñam adhikāriṇām aviśeṣeṇa vidhīyate svabhāvyāt naimittika mahā anuṣṭhānam avarjanīyam prayāṇa kāle prāpya anuguṇam mām viduḥ cakāra at jarā maraṇa mokṣāya yatamānāḥ prayāṇa kāle viduḥ samuccīyante jñāninaḥ svābhāvyāt adhiyajñam mām viduḥ prayāṇa kāle prāpya anuguṇam mām viduḥ bhavati adhiyajñaḥ katham kaḥ atra dehe madhusūdanam prayāṇa kāle katham jñeyaḥ asi niyata ātmabhiḥ jarā maraṇa mokṣāya bhagavantam āśritya yatamānānām jñātavya adhyātmam kim vaktavyam aiśvarya arthīnām jñātavyam adhibhūtam adhidaivam kim jñātavyaḥ adhiyajña nirdiṣṭa ḥ kaḥ adhi katham prayāṇa kāle ebhiḥ tribhiḥ niyata ātmabhiḥ katham jñeyaḥ asi nirdiṣṭam paramam kṣarati kṣetrajña samaṣṭi rūpam śrutiḥ akṣare līyate tamasi līyate ādikā paramam prakṛti vinirmuktam svarūpam svabhāvaḥ adhyātmam ucyate svabhāvaḥ anātma saṃbadhyamānam sūkṣma vāsanā ādikam jñāta vya uditam bhayam prāpyatayā tyājya mumukṣubhiḥ jñātavyam udbhava karaḥ visargaḥ saṃjñitaḥ udbhava karaḥ yaḥ visargaḥ pañcamyām āhutau vacasaḥ bhavanti siddhaḥ yoṣit jaḥ saṃjñitaḥ akhilam anubandham udvejanīya pariharaṇīya mumukṣubhiḥ jñātavyam pariharaṇīya anantaram vakṣyate yad icchantaḥ brahmacaryam caranti aiśvarya arthinām jñātavyatayā nirdiṣṭam adhibhūtam kṣaraḥ vartamānaḥ pariṇāma viśeṣaḥ kṣaraṇa svabhāvaḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ sparśa ḥ srayaḥ vilakṣaṇāḥ āśrayāḥ sparśa rasa gandhāḥ aiśvarya arthibhiḥ prāpya aḥ taiḥ anusandheyāḥ puruṣaḥ adhi daivatam adhidaivata nirdiṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ adhidaivatam vartamānaḥ indra prajāpati prabhṛti daivata vartamānaḥ indra prajāpati prabhṛtīnām bhogya jāta d ādeḥ bhoktā puruṣaḥ tvā aiśvarya arthibhiḥ prāpya anusandheyā adhiyajñaḥ aham adhiyajñaḥ yajñaiḥ ārādhya vartamānaḥ atra indra ādau mama bhūte avasthitaḥ aham yajñaiḥ ārādhya mahāyajña naimittika anuṣṭhāna velāyām adhikāriṇām anusandheyam etad idam sādhāraṇam antakāle mām smaran kalevaram tyaktvā yaḥ prayāti mad yāti mama yaḥ svabhāvaḥ tam yāti tadānīm mām anusandhatte tathāvidha ākāraḥ bhavati bharata tadānīm smaryamāṇa mṛga sajātīya ākārāt saṃbhūtāḥ ante antakāle yam yam smaran kalebaram tyajati tam tam maraṇa anantaram eti antima pratyayaḥ bhāvita viṣaya jāyate yasmāt kāla abhyasta viṣaya pratyayaḥ jāyate tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu āprayāṇa at ahar ahar mām anusmara aharahar karam yuddha ādikam varṇa āśrama anubandhi coditam naimittikam kuru upāyena mayi arpita buddhiḥ kale mām smaran abhilaṣita prakāram mām prāpsyasi atra saṃśayaḥ aharahar abhyāsa yogābhyām yukta gāminā cetasā antakāle paramam divyam mām vakṣyamāṇa prakāram cintayan mām yāti bharata mṛga prāptivat aiśvarya mad ākāraḥ bhavati abhyāsaḥ naimittikā viruddheṣu sarveṣu kāleṣu manasā upāsya saṃśīlanam yoga ḥ aharahar yoga kāle anuṣṭhīyamānam ukta lakṣaṇam upāsanam prayāṇa kāle manasā acalena bhaktyā yuktaḥ yoga balena iva bhruvoḥ madhye prāṇam āveśya samyak tam upaiti divyam kavim sarvajñan purāṇam purātanam anuśāsitāram viśvasya praśāsitāram aṇoḥ aṇīyāṃsam jīvāt sūkṣmataram sarvasya dhātāram sarvasya sraṣṭāram acintya rūpam sakala visajātīya svarūpam varṇam tamasaḥ parastād aprākṛta svāsa ādhāraṇa divya rūpam tam evaṃbhūtam aharahar abhyasyamāna bhakti yukta yoga balena ārūḍha acalena manasā prayāṇa kāle bhruvoḥ madhye prāṇam āveśya saṃsthāpya madhye divyam yaḥ anusmaret tam upaiti yāti samānāi śvaryaḥ bhavati yad asthūla guṇakam veda vadanti vīta rāgāḥ yatayaḥ yad viśanti yad prāptum icchantaḥ brahmacaryam caranti padam saṃgraheṇa pravakṣye padyate gamyate cetasā padam nikhila vedyam mad svarūpam upāsyam saṃkṣepeṇa pravakṣyāmi om vyāharan mām anusmaran yaḥ prayāti tyajan deham yāti paramām gatim śrotra ādī ni dvāra bhūtāni saṃyamya vyāpārebhyaḥ vinivartya hṛdaya kamala niviṣṭe mayi akṣare nirudhya yoga ākhyām dhāraṇām āsthitaḥ mayi niścalām āsthitaḥ om mad vācakam vyāharan vācyam mām anusmaran prāṇam mūrdhni ādhāya deham tyajan yaḥ prayāti yāti paramām gatim prakṛti viyuktam mad ākāram apunarāvṛttim ātmānam prāpnoti yaḥ sarveṣu naśyatsu vinaśyati śaḥ mām udyoga prabhṛti satatam sarvakālam cetāḥ yaḥ smarati atyartha mad mad smṛtyā vinā dhāraṇam alabhamānaḥ niratiśaya priyām smṛtim yaḥ karoti yuktasya kāṅkṣamāṇasya aham sulabhaḥ aham prāpyaḥ mad aiśvarya ādikaḥ su prāpaḥ viyogam asahamānaḥ aham tam vṛṇe yam eṣa vṛṇute tena labhyaḥ śrūyate mad prāpti anuguṇa upāsana vipākam virodhi nirasanam atyartha mad ādikam aham dadāmi vakṣyate satata yuktānām bhajatām prīti pūrvakam dadāmi tam yena mām upāyānti mām prāpya punar nikhila duḥkha ālayam aśāśvatam asthiram prāpnuvanti yata mahātmānaḥ mahāmanasaḥ avasthita mad jñānānā atyartha mad mayā vinā dhāraṇam alabhamānā mayi āskta manasaḥ mad āśrayā mām upāsya parama saṃsiddhi rūpam mām prāptāḥ paryantāḥ brahmāṇḍa udara vartinaḥ lokā bhogāi śvarya ālayāḥ punarāvartinaḥ vināśinaḥ ata aiśvarya gatim prāptānām prāpya vināśāt vināśi avarjanīyam mām sarvajñam saṅkalpam nikhila laya līlam parama kāruṇikam sadā rūpam prāptānām vināśa prasaṅga punarjanma vidyate avyaktāt vyaktayaḥ sarvāḥ prabhavanti ahar āgame rātri āgame pralīyante avyakta saṃjñake grāmaḥ ayam bhūtvā bhūtvā pralīyate rātri āgame avaśaḥ pārtha prabhavati ahar āgame ye caturmukha antānām mad saṅkalpa ahorātra vyavasthā janāḥ brahmaṇaḥ caturmukhasya yad ahar caturyuga sahasra avasānam viduḥ rātriṃ tathārūpām brahmaṇaḥ ahar āgama samaye trailokya vartinyaḥ indriya bhogya rūpā vyakta ḥ caturmukha ava sthāt avyaktāt prabhavanti avyakta viśeṣe caturmukha dehe rātri āgama samaye pralīyante ayam vaśyaḥ grāmaḥ ahar āgame bhūtvā bhutvā rātri āgame pralīyate punar ahar āgame prabhavati varṣata ava sāna yuga sahasra ante paryantā lokāḥ brahmā apsu pralīyate tejasi līyante ityādi avyakta tamaḥ paryantam mayi pralīyante mad vyatiriktasya kṛtsnasya kāla vyavasthayā matta utpatteḥ mayi pralayāt vināśa yogi avarjanīyam aiśvarya gatim prāptānām punarāvṛttiḥ aparihāryā mām upetānām punarāvṛtti avyaktaḥ ukta ḥ tam āhuḥ paramām gatim yam prāpya nivartante dhāma paramam mama tasmāt avyaktāt acetana prakṛti rūpāt utkṛṣṭaḥ ākāra tasmāt visajātīyaḥ avyaktaḥ kenacid pramāṇena vyajyata avyaktaḥ saṃvedya svāsa ādhāraṇa ākāra sanātanaḥ vināśān nityaḥ yaḥ sarveṣu kāraṇeṣu kāryeṣu vinaśyatsu sthitaḥ vinaśyati avyaktaḥ uktaḥ ye anirdeśyam paryupāsate kūṭa sthaḥ ucyate ityādiṣu tam veda paramām gatim āhuḥ ayam yaḥ prayāti tyajan deham yāti paramām gatim atra parama nirdiṣṭaḥ akṣaraḥ prakṛti saṃsarga viyukta svarūpeṇa avasthita yam evaṃbhūtam rūpeṇa avasthitam prāpya nivartante mama paramam dhāma niyamana sthānam acetana ekam niyamana sthānam saṃsṛṣṭa rūpā dvitīyam niyamana sthānam acit saṃsarga viyuktam rūeṇa avathitam svarūpam paramam niyamana sthānam punarāvṛtti rūpam vācī dhāma jñānam abhipretam prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭāt parichinna rūpāt aparicchinna svarūpam dhāma mattaḥ parataram anyat kiñcid dhanaṃjaya mayi sarvam idam protam sūtre maṇi gaṇā iva agniḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsā uttarāyaṇam prayātā gacchanti janāḥ atra kāla mārgasya ahar prabhṛti saṃvata ra kāla mārga yasmin mārge prayātā anāvṛttim puṇya karmāṇaḥ āvṛttim yānti tam mārgam vakṣyāmi agniḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsā uttarāyaṇam saṃvatsara ādīnām pradarśanam etad dhūma mārga pitṛ ādeḥ pradarśanam atra yogi puṇya saṃbandhi viṣayaḥ śuklā gatiḥ ādikā kṛṣṇā dhūma ādikā śukla yāna āvṛttim yāti kṛṣṇayā punar āvartate śukla kṛṣṇe gatī jñāninām vividhānām puṇya karmaṇām śrutau śāśvate mate ya ittham viduḥ ye araṇye śraddhā tapa upāsate arciṣam abhisaṃbhavanti ya iṣṭāpūrte dattam upāsate dhūmam abhisaṃbhavanti etau mārgau jānan yogī prayāṇa kāle kaścana muhyati yānena pathā yāti tasmāt aharahar cira cinta ākhya yoga yuktaḥ bhava ṛc yaju ssāma atharva veda abhyāsa tapaḥ dāna prabhṛtiṣu sarveṣu puṇyeṣu yad nirdiṣṭam idam adhyāya dvaya uditam bhagavat māhātmyam viditvā sarvam atyeti etad vedana atirekeṇa sarvam tṛṇavan manyate yogī jñānī bhūtvā jñāninaḥ prāpyam ādyam sthānam upaiti idam guhyatamam bhakti rūpam upāsana ākhyam jñānam sahitam upāsana gata sahitam anasūyave pravakṣyāmi mad viṣayam sakala visajātīyam aparimita prakāram māhātmyam śrutvā saṃbhavati manu ānāya pravakṣyāmi yaj jñānam anuṣṭhāna paryantam jñātvā mad prāpti virodhinaḥ sarvasmāt aśubhān mokṣyase rāja vidyānām rājā rāja guhyam guhyānām rājā rājñām rāja rājānaḥ vistīrṇa agādhya manasaḥ mahāmanasām iyam mahāmanasa gopanīya gopana kuśalā guhyam idam uttamam pavitram mad prāpti virodhi aśeṣa kalmaṣa apaham avagamam avagamyata avagamaḥ viṣayaḥ bhūtaḥ avagamaḥ viṣayaḥ yasya jñānasya avagamam bhakti rūpeṇa upāsanena upāsyamānaḥ aham tādānīm upāsituḥ pratyakṣatām upagataḥ bhavāmi dharmyam dharmāt anapetam niśśreyasa sādhana rūpeṇa atyartha tadānīm mad darśana āpādana svayam niśśreyasa rūpam niratiśaya niśśreyasa ātyantika mad prāpti sādhanam ata su sukham kartum su upādānam atyartha ena upādeyam avyayam akṣayam mad prāptim sādhayitvā svayam kṣīyate evaṃrūpam upāsanam mad pradāne kṛte kiṃcid kṛtam mayā me pratibhāti upāsana ākhyasya dharmasya niratiśaya madviṣaya svayam niratiśaya rūpasya parama niśśreyasa mad prāpti sādhanasya avyayasya upādāna yogya daśāyām prāpya aśraddadhānāḥ viśvāsa tvarā rahitāḥ puruṣāḥ mām aprāpya rūpe vartmani nitarām vartante ahaḥ idam āścaryam mad sthāni bhūtāni paśya me aiśvaram bhṛt sthaḥ mama bhūtabhāvanaḥ idam cetana cetana ātmakam kṛtsnam jagad avyakta mūrtinā aprakāśita svarūpeṇa mayā antaryāmiṇā tatam jagataḥ niyamana śeṣi vyāptam brāhmaṇe yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhan yam veda ya tiṣṭhan yam veda cetana acetana vastu jātaiḥ adṛṣṭeṇa antaryāmiṇā vyāptiḥ uktā tataḥ mad sthāni bhūtāni bhūtāni mayi antaryāmiṇi sthitāni brāhmaṇe yasya yaḥ pṛthivīm antaraḥ yamayati yasya ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati niyāmya pratipādanāt tadāyatte niyamane pratipādite śeṣi aham teṣu avasthitaḥ aham āyatta sthitiḥ mad sthitau taiḥ kaścid upakāra athaḥ mad sthāni bhūtāni ghaṭa ādīnām jala ādeḥ iva mama dhāraka katham mad saṅkalpena paśya mama aiśvaram kutracid asaṃbhāvanīyam mad sādhāraṇam āścaryam paśya kaḥ asau yoga bhṛt sthaḥ mama bhūtabhāvanaḥ bhūtānām bhartā aham taiḥ kaścid mama upakāraḥ mama bhūtabhāvanaḥ mama saṅkalpa bhūtānām bhāvayitā dhārayitā niyantā ākaśe anālambane mahān vayuḥ sthitaḥ gacchati vāyuḥ nirālambanaḥ mad āyatta sthitiḥ abhyupagamanīyaḥ bhūtāni taiḥ adṛṣṭe mayi sthitāni mayā dhṛtā ani upadhāraya āhuḥ veda megha udayaḥ sāgara sannivṛttiḥ indoḥ sphuritāni vāyoḥ vidyut vibhaṅgaḥ gatiḥ uṣṇa raśmeḥ viṣṇoḥ prabhavanti māyāḥ viṣṇoḥ sādhāraṇāni mahā āścaryāṇi śrutiḥ etasya akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate bhīṣodeti sūryaḥ bhīṣā asmāt agniḥ indraḥ ādikā sthāvara jaṅgama ātmakāni bhūtāni māmikām mad bhūtām prakṛtim tamaḥ vācyām vibhāgān arhām kalpa kṣaye catur mukha ava sāna samaye mad saṅkalpāt yānti bhūtāni kalpa ādau punar visṛjyāmi aham manuḥā āsīt idam tamaḥ abhidhyāya śarīrāt svāt śrutiḥ yasya akṣare līyate tamasi līyate ādikā tam āsīt tamasā gūḍham agre praketam svakīyām vicitra pariṇāminīm prakṛtim avaṣṭabhya aṣṭadhā pariṇāmyy imam caturvidham tiryak sthāvara ātmakam grāmam madīyāyā mohinyā mayyāḥ prakṛteḥ vaśād avaśam punar punar kāle kāle visṛjāmi viṣama sṛṣṭi ādīni karmāṇi mām nibadhnanti mayi nairghṛṇya ādikam apādayanti yataḥ kṣetrajñānām kṛtāni karmāṇi viṣama hetavaḥ aham vaiṣamye asaktaḥ udāsīn avat sūtra kāraḥ naiḥ ghṛṇye tasmāt kṣetrajña anuguṇam madīyā saṅkalpena mayā īkṣitā sacarācaram sūyate kṣetrajña anuguṇam dīkṣaṇena hetunā parivartata mad svāmyam saṅkalpa nairghṛṇya rahita ādikam mama vasudeva sūnoḥ aiśvaram paśya śrutiḥ asmān māyī sṛjate viśvam etad tasmin māyayā sanniruddhaḥ māyām prakṛtim vidyān māyinam mha īśvaram mām maheśvaram sarvajñam saṅkalpam nikhila kāraṇam parama kāruṇika samāśrayaṇīya tvāya mānuṣīm tanum āśritam kṛtaiḥ pāpa karmabhiḥ mūḍhā avajānanti prākṛta samam manyante maheśvarasya mama pāraka aruṇya udārya sauśīlya vātsalī nibandhanam samāśrayaṇa lakṣaṇam imam ajānantaḥ samāśrayaṇa mātreṇa mām itarasa jātīyam matvā tiraskurvanti mama tve parama kāruṇī paratvati rodhān karīm rākṣasīm āsurīm mohinīm prakṛtim āśritāḥ mogha āśāḥ moghvān chitāḥ niṣphalavān chitāḥ moghkarmāṇaḥ mogha ārambhāḥ mogha jñānāḥ sarveṣu madīyeṣu carācareṣu artheṣu viparīta niṣphala jñānāḥ vicetasaḥ vigata yāthātmya jñānāḥ mām sarveśvaram samam matvā mayi yad kartum icchanti yad uddiśya ārambhān kurvate sarvam mogham bhavati ye kṛtaiḥ puṇya sañcayaiḥ mām śaraṇam upagamya vidhvasta samasta pāpa bandhā daivīm prakṛtim āśritā mahātmānaḥ bhūtādim avyayam manasā agocara svarūpam parama kāruṇika sādhu paritrāṇāya avatīrṇam mām jñātvā manasaḥ mām bhajante mad atirekeṇa mad bhajanena vinā manasaḥ bāhya karaṇānām dhāraṇam alabhamānā mad bhajana prayojanā bhajante atyartha mad mad kīrtanayatana namaskāraiḥ vinā kṣaṇa aṇu mātre dhāraṇam alabhamānāḥ mad vācīni mad nāmāni smṛtvā pulaka āñcita aṅgāḥ harṣa gadgada kaṇṭhāḥ nārāyaṇa kṛṣṇa vāsa it ādīni satatam kīrtayantaḥ yatantaḥ mad karmasu arcana ādikeṣu upakāreṣu bhavana nandana vana karaṇa ādikeṣu dṛḍha saṅkalpā yatamānāḥ bhakti bhārau anam ita abhimāna pada dvaya kara dvaya śirobhiḥ aṣṭa aṅgaiḥ acintita pāṃsu kardama śarkarā ādike dharā tale daṇḍavat praṇipatantaḥ satatam mām yuktāḥ kāṅkṣamāṇā antam mad dāsya vyavasāyinaḥ upāsate mahātmanaḥ uktaiḥ kīrtana ādibhiḥ ākhyena yajñena yajantaḥ mām upāsate katham bahudhā pṛthaktvena ākāreṇa viśvatomukham viśva prakāram avasthitam mām ena upāsate etad bhavati bhagavān vāsudeva vibhāgān sūkṣma cit cit vastu ḥ san saṅkalpaḥ vividha vibhakta sthūla cit cit vastu śarīraḥ syām saṃkalpya tiryak sthāvara ākhya vicitra śarīraḥ avatiṣṭhata anusaṃdadhānāḥ mām upāsate aham aham jyotiṣṭoma ādikaḥ aham mahāyajñaḥ aham pitṛ gaṇa puṣṭi dā svadhā auṣadham haviḥ aham aham mantraḥ aham ājyam pradarśana idam soma ādikam havir aham aham āhavanīya ādikaḥ agniḥ homaḥ aham sthāvara jaṅgama ātmakasya jagataḥ pitṛ mātṛ dhātṛ pitāmaha vartamānaḥ aham atra dhātṛ mātā pitṛ vyatirikte prayojake cetana viśeṣe vartate yad kiñcid veda vedyam pavitram pāvanam aham vedakaḥ veda bīja bhūtaḥ praṇavaḥ aham ṛc sāma yajuḥ ātmakaḥ vedaḥ aham gamyata gatiḥ prāpya sthānam bhartā dhārayitā prabhuḥ śāsitā sākṣī dṛṣṭā nivāsaḥ vāsasthānam veśma śaraṇam iṣṭasya prāpaka aniṣṭasya nivāraṇa samāśrayaṇīyaḥ cetanaḥ śaraṇam aham su kṛt dhita eṣī prabhava pralaya sthānam yasya kasyacid kutracid pralayayoḥ yad sthānam aham nidhānam nidhīyata nidhānam utpādyam upasaṃhāryam aham avyayam bījam vyaya rahitam yad kāraṇam aham āt rūpeṇa aham tapāmi grīṣma ādau aham varṣam nigṛhṇāmi varṣāsu aham utsṛjāmi amṛtam iva mṛtyuḥ yena jīvati lokaḥ yena mriyate bhayam aham kim atra bahu uktena sat aham sat yad vartate asad yad atītam anāgatam avasthita cit cit vastu prakāraḥ aham avasthita bahudhā pṛthaktvena vibhakta avasthita prakāraḥ aham avasthita jñānena ananu saṃdadhānāḥ mām upāsate tam bhuktvā svarga lokam viśālam kṣīṇe puṇye martya lokam viśanti trayī anuprapannāḥ gatāgatam kāmā labhante ṛc yajussāma rūpāḥ tisraḥ vidyāḥ vidyam kevalam vidya niṣṭhāḥ traividyāḥ trayī niṣṭhāḥ trayī niṣṭhā mahātmanaḥ ukta prakāreṇa nikhila veda vedyam mām jñātvā atimātra mad bhakti kārita kīrtana ādibhiḥ yajñena mad prāpyā mām upāsate traividyāḥ veda pratipādya kevala indra yāga somān pibantaḥ pūta pāpāḥ svarga prāpti virodhi pāpāt pūtāḥ taiḥ kevala indra devatyatayā anusaṃhitaiḥ yajñaiḥ vastu rūpam mām iṣṭvā avasthitam mām ajānantaḥ svarga gatim prārthayante puṇyam duḥkha saṃbhinnam sura indra lokam prāpya divyān bhogān aśnanti tam viśālam svarga lokam bhuktvā anubhava bhūte puṇye kṣīṇe punar martya lokam viśanti trayī siddha vidhurāḥ kāmya svarga kāmāḥ kevalam trayī anuprapannāḥ gatāgatam labhante sthira svarga ādīn punar punar nivartanta ananyāḥ prayojanāḥ mad cintanena vinā alābhān mad cintana prayojanāḥ mām cintayantaḥ ye mahātmānaḥ janāḥ paryupāsate kalyānṇa anvitam vibhūti yuktam mām parita upāsate anyūnam upāsate abhiyuktānām mayi abhiyogam kāṅkṣamāṇānām aham mad prāpti lakṣaṇam apunarāvṛtti rūpam kṣemam vahāmi ye indra bhaktāḥ kevala trayī niṣṭhāḥ śraddhayā anvitāḥ indra ādīn yajante uktena nyāyena sarvasya mad mad indra śabdānām mad vastu mām yajante avidhi pūrvakam yajante indra ādīnām devatānām karamsvārādhya anvayam vākyāni catur hotāraḥ saṃpadam gacchanti deaiḥ ityādīni vidadhati pūrvakam yajante jātam parama avasthitānām indra ādīnām ārādhya vidadhat atma parama puruṣasya ārādhya vidadhāti catur hotāraḥ darśa pūrṇam āsa ādīni karmāṇi paramātmani avasthite indra devaiḥ saṃpadam gacchanti indra devānām ārādhanāni etāni karmāṇi i ti imām saṃpadam gacchanti prabhuḥ pradātā aham vrata saṅklpa vācī devavratāḥ darśa pūrṇamāsa ādibhiḥ karmabhiḥ indra ādīn yajāmahe indra ya jana saṅkalpā ye indra ādīn devān yānti ye pitṛ ādibhiḥ pitñn yajāmahe pitṛ ya jana saṅkalpāḥ pitñn yānti ye yakṣara kaṣaḥ piśāca ādīni bhūtāni yajāmahe yajana saṅkalpāḥ bhūtāni yānti ye taiḥ yajñaiḥ pitṛ śarīrakam paramātmānam bhagavantam vāsudevam yajāmahe mām yajante madya ajinaḥ mām yānti vratāḥ ādīn prāpya taiḥ parimitam bhogam bhuktvā vinaśa kāle taiḥ vinaṣṭā bhavanti mad ya ajina ḥ mām nidhanam sarvajñam saṅkalpam anavadhika atiśaya saṃkhyeya kalyāṇa gaṇa mahā udadhim anavadhika atiśaya ānandam prāpya punar nivartanta sulabham patram puṣpam toyam yaḥ bhaktyā me prayacchati atyartha mad pradānena vinā dhāraṇam alabhamāna prayojanaḥ yaḥ me patra ādikam dadāti prayata śuddhi yukta manasaḥ tathāvidha bhakti upahṛtam aham īśvaraḥ nikhila udaya vibhava laya avāpta samasta kāmaḥ saṅkalpaḥ anavadhika atiśaya saṃkhyeya kalyāṇa gaṇaḥ svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya anubhave vartamānaḥ manoratha patha dūra varti priyam prāpya aśnāmi dharme yāḥ kriyāḥ saṃprayuktā aḥ syuḥ ekānta gata buddhibhiḥ sarvāḥ śirasā devaḥ pratigṛhṇāti vai svayam yad yātrā aśeṣa laukikam karoṣi yad dhāraṇāya aśnāsi yad vaidikam homa dāna tapaḥ prabhṛti naimittikam karoṣi sarvam mad arpaṇam kuruṣva arpyata arpaṇam sarvasya laukikasya vaidikasya karmaṇaḥ ārādhya mayi samarpitam bhavati kuru etad bhavati yāga dāna ārādhya pratīyamānānām ādīnām bhoktuḥ tava madīyatayā mad saṅkalpa āyatta pravṛtti mayi parama śeṣiṇi parama kartari tvām kartāram bhoktāram ārādhakam ārādhyam jātam ārādhanam jātam sarvam samarpaya tava mad niyāmya kama cheṣa rasa tām ārādhya ādeḥ etad svabhāva garbhatām atyartha prīti yuktaḥ anusaṃdhatsva saṃnyāsa ākhya yoga yukta manāḥ ātmānam mad tām at niyāmyata rasam sarvam mad ārādhanam anusaṃdadhānaḥ laukikam vaidikam kurvan śubha aśubha phalaiḥ anantaiḥ prācīna ākhyaiḥ bandhanaiḥ mad prāpti virodhibhiḥ sarvaiḥ mokṣyase taiḥ vimuktaḥ mām eṣyasi tiryak sthāvara avasthiteṣu jātitaḥ ākārataḥ svabhāvataḥ jñānataḥ utkṛṣṭa apakṛṣṭa rūpeṇa vartamāneṣu sarveṣu samāśrayaṇīya tve samaḥ aham ayam jāti ākāra svabhāva ādibhiḥ nirkṛṣṭa samāśrayaṇe me dveṣyaḥ udvejanīya tyājyaḥ samāśrita atirekeṇa jāti ādibhiḥ atyanta utkṛṣṭaḥ ayam vyukta samāśrayaṇe kaścid priyaḥ saṃgrāhyaḥ atyartha mad mad bhajanena vinā alābhān mad bhajana prayojanā ye mām bhajante jāti ādibhiḥ utkṛṣṭā apakṛṣṭā mad guṇavat yathāsukham mayi vartante aham teṣu mad utkṛṣṭa iṣu iva varte jāti viśeṣe jātānām yaḥ samācāra upādeyaḥ pariharaṇīyaḥ tasmāt ativṛttaḥ ukta prakāreṇa mām bhajana prayojanaḥ bhajate sādhuḥ vaiṣṇava agresara mantavyaḥ bahu mantavyaḥ uktaiḥ sama kuta etad samyak vyavasitaḥ yataḥ vyavasāyaḥ su samīcīnaḥ bhagavān nikhila bhūtaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ patiḥ asmad svāmī mama guruḥ mama suhṛd mama paramam bhogyam sarvaiḥ duṣprāpaḥ ayam vyavasāya ḥ tena kṛtaḥ prayojanam nirantaram bhajanam ataḥ sādhuḥ bahu mantavyaḥ vyavasāye ukta prakāra bhajane saṃpanne vyatikramaḥ su vaikalyam tāvatā anādaraṇīyaḥ bahu mantavya mad kāritān mad bhajanena vidhūta pāpa unmūlita rajaḥ tamaḥ guṇaḥ kṣipram bhavati kṣipram virodhiḥ ahita parikara mat bha jana ekamanā bhavati evaṃrūpa bhajanam dharmasya parantapa upakrame uditam śaśvat śāntim nigacchati śaśvatīm apunarāvartinīm mad prāpti virodhi nivṛttim gacchati kaunteya arthe pratijñām kuru mad bhaktau upakrāntaḥ virodhi miśraḥ naśyati mad bhakti māhātmyena sarvam virodhi jātam nāśayitvā śāśvatīm virodhi nivṛttim adhigamya kṣipram paripūrṇa bhaktiḥ bhavati kim punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayaḥ anityam asukham lokam imam prāpya bhajasva mām striyaḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ pāpa yona yaḥ mām vyapāśritya parām gatim yānti kim punar puṇya yona yaḥ brāhmaṇā rājarṣayaḥ mad bhaktim āsthitāḥ ataḥ rājarṣiḥ asthiram tāpa traya abhihata asukham imam lokam prāpya vartamānaḥ mām bhajasva mad manā bhava mayi īśvara īśvare nikhila pratyanīka kalyāṇa tāne sarvajñe saṅkalpe nikhila kāraṇe parasmin brahmaṇi puruṣottame puṇḍarī ka dalā amala āyata svaccha nīla jīmūta saṅkāśe yugapad udita dinakara sahasra sadṛśa tejasi lāvaṇya mahā udadhau udāra pīvara catur bāhau ujjvala pīta ambare amala kirīṭa makara hāra keyūra kaṭaka bhūṣite apāraka aruṇya sauśīlya saundarya mādhurya gāmbhīryā dārya vātsalī jaladhau anālocita aśeṣa śaraṇye svāmini taila dhārāvat avicchedena niviṣṭa manā bhava viśinaṣṭi mad bhaktaḥ atyartha mad yuktaḥ mad manā bhava punar viśinaṣṭi mad yājī anavadhika atiśaya priyamadanubhava kārita madya jana bhava yajanam paripūrṇa aupacārika sāṃsparśika abhyavahāri kā sakala rūpaḥ yāgaḥ mad anubhava janita nirvadhikā atiśaya prīti kārita madya jana bhavasi mad manā bhava bhavati punar viśinaṣṭi mām namaskuru anavadhika atiśaya madanubhava kārita atyartha aśeṣa vṛttau aparyavasyan mayi antarātmani atimātra prahvībhāva vyavasāyam kuru mad parāyaṇaḥ aham ayanam yasya asau mad parāyaṇaḥ mayā vinā saṃbhāvanayā mad ātmānam yuktvā mad parāyaṇaḥ anavadhika atiśaya prītyā mad anubhava samartham prāpya mām eṣyasi atra viṣayaḥ evaṃrūpeṇa manasā mām dhyātvā mām mām iṣṭvā mām namaskṛtya mad parāyaṇaḥ mām prāpsyasi laukikāni arthāni vaidikāni naimittikāni karmāṇi mad prītaye mad rasaḥ mayā kārita kurvan satatam mad kīrtanayatana namaskāra ādikān prītyā kurvāṇaḥ mad niyāmyam nikhila jagan mad rasam sandhānaḥ atyartha mad gaṇam sandhāya āharahar ukta lakṣaṇam idam upāsanam upādadānaḥ mām prāpsyasi mama māhātmyam śrutvā prīyamāṇāya mad bhakti vivṛddhi hita kāmanayā mad māhātmya prapañca viṣayam paramam vacaḥ yad vakṣyāmi avahita manāḥ śṛṇu sura gaṇā mahā ṛṣayaḥ indriya darśinaḥ adhikatara jñānā me prabhavam prabhāvam viduḥ mama svabhāva ādikam jānanti yataḥ devānām mahā ṛṣīṇām śaḥ aham svarūpasya ādeḥ aham am ahā ṛṣi puṇya anuguṇam mayā dattam jñānam parimitam ataḥ parimita jñānā mad ādikam yathāvan jānanti jāyata ajaḥ vikāridravyād acetanāt saṃsṛṣṭāt saṃsāri cetanā c visajātīya saṃsāri cetanasya ācid saṃsargaḥ anādim padena ādimataḥ ajān visajātīya aja saṃbandhasya vṛtta arhatā ataḥ anādim anarha pratyanīka ucyate niravadyam ityādi śrutyā pratyanīka anarham mām maheśvaram īśvarāṇām īśvaram martyeṣu asaṃmūḍhaḥ yaḥ vetti itarasa jātīya ekīkṛtya mohaḥ saṃmohaḥ rahitaḥ asaṃmūḍhaḥ mad bhakti virodhibhiḥ sarvaiḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate etad bhavati manuṣyāṇām rājā sajātīyaḥ kenacid karmaṇā ādhipatyam prāptaḥ devānām aṇḍa saṃsāri sajātīyaḥ bhāvanā traya antargata yaḥ brahmāṇam vidadhāti ye kecana aṇima aiśvaryam prāptāḥ ayam maheśvaraḥ avasthāt acetanāt baddhān muktā c cetanāt iśita vyāt sarvasmān nikhila pratyanīkāna vadhika atiśaya saṃkhyeya kalyāṇa tāna niyamana svabhāva visajātīya ītra jātīya moha rahitaḥ yaḥ mām vetti sarvaiḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate ahiṃsā sama tuṣṭhi ḥ tapaḥ dānam yaśaḥ ayaśaḥ bhavanti bhāvā bhūtānām matta pṛthagvidhāḥ buddhiḥ manasaḥ nirūpaṇa sāmarthyam jñānam cit cit vastu viṣayaḥ niścayaḥ asaṃmohaḥ gṛhītāt rajata ādeḥ visajātīye śuktikā vastuni sajātīya nivṛttiḥ kṣamā hetau avikṛta satyam viṣayam hita rūpam vacanam anuguṇā abhipretā vṛtti at damaḥ bāhya karaṇānām anartha viṣayebhyaḥ niyamanam śamaḥ antaḥkaraṇasya niyamanam sukham anukūla anubhavaḥ duḥkham pratikūla anubhavaḥ bhavaḥ bhavanam anukūla anubhava hetukam manasaḥ bhavanam pratikūla anubhava kaḥ manasaḥ avasādaḥ bhayam āgāminaḥ duḥkhasya darśana jam duḥkham nivṛttiḥ abhayam ahiṃsā duḥkha sama sukṛtsu vipakṣeṣu anarthayoḥ samam tuṣṭiḥ sarveṣu ātmasu dṛṣṭeṣu toṣa svabhāva tapaḥ śāstrīyaḥ saṅkoca rūpaḥ kāya kleśaḥ dānam svakīya bhogyānam parasmai pratipādanam yaśaḥ guṇavat prathā ayaśaḥ nairguṇya prathā etad bhayam anuguṇa vṛtti dvayam mantavyam tapaḥ dāne ādyāḥ bhūtānām bhāvāḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti hetavaḥ vṛttayaḥ matta mad saṅkalpa āyattā bhavanti mahā ṛṣayaḥ atīta manvantare ye bhṛgu mahā ṛṣa yaḥ sṛṣṭi pravartanāya brahmaṇaḥ mana ssaṃbhavāḥ pravartanāya ye sārvaṇikā catvāraḥ manavaḥ sthitāḥ yeṣām santāna maye jātā imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ pratikṣaṇam āpralayāt apatyānām utpādakāḥ pālakāḥ bhavanti bhṛgu manavaḥ mad bhāvāḥ mama yaḥ yeṣām mad bhāvāḥ mad mate sthitāḥ mad saṅkalpā nuvartina vibhūtiḥ aiśvaryam etām sarvasya mad āyatta pravṛtti rūpām vibhūtim mama pratyanīka kalyāṇa gaṇa rūpam yaḥ tattvataḥ vetti avikampena aprakampyena bhakti yogena yujyate atra saṃśayaḥ mad vibhūti viṣayam kalyāṇa viṣayam jñānam bhakti yoga vardhanam svayam drakṣyasi abhiprāyaḥ aham sarvasya vicitra cit cit prapañcasya prabhavaḥ kāraṇam sarvam matta pravartate idam mama svābhāvikam niraṃkuśāi śvaryam sauśīlya saundarya vātsalī kalyāṇa gaṇa matvā budhā jñāninaḥ samanvitāḥ mām kalyāṇa anvitam bhajante vṛtti viśeṣaḥ mayi spṛhayā alavaḥ mām bhajanta mad cittāḥ mayi niviṣṭa manasaḥ mad gata mad gata jīvitāḥ mayā vinā dhāraṇam alabhamānā svaiḥ svaiḥ anubhūtān madīyān guṇān parasparam bodhayantaḥ madīyāni divyāni ramaṇīyāni karmāṇi kathayantaḥ tuṣyanti ramanti vaktāraḥ vacanena prayojanena tuṣyanti śrotāraḥ śravaṇena anavadhika atiśaya priyeṇa ramante satata yuktānām mayi satata āśaṃsamānānām mām bhajamānānām aham tam vipāka daśa āpannam prīti pūrvakam dadāmi yena mām upayānti anugraha aham sthaḥ vṛttau viṣaya avasthitaḥ madīyān kalyāṇa gaṇān mad viṣaya ākhyena bhāsvatā dīpena virodhi prācīna ajñāna jam mad vyatirikta abhyasta viṣaya prāvaṇya rūpam tamaḥ nāśayāmi ab śāśvatam divyam ādidevam ajam vibhum ṛṣayaḥ parāvara tattva yāthātmya tvām śāśvatam divyam ādidevam ajam vibhum āhuḥ devarṣiḥ nāradaḥ asitaḥ devalaḥ vyāsaḥ ye vipraḥ ye adhyā janāḥ vadanti mahātmānam kṛṣṇam sanātanam ataḥ sarvam etad avasthita vastu kathanam manye praśaṃsā abhiprāyam yad mām sādhāraṇam anavadhika atiśayam svābhāvikam tava aiśvaryam kalyāṇa ānantyam vadasi ataḥ bhagavan niratiśaya balāi śvarya vīrya tejasām nidhe vyaktim vyañjana prakāram parimita jñānā devāḥ dānavāḥ viduḥ he puruṣottama ātmānam tvām svayam jñānena vettha bhāvana bhūtānām utpādayitaḥ bhūteśa niyantaḥ devadeva daivatānām parama daivata mṛga pakṣi sarīsṛpa ādīn saundarya sauśīlya kalyāṇa gaṇaiḥ daivatāni atītya vartante daivatāni taiḥ taiḥ guṇaiḥ atītya vartamāna jagatpate jagatsvāmin divyāḥ tvad asādha araṇyaḥ vibhūtayaḥ yāḥ aśeṣeṇa vaktum arhasi vyañjaya yābhiḥ anantābhiḥ vibhūtibhiḥ yaiḥ niyamana viśeṣaiḥ yuktaḥ imān lokān niyantṛ vyāpya tiṣṭhasi aham yogī bhakti yoga niṣṭhaḥ san bhaktyā tvām sadā paricintayan cintayitum pravṛttaḥ cintanīyam tvām paripūrṇa aiśvarya kalyāṇa gaṇam katham vidyām ukta vyatirikteṣu keṣu keṣu bhāveṣu mayā niyantṛ cintyaḥ asi aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate saṃkṣepeṇa tava sraṣṭṛ vibhūtim niyamanam vistareṇa kathaya tvayā ucyamānam tvad māhātmya amṛtam śṛṇvataḥ me tṛptiḥ mama tṛptiḥ tvayā vidita abhiprāyaḥ he kuru śreṣṭha madīyāḥ kalyāṇīḥ vibhūtīḥ prādhānyataḥ kathayiṣyāmi prādhanya śabdena utkarṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ purodhasām mukhyam mām vakṣyate jagati utkṛṣṭāḥ kāścana vibhūtīḥ vakṣyāmi vistareṇa vaktum śrotum śakyate tāsām ānantyāt vibhūti niyāmya bhūtānām pṛthagvidhā bhāvā matta bhavanti uktvā etām vibhūtim mama yaḥ vetti tattvataḥ pratipādanāt yoga nirdiṣṭam sraṣṭṛ ādikam vibhuti nirdiṣṭam pravartya punar aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate matvā bhajante mām budhā samanvitāḥ bhūtānām mama bhūtānām āśaye hṛdaye aham avasthitaḥ śarīrasya ādhāraḥ niyantā śeṣī vakṣyate sarvasya aham sanniviṣṭaḥ matta ḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam apohanam īśvaraḥ bhūtānām hṛd deśe arjuna tiṣṭhati bhrāmayan bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā saṃkhyātānām ādityānām dvādaśaḥ ya utkṛṣṭaḥ viṣṇuḥ ādityaḥ aham jyotiṣām jagati prakāśakānām yaḥ aṃśumān raviḥ gaṇaḥ aham marutām utkṛṣṭaḥ marīciḥ yaḥ aham asmi nakṣatrāṇām aham śaśī iyam ṣaṣṭhī bhūtānām asmi cetanā itivat nakṣatrāṇām patiḥ yaḥ candraḥ aham asmi vedānām ṛc yajuḥ sāma ātharvaṇām ya utkṛṣṭaḥ sāmavedaḥ aham devānām indraḥ aham asmi ekādaśānām indriyāṇām yad utkṛṣṭam mana indriyam aham asmi iyam bhūtānām cetanāvatām yā cetanā aham asmi rudrāṇām ekādaśānām śaṅkaraḥ aham asmi yakṣa rakṣasām vaiśravaṇaḥ aham vasūnām aṣṭānām pāvakaḥ aham śikhariṇām śikhara śobhinām parvatānām madhye meruḥ aham purodhasām utkṛṣṭaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ yaḥ aham asmi senānīnām senāpatīnām skandaḥ aham asmi sarasām sāgaraḥ aham asmi mahā ṛṣīṇām marīci ādīnām bhṛguḥ aham abhidhāyinaḥ śabdā giraḥ tāsām ekam praṇavaḥ aham asmi yajñānām utkṛṣṭaḥ japa yajñaḥ asmi mātrāṇām himavān aham uccaiśśravasam aśvānām viddhi mām udbhavam airāvatam gaja indrāṇām narāṇām narādhipam āyudhānām aham vajram dhenūnām asmi kāmadhuk prajanaḥ asmi kandarpaḥ sarpāṇām asmi vāsukiḥ ananta ḥ asmi nāgānām yādasām aham pitñṇām aryamā asmi yamaḥ saṃyamatām aham vṛkṣāṇām pūjyaḥ aśvatthaḥ aham rṣīṇam nāradaḥ aham kāmadhuk divyā surabhiḥ janana hetuḥ kandarpaḥ aham asmi sarpāḥ ekāśirasaḥ nāgāḥ bahu śirasaḥ yādāṃsi jala vāsinaḥ aham daṇḍayatām vaivasvataḥ aham anartha prepsutayā gaṇayatām madhye kālaḥ mṛtyuḥ aham pavatām gamana svabhāvānām pavanaḥ aham śastrabhṛtām rāmaḥ aham śastrabhṛt atra vibhūtiḥ kṣetrajñā ena avasthitasya bhagavataḥ bhūtā śastrabhṛt sthānīyāḥ sṛjyanta sargāḥ kāraṇam sarvadā sṛjyamānānām prāṇinām sraṣṭāraḥ aham sarvadā saṃhriyamāṇānām saṃhartāraḥ aham madhyam pālanam sarvadā pālyamānānām pālayitāraḥ aham jalpa vitaṇḍa kurvatām tattva nirṇayāya pravṛttaḥ yaḥ aham akṣarāṇām madhye akāraḥ vai sarvā varṇānām akāraḥ aham sāmāsikaḥ samāsa samūhaḥ madhye dvandva samāsaḥ aham padārtha utkṛṣṭaḥ kalā muhūrta akṣayaḥ kālaḥ aham sarvasya sraṣṭā hiraṇyagarbhaḥ caturmukhaḥ aham haraḥ mṛtyuḥ aham utpatsyamānānām udbhava ākhyam aham śrīḥ aham kīrtiḥ aham aham smṛtiḥ aham medhā aham dhṛtiḥ aham kṣamā aham sāmnām bṛhatsāma aham chandasām gāyatrī aham kusuma ākaraḥ vasantaḥ chalam kurvatām chala āspadeṣu akṣa lakṣaṇam dyutam aham jetñṇām jayaḥ asmi vyavasāyinām vyavasāyaḥ asmi sattvavatām sattvam aham sattvam mahāmanaḥ vasudeva sūnu atra vibhūtiḥ pāṇḍavānām dhanañjayaḥ arjunaḥ aham munayaḥ mananena yāthātmya darśinaḥ vyāsaḥ aham kavayaḥ vipaścitaḥ niyama atikramaṇe daṇḍam kurvatām daṇḍaḥ aham vijigīṣūṇām jaya upāya bhūtā nītiḥ asmi guhyānām saṃbandhiṣu gaḥ pāneṣu maunam asmi jñānavatām jñānam aham bhūtānām avasthitānām bīja pratīyamānam apratīyamānam yad aham jātam mayā avasthitena vinā yad aham guḍākeśa āśaya sthitaḥ prakramāt vinā yad mayā carācaram atra avasthānam vivakṣitam sarvam vastu jātam avastham mayā bhūtena yuktam sarvasya sāmānādhikaraṇya nirdeśasya hetuḥ prakaṭitam mama divyānām kalyāṇīnām vibhūtīnām antaḥ eṣa vibhūteḥ vistaraḥ mayā kaiścid upādhibhiḥ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ yad yad vibhūtimat iśitavya saṃpannam jātam śrīmat kāntimat dhana dhānya samṛddham ūrjitam kalyāṇa ārambheṣu udyuktam mama aṃśa saṃbhavam avagaccha abhibhavana sāmarthyam mama acinti śakteḥ niyamana deśa saṃbhavati bahunā ucyamānena jñānena kim prayojanam idam cit cit ātmakam kṛtsnam avastham avastham sthūlam sadbhāve sthitau pravṛtti mad saṅkalpam ativarteta mama ayuta ayuta aṃśena viṣṭabhya aham avasthitaḥ bhagavatā parāśareṇa yasya ayuta ayuta aṃśa aṃśe viśva śaktiḥ iyam sthitā abhimāna mohena mohitasya mama anugraha prayojanāya paramam guhyam paramam rahasyam saṃjñitam vaktavyam vacaḥ aham jātu sam ityādi tasmāt yogī bhava arjuna etad antam yad tvayā tena ayam mama viṣayaḥ mohaḥ sarvaḥ vigataḥ dūrataḥ nirastaḥ saptama prabhṛti daśama paryante tvad vyatiriktānām bhūtānām tvattaḥ paramātmanaḥ bhava apyayau pralayau vistaraśaḥ mayā śrutau kamala patra akṣa tava avyayam cetana acetana vastu śeṣi bala kalyāṇa gaṇaiḥ tava paratara ādhāra cintita nimiṣita pravṛttiṣu tava pravartayitṛ ityādi aparimitam māhātmyam vakṣyamāṇa didṛkṣādyotana he parameśvara etad avadhṛtam ātmānam bravīṣi puruṣottama vātsalī jaladhe tava aiśvaram tvad asādhāraṇam sarvasya praśāsitṛ tve pālayitṛ tve sraṣṭṛ tve saṃhartṛ tve bhartṛ tve kalyāṇa ākara tve paratara tve sakala visajātīya tve avasthitam rūpam draṣṭum sākṣātkartum icchāmi sarvasya sraṣṭṛ sarvasya praśāsitṛ sarvasya ādhāra tvad rūpam mayā draṣṭum śakyam yadi manyase tataḥ yogeśvara kalyāṇa paśya me aiśvaram vakṣyate tvad vyatiriktasya kasya asaṃbhāvitānām balāi śvarya vīrya tejasām nidhe ātmānam tvām avyayam me darśaya avyayam viśeṣaṇam tvām sakalam me darśaya paśya me āśrayāṇi rūpāṇi śataśaḥ sahasraśaḥ nānāvidhāni prakārāṇi divyāni aprākṛtāni varṇa ākṛtīni śukla kṛṣṇa varṇāni ākārāṇi paśya mama rūpe paśya ādityān vasūn aṣṭau rudrān ekādaśa aśvinau dvau maruta ḥ ekonapañcāśatam pradarśana idam jagati dṛṣṭāni dṛṣṭāni yāni vastūni anyāni sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu śāstreṣu pūrvāṇi bahūni āścaryāṇi paśya mama dehe ekastham deśa stham sacarācaram kṛtsnam paśya yad anyat draṣṭum icchasi deśa paśya aham mama deśe sarvam jagad darśayiṣyāmi niyata parimita vastu grāhiṇā prākṛtena cakṣuṣā mām tathābhūtam sakala visajātīyam aparimeyam draṣṭum śakṣyase tava divyam aprākṛtam mad darśana sādhanam dadāmi paśya me aiśvaram mad sādhāraṇam paśya mama ananta ananta vibhūti paśya uktvā sārathye avasthitaḥ pārtha mātula jaḥ mahā yoga īśvaraḥ hariḥ mahā āścarya yogānām īśvaraḥ bhūtaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ paramam aiśvaram svāsa ādhāraṇam rūpam pārthāya pitṛṣvasuḥ pṛthāyāḥ putrāya darśayām āsa vividha vicitra nikhila āśrayam viśvasya praśāsitṛ rūpam i īdṛśam vaktra nayanam adbhuta divya ābharaṇam divya udyata āyudham divya mālya dharam divya anulepanam āścarya mayam devam anantam viśvatomukham devam dyotamānam anantam kāla traya varti nikhila deśa kāla pariccheda anarham viśvatomukham viśva diḥ varti mukham ucita divya mālya ābharaṇa āyudha anvitam tejasaḥ aparimita darśana idam akṣaya tejassvarūpam anantāyām avistāre ananta bāhu udara vaktra netre aparimita tejaske aparimita divya āyudha upete ucita parimita divya bhūṣaṇe divya mālya dhare divya anulepane ananta āścarya maye devadevasya divye anekadhā pravibhaktam vividha vicitra tiryak sthāvara varga antarikṣa svarga pātāla tala vitala sutala bhaḥ prakṛti ātmakam kṛtsnam aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate hanta kathayiṣyāmi vibhūtīḥ śubhāḥ aham guḍākeśa āśaya sthitaḥ ādityānām aham viṣṇuḥ ityādinā vinā yad mayā carācaram viṣṭabhya aham idam kṛtsnam aṃśena sthitaḥ uditam ekastham deśa stham pāṇḍavaḥ bhagavat prasāda labdha darśana anuguṇa divya apaśyat tataḥ dhanañjayaḥ mahā āścaryasya kṛtsnasya jagataḥ deśena kṛtsnasya pravartayitāram āścaryatama ananta kalyāṇa gaṇam devam dṛṣṭvā vismaya āviṣṭaḥ hṛṣṭa romā śirasā daṇḍavat praṇamya kṛtāñjaliḥ abhāṣata tava dehe devān paśyāmi prāṇi viśeṣāṇām saṃghān brahmāṇam caturmukham aṇḍa adhipatim īśam kamalāsana stham kamala āsane brahmaṇi sthitam īśam mate avasthitam ṛṣi pramukhān ṛṣīn uraga vāsuki takṣaka ādīn dīptān bāhu udara vaktra netram ananta rūpam tvām sarvataḥ paśyāmi viśveśvara viśvasya niyantaḥ viśvarūpa viśva yataḥ anantaḥ ataḥ tava antam madhyam punar tava ādim paśyāmi rāśim sarvataḥ dīptimantam samantāt durnirīkṣam dīpta anala arka dyutim aprameyam tvām kirīṭinam gadinam cakriṇam paśyāmi upaniṣatsu dve vidye veditavye ityādiṣu veditavyatayā nirdiṣṭam paramam viśvasya nidhānam viśvasya parama ādhāra ḥ avyayaḥ vyaya rahitaḥ yad yad guṇaḥ yad vibhavaḥ tena rūpeṇa sarvadā ava tiṣṭhase śāśvata goptā śāśvatasya nityasya vaidikasya dharmasya ādibhiḥ avatāraiḥ goptā sanātanaḥ puruṣaḥ mataḥ me veda aham etam mahāntaṃ uditaḥ sanātana ḥ me mataḥ jñātaḥ yad ukula tilaka ḥ evaṃbhūta idānīm sākṣātkṛtaḥ mayā madhya antam madhya rahitam ananta vīryam anavadhika atiśaya vīryam vīrya pradarśana anavadhika atiśaya balāi śvarya vīrya tejasām nidhim ananta bāhum asaṃkhyeya bāhum pradarśana ananta bāhu udara vaktra ādikam śaśi sūrya netram śaśivat sūryavac prasāda pratāpa yukta netram ādīn anukūlān namaskāra kurvāṇān prasādaḥ viparītān asura rākṣasa ādīn pratāpaḥ rakṣāṃsi bhītāni diśaḥ dravanti namasyanti siddha saṃghāḥ vakṣyate dīpta hutāśa vaktram pradīpta kāla analavat saṃhāra anuguṇa vaktram tejasā viśvam idam tapantam abhibhavana sāmarthyam svakīyena tejasā viśvam idam tapantam tvām paśyāmi evambhūtam sarvasya sraṣṭāram sarvasya ādhāra sarvasya praśāsitāram sarvasya saṃhartāram parimita sāgaram madhya rahitam evaṃbhūta divya deham tvām upadeśam karomi divya dehe udara ādikam katham ittham ekasmāt kaṭi pradeśāt ananta parimāṇāt ūrdhvam udgatā udita udara adhaḥ udita divya pādāḥ mukhe netra dvayam ubhau uparitanānām adhastanānām lokānām pradarśana arthau dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ antaram avakāśaḥ yasmin avakāse lokāḥ tiṣṭhanti sarvaḥ ayam avakāśaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ tvayā ekena vyāptāḥ dṛṣṭvā adbhutam rūpam ugram tava idam anantāyām avistāram adbhutam ugram rūpam dṛṣṭvā lokatrayam pravyathitam yuddha didṛkṣayā āgateṣu asura pitṛ gaṇa siddha gandharva yakṣa rākṣaseṣu pratikūla anukūla madhya rūpam lokatrayam sarvam pravyathitam atyanta bhītam mahātman aparicchedya vṛtte eteṣām arjunasya iva viśva sākṣātkāra sādhanam divyam bhagavatā dattam kim arjunāya svāiśvaryam sarvam pradarśayitum ata idam ucyate dṛṣṭvā adbhutam rūpam ugram tava idam lokatrayam pravyarthitam mahātman amī sura saṃghāḥ utkṛṣṭā aḥ tvām viśva āśrayam avalokya hṛṣṭa manasaḥ tvan samīpam viśanti teṣu kecid ugram adbhutam tava ākāram ālokya bhītāḥ prāñjalayaḥ anuguṇam rūpāṇi vākyāni gṛṇanti uccārayanti apare mahā ṛṣi saṃghāḥ siddha saṃghāḥ parāvara tattva yāthātmya svasti uktvā puṣkalābhiḥ bhavat anurūpābhiḥ stutibhiḥ stuvanti ūṣmapāḥ pitaraḥ ūṣma bhāgā pitaraḥ vismayam āpannāḥ tvām vīkṣante bahvībhiḥ daṃṣṭrābhiḥ bhīṣaṇa ākāram lokāḥ uktāḥ pratikūla anukūla madhya sthāḥ trividhāḥ aham īdṛśam rūpam dṛṣṭvā atīva vyathitā bhavāmaḥ namaḥ akṣare parame vyoman varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt kṣayantam rajasaḥ parāke yaḥ adhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman ityādi siddhi triguṇa prakṛti atīta parama vācī vikārasya prakṛti tattvasya puruṣasya avasthasya kṛtsnasya nabhaḥ spṛśam dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ idam antaram vyāptam ukta dīptam varṇam vyātta ānanam dīpta viśāla netram tvām dṛṣṭvā pravyathita atyanta bhīta manāḥ dhṛtim vindāmi dehasya dhāraṇam labhe manasaḥ indriyāṇām śamam labhe viṣṇaḥ vyāpin vyāpinam atimātram adbhutam ghoram tvām dṛṣṭvā praśithika avayavaḥ vyākula indriyaḥ bhavāmi yuga kāla analavat saṃhāre pravṛttāni ghorāṇi tava mukhāni dṛṣṭvā diśaḥ jāne sukham labhe jagatām nivāsa deveśa ādīnām īśvarāṇām parama maheśvara mām prasannaḥ bhava aham prakṛtim gataḥ bhavāmi kurv vaktrāṇi tvaramāṇā viśanti daṃṣṭrā karālāni bhayānakāni kecid vilagnā daśana antareṣu saṃdṛśyante cūrṇitaiḥ uttamāṅgaiḥ amī dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāḥ duryodhana āt ayaḥ bhīṣmaḥ droṇaḥ sūtaputraḥ karṇaḥ pakṣīyaiḥ avanipāla samūhaiḥ sarvaiḥ asmadīyaiḥ kaiścid yodha mukhyaiḥ tvaramāṇā daṃṣṭrā karālāni bhayānakāni tava vaktrāṇi vināśāya viśanti kecid cūrṇitaiḥ uttamāṅgaiḥ daśāna antareṣu vilagnāḥ saṃdṛśyante pradīpta pataṅgā viśanti nāśāya samṛddha vegāḥ nāśāya viśanti lokāḥ tava vaktrāṇi samṛddha vegāḥ rāja lokāḥ bahavaḥ nadīnām pravāhāḥ samudram iva pradīpta iva śalabhāḥ tava vaktrāṇi abhivijvalanti svayam tvaramāṇā nāśāya viśanti rāja lokān samagrān jvaladbhiḥ vadanaiḥ grasamānaḥ kopa vegena rudhira avasiktam oṣṭha puṭa ādikam lelihyase punar punar lehanam karoṣi tava ghorā bhāsaḥ raśmayaḥ tejobhiḥ svakīyaiḥ prakāśaiḥ samagram āpūrya pratapanti darśaya ātmānam avyayam tava aiśvaryam niraṅkuśam kartum prārthitena bhavatā niraṅkuśam aiśvaryam darśayatā ghora rūpam idam ghora rūpaḥ kaḥ bhavān kim kartum pravṛtta bhavantam jñātum icchāmi tava abhipretām pravṛttim jānāmi etad ākhyāhi me namaḥ vara prasīda namaḥ īśvara kartum abhiprāyeṇa idam saṃhartṛ rūpam uktvā prasanna ḥ bhava kalayati gaṇayati kālaḥ dhārtarāṣṭra pramukhānām rāja lokānām āyuḥ avasānam gaṇayan aham kṣaya kṛt ghora rūpeṇa pravṛddhaḥ rāja lokān samāhartum ābhimukhyena saṃhartum pravṛttaḥ asmi ataḥ mad tvām ṛte tvad udyogāt rte dhārtarāṣṭra pramukhāḥ tava pratyanīkeṣu ye avasthitā yodhāḥ bhaviṣyanti vinaṅkṣyanti tasmāt tān yuddhāya uttiṣṭha tān śatrūn jitvā yaśaḥ labhasva dharmyam rājyam samṛddham bhuṅkṣva mayā aparādhāḥ nihatāḥ hanane viniyuktāḥ hanane bhava mayā hanyamānānām śatra sthānīyaḥ bhava savyasācin ṣaca samavāye savyena śara sacana śīlaḥ savyasācī savyena kareṇa śara karaḥ kara dvayena yoddhum samartha droṇa bhīṣma karṇa ādīn aparādha mayā hanane viniyuktān jahi hanyāḥ etān gurūn bandhūn anyān saktān katham haniṣyāmi mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ tān uddiśya adharma bhayena bandhu snehena kāruṇyena mā vyathām kṛthāḥ yataḥ aparādhā mayā hanane viniyuktāḥ ataḥ nirviśaṅkaḥ yudhyasva raṇe sapatnān jetāsi jeṣyasi eteṣām vadhe nṛśaṃsa gandhaḥ jaya labhyata etad aśrita vātsalya jaladheḥ keśavasya vacanam śrutvā arjuna ḥ namaskṛtya bhīta bhītaḥ tam praṇamya kṛtāñjaliḥ vepamānaḥ kirīṭī gadgadam sthāne yuktam yad etad yuddha didṛkṣayā āgatam aśeṣa gandharva siddha yakṣa vidyādhara kinnara kiṃpuruṣa ādikam tvad prasādāt tvām sarveśvaram avalokya tava prakīrtyā sarvam prahṛṣyati anurajyate yad tvām avalokya rakṣāṃsi bhītāni sarvā diśaḥ pradravanti siddha saṃghāḥ siddha anukūla saṃghāḥ namasyanti etad sarvam yuktam pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ ananta deveśa jagannivāsa kṣarati tattvam jāyate mriyate vipaścit siddhaḥ jīvātmā kṣarati sat asac sat sat nirdiṣṭam bhāvena avasthitam prakṛti tattvam vibhāgavat avastham sat nirdiṣṭam anarha avastham nirdiṣṭam yad tasmāt prakṛteḥ prakṛti saṃbandhinaḥ jīvātmanaḥ anyan tattvam yad jagati sarvaḥ veditā vedyam sarvam avasthita ḥ dhāma sthānam prāpya sthānam tvayā tatam viśvam ananta tvayā viśvam cit acit miśram tatam vyāptam namaḥ purastād pṛṣṭhataḥ namaḥ sarvata ananta vīrya amita vikramaḥ sarvam samāpnoṣi tataḥ asi sarvaḥ amita vīrya aparimita parākrama ḥ samāpnoṣi tataḥ sarvaḥ asi yataḥ sarvam cit acit vastu jātam samāpnoṣi ataḥ sarvasya cit acit vastu jātasya tvad tvad prakāra prakāra ḥ vācyaḥ asi sat vāyuḥ yamaḥ agniḥ ityādi sāmānādhikaraṇya nirdeśasya vyāptiḥ hetuḥ su vyaktam tvayā tatam viśvam ananta sarvam samāpnoṣi tataḥ asi sarvaḥ yaḥ apa hāsa asatkṛtaḥ asi śayyā āsana bhojaneṣu ekaḥ acyuta samakṣam kṣāmaye tvām aham aprameyam tava ananta vīrya amita vikrama antarātma sraṣṭṛ ādikaḥ yaḥ mahimā tam imam ajānatā mayā pramādān mohāt praṇayena cira paricayena sakhā mama vayasyaḥ matvā he kṛṣṇa he yādava he sakhā tvayi prasabham vinaya apetam yad yad prihāsa sarvadā satkāra ḥ asatkṛtaḥ asi śayyā āsana bhojaneṣu kṛteṣu ekānte vaḥ samakṣam yad asatkṛtaḥ asi sarvam tvām aprameyam aham kṣāmaye apratima prabhāva sarvasya carācarasya lokasya pitā asi lokasya guru ḥ asi ataḥ carācarasya lokasya garīyān pūjyatamaḥ tvad samaḥ abhyadhikaḥ kutaḥ lokatraye tvad kāruṇya kena guṇena tvad samaḥ kutaḥ abhyadhikaḥ yasmāt sarvasya pitā pūjyatamaḥ guru ḥ kāruṇya guṇaiḥ adhikaḥ asi tasmāt tvām īśam īḍyam praṇamya praṇidhāya kāyam prasādaye aparādhasya putrasya sakhyuḥ praṇāma prārthitaḥ pitā sakhā prasīdati parama kāruṇikaḥ priyāya me sarvam soḍhum arhasi adbhutam ugram tava rūpam dṛṣṭvā hṛṣitaḥ asmi prītaḥ asmi bhayena pravyathitam me ataḥ tava su prasannam rūpam me darśaya prasīda deveśa jagannivāsa mayi prasādam kuru devānām ādīnām īśa nikhila kirīṭinam gadinam cakra hastam tvām draṣṭum icchāmi ataḥ tena siddhena catur bhujena rūpeṇa yuktaḥ bhava sahasra bāhaḥ viśvamūrte idānīm sahasra bāhu viśva dṛśyamāna ḥ tena rūpeṇa yuktaḥ bhava yad me mayam tejasām rāśiḥ viśvam viśvātma anantam antarahitam pradarśana idam madhya rahitam ādyam mad vyatiriktasya kṛtsnasya tvad anyena kena rūpam idam prasannena mayā mad bhaktāya darśitam atmanaḥ saṃkalpa evaṃrūpaḥ yathāvat avathitaḥ aham mayi bhaktimataḥ tvad anyena ekānta bhakti rahitena kena puruṣeṇa veda ādibhiḥ kevalaiḥ draṣṭum śakyaḥ īdṛśa ghora darśanena yā vyathā yaḥ vimūḍha vartate bhayam mā bhūt tvayā abhyasta saumyam rūpam darśayāmi idam mama rūpam prapaśya pāṇḍu tanayam bhagavān vasudeva sūnuḥ uktvā svakīyam catur bhujam rūpam darśayām āsa aparicitarupa darśanena bhītam punar paricita saumya vapuḥ bhūtvā āśvāsayām āsa mahātmā saṅkalpaḥ īśvarasya parama puruṣasya brahmaṇaḥ upakṛti martyasya vasudeva sūnoḥ catur bhujam svakīyam rūpam kaṃsāt bhīta vasudeva prārthanena ākaṃsa vadhāt bhuja dvayam upasaṃhṛtam paścāt jātaḥ asi deveśa śaṅkha cakra gadā dhara divyam rūpam idam prasādena upsaṃhara anavadhika atiśaya saundarya saukumārya lāvaṇya yuktam tava asādhāraṇam saṃsthāna saṃsthitam saumyam idam tava rūpam dṛṣṭvā idānīm cetāḥ saṃvṛttaḥ asmi prakṛtim gata ḥ mama idam sarvasya praśāsane avasthitam asrayam rūpam yad dṛṣṭavān asi su duḥ darśam kena draṣṭum śakyam rūpasya devāḥ darśana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ dṛṣṭavantaḥ bhaktyā ananyayā śakya aham evaṃvidhaḥ arjuna jñātum draṣṭum tattvena praveṣṭum parantapa vedaiḥ adhyāpana pravacana japa viṣayaiḥ yāga dāna homa tapobhiḥ mad bhakti virahitaiḥ kevalaiḥ yathāvat avasthitaḥ aham draṣṭum aśakyaḥ ananyayā bhaktyā tattvata ḥ śāstraiḥ jñātum tattvataḥ kartum tattvataḥ praveṣṭum śakyaḥ śrutiḥ ayam pravacanena labhyaḥ medhayā bahunā śrutena yam eṣa vṛṇute tena labhya ḥ eṣa vivṛṇute tanūm svām veda adhyaya ādīni karmāṇi mad ārādhana rūpāṇi yaḥ karoti mad kṛt mad paramaḥ ārambhāṇām aham parama uddeśyaḥ yasya mad paramaḥ mad bhaktaḥ atyartha mad mad kīrtana dhyāna arcana praṇāma ādibhiḥ vinā dhāraṇam alabhamānaḥ mad yaḥ satatam karoti mad bhaktaḥ saṅga varjitaḥ mad ena saṅgam asahamānaḥ nirvairaḥ mad saṃśleṣa viyoga duḥkha svabhāva duḥkhasya aparādhana anusaṃdhānāt bhūtānām parama paratantra anusaṃdhānāt vaira teṣu nirvairaḥ ya bhūtaḥ mām mām yathāvat avasthitam prāpnoti nirasta aśeṣa gandhaḥ mad anubhavaḥ bhavati mad kṛt ityādinā uktena prakāreṇa satata yuktāḥ bhagavantam tvām prāpyam manvānāḥ ye bhaktāḥ tvām sakala vibhūti yuktam anavadhika atiśaya saundarya sauśīlya sārvajñi saṃkalpa ananta sāgaram paripūrṇam upāsate ye pratyak svarūpam karaṇa svarūpam upāsate ubhayeṣām ke yoga vittamāḥ ke sādhyam śīghra gāmina bhavāmi cirāt pārtha yoga vittama śaighrya viṣayam vyañjayiṣyate atyartha mad mayi āveśya śraddhayā parayā upetāḥ yuktāḥ kāṅkṣamāṇāḥ ye mām upāsate prāpya viṣayam mayi āveśya ye mām upāsata yuktatamāḥ mām sukhena acirāt prāpnuvanti sanniyamya indriya grāmam sama buddhayaḥ prāpnuvanti mām hite ratāḥ kleśaḥ adhikatara ḥ avyakta āsakta cetasām avyaktā gatiḥ duḥkham dehavadbhiḥ avāpyate ye pratyak svarūpam anirdeśyam dehāt anyatayā nirdeśyam tataḥ karaṇān abhivyaktam sarvatragam acintyam deheṣu vartamānam visajātīya tena tena rūpeṇa cintayitum anarham tataḥ kūṭastham sādhāraṇam asa ādhāraṇa ākāra saṃbaddham apariṇāmi svāsa ādhāraṇa ākārān calati cyavata acalam tataḥ dhruvam sat niyāmya indriya grāmam ādikam indriya grāmam sarvam vyāpārebhya ḥ samyak niyamya sama buddhayaḥ viṣama ākāreṣu iṣu avasthita iṣu ātmasu ākāra sama buddhayaḥ tataḥ hite ratāḥ ahita rahita nivṛttāḥ ahita rahita viṣama ākāra abhimāna nimittam ya upāsate mām prāpnuvanti mad ākāram asaṃsāriṇam ātmānam prāpnuvanti mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ vakṣyate śrūyate nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti nirdiṣṭāt kūṭasthād brahmaṇaḥ vakṣyate kūṭa sthaḥ ucyate uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ parā yayā adhikgamyate nirdiṣṭam ādeḥ avyakta āsakta cetasām kleśa ḥ adhikataraḥ avyaktā gatiḥ avyakta viṣayā dehavadbhiḥ abhimāna yuktaiḥ duḥkhena avāpyate dehavantaḥ deham ātmānam manyante aham samuddhartā sāgarāt bhavāmi cirāt pārtha mayi āveśita cetasām ye laukikāni yātrā aśeṣa bhūtāni arthāni ādīni karmāṇi vaidikāni yaga dāna homa tapaḥ prabhṛtīni kāraṇāni uddeśyāni cetasā mayi saṃnyasya mad parāḥ mad prāpyāḥ ananyena yogena prayojanena yogena mām dhyāyanta upāsate dhyāna arcana praṇāma kīrtana ādīni svayam priyāṇi prāpya samāni kurvantaḥ mām upāsata mad prāpti virodhitayā bhūtāt ākhyāt sāgarāt aham acireṇa kālena samuddhartā bhavāmi ataḥ atiśayita sulabha aciralabhya mayi sahasā mayi sthiram cittam samādhātum śaknoṣi tataḥ abhyāsa yogena mām āptum iccha svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya saundarya sauśīlya sauhārda vātsalī ka aruṇya mādhurya gāmbhīryāu dārya śairya vīrya karmāṇi ālaya nirmāṇa udyona karaṇa pradī pāra paṇa mārjana abhyukṣaṇa upalepana puṣpa āharaṇa pūjā pravartana saṃkīrtana pradakṣi atyartha ācara atyartha mad karmāṇi kurvan acirāt abhyāsa yoga pūrvikām mayi sthirām citta labdhvā mad prāpti rūpām siddhim avāpsyasi mad āśritya etad kartum śaknoṣi mad anusandhāna mad ākāram bhakti āśritya bhakti yoga aṅkura rūpam etad mad karmā kartum śaknoṣi tataḥ svabhāva anusandhāna rūpam bhakti jananam ṣaṭka uditam āśritya upāya tyāgam kuru mad mad prāpyatā buddhiḥ prakṣīṇa aśeṣa pāpasya iva jāyate yata ātmavān yatamanaskaḥ tataḥ anabhisaṃhita phalena mad ārādhana rūpeṇa anuṣṭhitena karmaṇā siddhena dhyānena nivṛtta avidyā tirodhāne mad svarūpe pratyagātmani sākṣātkṛte mayi parā bhaktiḥ svayam utpadyate vakṣyate karmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mānavaḥ ārabhya vimucya nirmamaḥ śāntaḥ bhūyāya kalapate bhūtaḥ prasanna śocati kāṅkṣati samaḥ sarveṣu mad bhaktim labhate parām atyartha prīti virahitāt karkaśa rūpāt yāthātmya anusandhāna pūrvakam aparokṣya jñānam hita viśiṣyate aparokṣya jñānāt aniṣpanna rūpāt upāya dhyānam hita tve viśiṣyate aniṣpanna rūpāt upāya tyāgena anuṣṭhitam viśiṣyate anabhisaṃhita phalāt anuṣṭhitāt karmaṇaḥ anantaram nirasta pāpa manasaḥ śāntiḥ bhaviṣyati śānte dhyānam saṃpatsyate dhyāna āt aparokṣyam aparokṣyāt parā bhaktiḥ bhakti yoga abhyāsa aśaktasya niṣṭhā śreyasī aśānta manasaḥ niṣṭhā prāptaye antargata anabhi saṃhita niṣṭhā śreyasi santuṣṭaḥ satatam yogī yata dṛḍha niścayaḥ mayi arpita buddhiḥ yaḥ mad bhaktaḥ me priyaḥ adveṣṭā bhūtānām vidviṣatām apakurvatām bhūtānām adveṣṭā mad aparādha anuguṇam īśvara preritāni etāni bhūtāni dviṣanti apakurvanti anusandadhānaḥ teṣu dviṣatsu apkurvatsu maitrīm matim kurvan maitraḥ teṣu duḥkhiteṣu karuṇām kurvan karuṇaḥ nirmamaḥ indriyeṣu saṃbandhiṣu nirmamaḥ nirahaṅkāraḥ abhimāna rahitaḥ tataḥ sama duḥkha sukhaḥ duḥkha āgamayoḥ aṅkalpikayoḥ harṣa udvega rahitaḥ kṣamī sparśa prabhavayoḥ avarjanīyayoḥ tayoḥ rahitaḥ saṃtuṣṭaḥ yadṛcchā upanatena yena kena dravyeṇa saṃtuṣṭaḥ satatam yogī satatam prakṛti viyukta sandhāna yata niyamita dṛḍha niścayaḥ udita iṣu artheṣu dṛḍha niścayaḥ mayi arpita buddhiḥ bhagavān vāset iva anabhisaṃhita phalena anuṣṭhitena karmaṇā ārādhyate ārādhita ḥ mama parokṣyam sādhayiṣyati mayi arpita buddhiḥ ya evaṃbhūtaḥ mad bhaktaḥ yogena mām bhajamānaḥ yaḥ me priyaḥ yasmāt niṣṭhāt puruṣān tāl lokaḥ udvijate yaḥ udvega karam kiñcid karoti lokāt bhūtāt yaḥ udvijate yam uddiśya lokaḥ udvega karam karoti avirodhi niścayāt ata kañcana harṣeṇa kañcana amarṣeṇa kañcana bhayena kañcana udvegena h evaṃbhūtaḥ yaḥ mama priyaḥ anapekṣaḥ vyatirikte kṛtsne vastuni anapekṣaḥ śuciḥ dravya vardhita kāyaḥ dakṣaḥ śāstrīya upādāna samarthaḥ udāsīnaḥ gana vyathaḥ śāstrīya nirvṛttau avarjanīya śīta uṣṇa sparśa duḥkheṣu vyathā rahitaḥ ārambha parityāgī śāstrīya vyatirikta ārambha parityāgī ya evaṃbhūtaḥ mad bhaktaḥ me priyaḥ yaḥ hṛṣyati yad manuṣyāṇām harṣa nimittam jātam prāpya yaḥ yogī hṛṣyati yad priyam prāpya dveṣṭi yad manuṣyāṇām śoka nimittam bhāryā vitta kṣaya ādikam prāpya śocati tathāvidham aprāptam kāṅkṣati śubha aśubha parityāgī pāpavat puṇyasya parityāgī ya evaṃbhūtaḥ bhaktimān me priyaḥ tulya nindā stutiḥ maunī saṃtuṣṭaḥ yena kenacid aniketaḥ sthira matiḥ bhaktimān me priyaḥ naraḥ adveṣṭā bhūtānām ityādinā śatru mitra dveṣa rahita atra teṣu sannihita iṣu sama citta tataḥ atiriktaḥ ucyate sthiram niketa asakta aniketaḥ tataḥ māna avamāna samaḥ ya evaṃbhūtaḥ bhaktimān me priyaḥ dharmyam mṛtam dharmya amṛtam ye prāpya samam prāpakam bhakti mayi āveśya ye mām uktena prakāreṇa upāsate bhaktāḥ atitarām mama priyāḥ idam devaḥ aham manuṣyaḥ aham sthūlaḥ aham kṛśaḥ aham bhoktrā sāmānādhikaraṇyena pratīyamānam bhoktuḥ kṣetram yāthātmya vidbhiḥ abhidhīyate etad avayavaśaḥ saṃghāta rūpeṇa idam aham vedmi yaḥ vetti tam vedya bhūtāt asmāt veditṛ ena kṣetrajña yāthātmya prāhuḥ yadi vyatirikta ghaṭa anusandhāna velāyām aham manuṣyaḥ aham ghaṭa ādikam jānāmi sāmāna adhikaraṇyena jñātāram ātmānam anusandhatte anubhava velāyām deham ghaṭa ādikam iva idam aham vedmi vedya veditā anubhavati vedituḥ vedya ghaṭa ādivat ghaṭa ādeḥ iva vedya bhūtāc charīrāt veditā kṣetrajñaḥ bhūtaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyena pratīti ḥ vastutaḥ śarīrasya gaḥ ādivat atma svabhāva upapannā vedituḥ asādhāraṇa ākārasya karaṇā viṣaya yoga saṃskṛta viṣaya prakṛti sannidhānāt mūḍhāḥ prakṛti ākāram veditāram paśyanti vakṣyati utkrāmantam sthitam bhuñjānam anvitam vimūḍhā anupaśyanti paśyanti jñānacakṣuṣaḥ kṣetreṣu veditṛ tuākāram kṣetrajñam mām viddhi mad ātmakam viddhi kṣetrajñam kṣetram mām viddhi gamyate kṣetram kṣetrajña svabhāva māna adhi karaṇyena nirdeśyam kṣetram kṣetrajñam mad svabhāva mada mad āmāna adhikaraṇyena nirdeśyau viddhi saṃghāta rūpasya kṣetrasya kṣetrajñasya bhagavat bhagavat śrutayaḥ vadanti yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhan pṛthivyāḥ antaraḥ yam veda yasya yaḥ pṛthivīm antaraḥ yamayati ta amṛtaḥ ārabhya ya tiṣṭhan antaraḥ yam veda yasya ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati ta amṛtaḥ ādyāḥ idam kṣetrajñānām ena avasthānam bhagavataḥ māna adhi karaṇyena hetuḥ aham guḍākeśa āśaya sthitaḥ vinā yad mayā carācaram viṣṭabhya aham idam kṛtsnam aṃśena sthitaḥ purastād upariṣṭāt abhidhāya madhye sāmānādhikaraṇyena vyapadiśati ādityānām aham viṣṇuḥ ityādinā yad idam kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ viveka viṣayam tayoḥ mad viṣayam jñānam upādeyam jñānam mama matam kecid āhuḥ kṣetrajñam mām viddhi sāmāna adhikaraṇyena avagamyate tataḥ īśvarasya ajñānāt kṣetrajña iva bhavati abhyupagantavyam nivṛtti ayam āptatama bhagavat upadeśena rajjuḥ eṣā sarpaḥ āpta upadeśena sarpa bhrama nivṛttivat kṣetrajña bhramaḥ nivartate praṣṭavyāḥ ayam upadeṣṭā bhagavān vāsudevaḥ parameśvaraḥ kim yāthātmya sākṣātkāreṇa nivṛtta ajñānaḥ uta nivṛtta ajñānaḥ nirviśeṣa cit svarūpe ru adhyāsa saṃbhāvanayā kaunteya tān praty vyāpārāḥ saṃbhavanti sākṣātkāra anivṛtta ajñānaḥ tarhi ajña saṃbhavaḥ upadekṣyanti jñānam jñāninaḥ tattva darśinaḥ ata ādivādā anākalita itihāsa purāṇa nyāya virodhaiḥ ajñānibhiḥ mohanāya pravartitā anādaraṇīyāḥ atra idam tattvam acit vastunaḥ cit vastunaḥ brahmaṇaḥ bhogya ceśitṛ vivekam āhuḥ kāścana śrutayaḥ asmān māyī sṛjate viśvam etad tasmin māyayā sanniruddhaḥ māyām prakṛtim vidyān māyinam maheśvaraṃ kṣaram pradhānam haraḥ kṣara īśate ekaḥ haraḥ bhoktā nirdiśyate pradhānam bhogya harati haraḥ kāraṇam karaṇa adhipa adhipaḥ kaściñ janitā adhipaḥ kṣetrajña patiḥ īśaḥ patim viśvasya īśvaram śāśvatam śivam acyutam jñā ājñau dvau ajau īśa ni īśau nityaḥ nityānām cetanaḥ cetanānām ekaḥ bahūnām yaḥ vidadhāti kāmān bhoktā bhogyam preritāram matvā ātmānam preritāram matvā juṣṭaḥ tataḥ tena eti tayoḥ pippalam svāt v atty anaśnan abhicākaśīti ajām ekām lohita śukla kṛṣṇām bahvīm prajām janayantīm sarūpām ajaḥ ekaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ anuśete jahāti enām bhukta bhogām ajaḥ ityādyāḥ atra ahaṅkāra iyam me bhinnā aṣṭadhā aparā iyam itaḥ anyām prakṛtim viddhi me parām bhūtāṃ bhūtāni kauntteya prakṛtim yānti māmikām kalpa kṣaye punar kalpa ādau visṛjāmi aham kṣetram yad yad dravyam yādṛḥ yeṣām yad vikāri ye vikārāḥ yataḥ yataḥ hetoḥ idam utpannam yasmai aya utpannam yad yad svarūpam idam yaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ yaḥ yad yad prabhāvaḥ ye prabhāvāḥ sarvam samāsena saṃkṣepeṇa mattaḥ śṛṇu idam kṣetra kṣetrajñayāthātmyam ṛṣibhiḥ parāśara ādibhiḥ bahudhā bahu prakāram gītam aham bhūtaiḥ uhyāma pārthiva pravāha patitaḥ vargaḥ yāti ayam icchā dveṣaḥ sukham duḥkham saṃghāta ḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ etad kṣetram samāsena vikāram udāhṛtam mahābhūtāni ahaṃkāraḥ buddhiḥ kṣetra ārambhaka dravyāṇi ap vāyu ākāśāḥ mahābhūtāni ahaṃkāraḥ bhūtādiḥ buddhiḥ mahān daśa ekam indriya gocarā kṣetra āśritāni tattvāni śrotra tvac jihvā ghrāṇāni pāṇi pāyu upasthāni karmendriyāṇi daśa ekam indriya gocarāḥ sparśa rasa gandhāḥ icchā dveṣaḥ sukham duḥkham kṣetra kāryāṇi kṣetra vikārā ucyante yadi icchā dveṣa duḥkhāni bhūtāni kṣetra prayuktāni kṣetra kṣetra vikārā ucyante puruṣaḥ duḥkhānām tve hetuḥ ucyate vakṣyate saṃghāta ḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ ādhṛtiḥ ādhāraḥ duḥkhe bhuñjānasya apavargau sādhayataḥ cetanasi ādhāra utpannaḥ saṃghātaḥ prakṛti dravya ārabdham indriya icchā dveṣa duḥkha vikāri saṃghāta rūpam cetana duḥkha upabhoga ādhāra prayojanam kṣetram bhavati etad kṣetram samāsena saṃkṣepeṇa ki vāram udāhṛtam amāni utkṛṣṭa janeṣu avadhīraṇā rahita adambhi dhārmika yaśaḥ anuṣṭhānam dambhaḥ rahita ahiṃsā kāyaiḥ pīḍā rahita kṣāntiḥ paraiḥ pīḍyamānasya tān avikṛta citta ārjavam parān kāya prabhṛtīnām ācārya upāsanam pradāyini ācārye praṇipāta paripraśna sevā nirata śaucam sādhana yogya kāya gatā siddhā stairyam udite arthe niścala vinigrahaḥ vyatirikta viṣayebhyaḥ manasaḥ nivartanam indriya artheṣu vairāgyam vyatirikteṣu viṣayeṣu sadoṣa anusaṃdhānena udvejanam anahaṃkāraḥ anātmani dehe abhimāna rahita pradarśana idam anātmīya iṣu ātmīya abhimāna rahita vivakṣitam jarā vyādhi duḥkha tve jarā vyādhi duḥkha rūpasya doṣasya auvarjanīya anusaṃdhānam asaktiḥ vyatirikta parigraheṣu saṅga rahita anabhiṣvaṅgaḥ dāra gṛha teṣu śāstrī ya upakaraṇa atirekeṇa śleṣa rahita saṃkalpa prabhaveṣu niṣṭa nipāteṣu harṣa udvega rahita mayi īśvare aikāntya yogena sthirā bhaktiḥ jana varjita deśa vāsi jana saṃsadi prītiḥ jñānam jñānam niṣṭha tattva cintanam tattva prayojanam yad cintanam nirata jñāyate jñānam sādhanam kṣetra saṃbandhinaḥ puruṣasya āmāni ādikam bṛnham upayogi etad vyatiriktam sarvam kṣetra virodhi ajñānam amāni ādibhiḥ sādhanaiḥ jñeyam prāpyam yad pratyak svarūpam pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvā jarā maraṇa prākṛta rahitam amṛtam ātmānam prāpnoti yasya vidyate pratyak ātmana utpattiḥ vidyate tataḥ antaḥ vidyate śrutiḥ jāyate mriyate vipaścit mad aham yasya mad itaḥ anyām prakṛtim viddhi me parām bhūtām bhagavat bhagavat rasam svarūpam śrutiḥ ya tiṣṭhan antaraḥ yam atmā veda yasya ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati kāraṇam karaṇa adhipa adhipaḥ kaściñ janitā adhipaḥ kṣetrajña patiḥ īśaḥ ādikā bṛhat yogi ādeḥ svataḥ ādibhiḥ pariccheda rahitam kṣetrajña tattvam ānantyāya kalpate śrūyate paricchinna aṇu kṛtam bandhān muktasya ānantyam prayujyate guṇān samatītya etān bhūyāya kalpate brahmaṇaḥ pratiṣṭhā aham amṛtasya avyayasya bhūtaḥ prasanna śocati kāṅkṣati samaḥ sarveṣu mad bhaktim labhate parām sarvataḥ pāṇi pādam pariśuddha svarūpam sarvataḥ pāṇi śaktam sarvataḥ akṣi mukham sarvataḥ śrutimat sarvataḥ kṛtpāṇi pādaḥ javanaḥ grahītā paśyati acakṣuḥ śṛṇoti akarṇaḥ brahmaṇaḥ apāṇi pādasya sarvataḥ pāṇi kṛt śrūyate pratyak pariśuddhasya āpattyā sarvataḥ pāṇi kṛt siddham vidvān puṇya pāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti śrūyate idam jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ vakṣyate sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati yad vastu jātam sarvam vyāpya tiṣṭhati pariśuddha svarūpam deśa pariccheda rahita gatam indriya ābhāsam indriya guṇaiḥ yasya indriya ābhāsam indriya guṇā indriya vṛttayaḥ indriya vṛttibhiḥ viṣayān jñatum samartham svabhāvataḥ indriya vivarjitam vinā indriya vṛttibhiḥ svata sarvam jānāti asaktam svabhāvataḥ saṅga rahitam bhṛt iva bharaṇa samartham ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati ityādi nirguṇam svabhāvataḥ sattva rahitam sattva ādīnām guṇānām samartham ādīni bhūtāni parityajya śarīraḥ bahiḥ vartate vartate jakṣat krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ strībhiḥ yānaiḥ ityādi siddha svacchanda vṛttiṣu acaram caram svabhāvataḥ acaram caram dehi tve sūkṣma vijñeyam yuktam sarvajñām atma tattvam kṣetre vartamānam sūkṣma dehāt pṛthaktvena saṃsāribhiḥ avijñeyam dūra stham antike amāni ukta rahitānām viparīta guṇāṇām puṃsām dehe vartamānam dūra stham amāni upetānām antike vartate sthitam vastu veditṛ ākāra avibhaktam aviduṣām ākāreṇa ayam devaḥ manuṣyaḥ vibhaktam iva sthitam devaḥ aham manuṣyaḥ aham sāmāna adhikaraṇī ena anusandhīyamānam veditṛ dehāt jñātum śakyam ādau etad yaḥ vetti idānīm prakāra antaraiḥ jñātum śakyam āja bhartṛ bhūtānām ādīnām rūpeṇa saṃhatānām yad bhartṛ bhartavyebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ antaram jñeyam antaram jñātum śakyam grasiṣṇu anna ādīnām bhautikānām grasiṣṇu grasyamānebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ grasitṛ ena antra jñātum śakyam prabhaviṣṇu prabhava hetuḥ grastānām anna ādīnām ākāra pariṇatānām prabha hetuḥ tebhyaḥ antaram jñātum śakyam mṛta grasana prabhava ādīnām adarśanān saṃghāta rūpam kṣetram grasana prabhava bharaṇa hetuḥ niścīyate jyotiśām dīpa maṇi prabhṛtīnām prakāśakam dīpāt ādīnām prabhā rūpam jñānam prakāśakam dīpa viṣaya indriya sannikarṣa virodhi saṃtama nirasana kurvate tāvan mātreṇa prakāśaka tamasaḥ ucyate tamaḥ sūkṣma avastha prakṛti vacanaḥ prakṛteḥ ucyata ataḥ jñānam jñeyam ākāram jñeyam gamyam amāni ādibhiḥ sādhanaiḥ uktaiḥ prāpyam sarvasya viṣṭhitam sarvasya ādeḥ avasthitam sannihitam mahābhūtāni ahaṅkāraḥ ityādinā saṃghāta ḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ kṣetra tattvam samāsena amāni ityādinā tattva cintanam jñātavyasya tattvasya sādhanam ana mad ityādinā sarvasya viṣṭhitam jñeyasya kṣetrajñasya yāthātmyam saṃkṣepeṇa mad bhaktaḥ etad kṣetrayāthātmyam kṣetrād vivikta prāpti upāya yāthātmyam kṣetrajña yāthātmyam vijñāya mad aya mama yaḥ svabhāvaḥ asaṃsāri asaṃsāri prāptaye bhavati prakṛti puruṣau ubhau anyonya saṃsṛṣṭau anādī viddhi bhūtān vikārān icchā dveṣa ādīn amāni ādikāṃḥ guṇām bhūtān prakṛti saṃbhavān viddhi puruṣeṇa saṃsṛṣṭā iyam kāla pravṛttā kṣetra ākāra pariṇātā vikāraiḥ icchā dveṣa ādibhiḥ puruṣasya bandhu hetuḥ bhavati āmā ni ādibhiḥ vikāraiḥ puruṣasya apavarga hetuḥ bhavati kāraṇāni ātmakāni manaskāni kāri tve adhiṣṭhitā hetuḥ adhiṣṭhita kṣetra ākāra pariṇata prakṛti āśrayāḥ sādhana bhūtāḥ puruṣasya adhiṣṭhātṛ at ādikam puruṣasya prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ duḥkhānām tve hetuḥ duḥkha anubhava prakṛti pariṇāma viśeṣeṣu sthitaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ prayukta sattva mayeṣu duḥkha saktaḥ sādhana puṇya pāpa karmasu pravartate tataḥ puṇya pāpa anubhavāya sat sat yoniṣu sādhu asādhuṣu yoniṣu jāyate tataḥ ārabhate tataḥ jāyate yāvat amāni ādikān prāpti sādhana bhūtān guṇān sevate tāvat saṃsarati idam kāraṇam saṅgaḥ sat sat janmasu dehe avasthitaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ pravṛtti anuguṇa saṅkalpa rūpeṇa dehasya upadraṣṭā anumantā bhavati dehasya bhartā bhavati pravṛtti janita duḥkhayoḥ bhoktā bhavati niyamanena bharaṇena śeṣi indriya manāṃsi maheśvaraḥ bhavati vakṣyate yad avāpnoti yad utkrāmati īśvaraḥ gṛhītvā etāni saṃyāti vāyuḥ gandhān iva āśayāt ukta svabhāvam ukta svabhāvām prakṛtim vakṣyamāṇa svabhāva yuktaiḥ sattva ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ yaḥ vetti yathāvat vivekena jānāti iṣu atimātra kliṣṭa prakāreṇa vartamānaḥ abhijāyate prakṛtyā saṃsargam arhati aparicchinna anala kaṣaṇam apahata pāpmānam ātmānam avasāna samaye prāpnoti kecid niṣpanna yogāḥ avasthitam ātmānam manasā dhyānena yogena paśyanti aniṣpanna yogāḥ sāṃkhyena yogena yogena yoga yogyam kṛtvā ātmānam paśyanti apare yogān adhikāriṇaḥ adhikāriṇaḥ sukara upāya saktāḥ vyapadeśya āḥ yogena antargata jñānena manasaḥ yoga yogya tām āpādya ātmānam paśyanti yoga avalokana sādhaneṣu anadhikṛtāḥ anyebhyaḥ tattva darśibhyaḥ jñānibhyaḥ śrutvā yoga ādibhiḥ ātmānam upāsate darśanena mṛtyum atitaranti ye parāyaṇāḥ niṣṭhāḥ niṣṭhāḥ pūta pāpāḥ yoga ādikam ārabhya atitaranti mṛtyum āt bhedaḥ avagamyate yāvat sthāvara jaṅgama sattvam jāyate tāvat kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ saṃyoga at jāyate saṃyuktam jāyate viyuktam yukteṣu sarveṣu viṣama ākārāt viyuktam indriya manāṃsi parameśvara sthitam ātmānam jñātṛ ākāram teṣu vinaśyatsu vināśānarha svabhāvena avinaśyantam yaḥ paśyati paśyati ātmānam yathāvat avasthitam paśyati yaḥ viṣama ākāreṇa ātmānam viṣama ākāram vināśa yuktam paśyati saṃsarati abhiprāyaḥ śarīreṣu śeṣi ādhāra viyantṛ sthitam īśvaram ātmānam viṣama ākāra viyuktam ākāra samam paśyan manasā svam ātmānam hinasti rakṣati saṃsārān mocayati tataḥ tasmāt jñātṛ ākāra parām gatim yāti gamyata gatiḥ gantavyam yathāvat avasthitam ātmānam prāpnoti ākāra yukta viṣamam ātmānam paśyan ātmānam hinasti bhava jaladhi madhye prakṣipati karmāṇi tve hetuḥ ucyate ukta rītyā prakṛtyā kriyamāṇā ani yaḥ paśyati ātmānam ākāram akartāram yaḥ paśyati prakṛti saṃyoga ḥ janya duḥkha anubhavaḥ ajñāna kṛtāni yaḥ paśyati ātmānam yathāvat avasthitam paśyati prakṛti tattva dvaya ātmakeṣu sarveṣu satsu ekastham tattva stham prakṛti stham yadā paśyati stham tataḥ prakṛtita pautra vistāram yadā paśyati anavacchinnam ākāram ātmānam prāpnoti ayam paramātmā dehān niṣkṛṣya svabhāvena nirūpitaḥ sthaḥ anārabhya avyayaḥ vyaya rahitaḥ nirguṇa sattva rahita tvān karoti lipyate svabhāvaiḥ lipyate ākāśam gatam sarvaiḥ vastubhiḥ saṃyuktam saukṣmyāt vastu svabhāvaiḥ lipyate saukṣmyāt ādau dehe avasthitaḥ svabhāvaiḥ lipyate ādityaḥ svayā prabhayā kṛtsnam imam lokam prakāśayati kṣetram kṣetrī mama idam kṣetram īdṛśam kṛtsnam bahi ḥ āpāda tala mastakam svakīyena jñānena prakāśayati ataḥ prakāśi al lokāt prakāśaka āt avat veditṛ vedya bhūtāt asmāt kṣetrād atyanta vilakṣaṇaḥ ayam ukta uktena prakāreṇa kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ antaram viveka viṣaya ākhyena cakṣuṣā ye viduḥ prakṛti mokṣam yānti nirmukta bandham ātmānam prāpnuvanti mokṣyate mokṣaḥ amāni ādikam sādhanam kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ viveka viṣayeṇa uktena jñānena tayoḥ vivekam viditvā ākāra pariṇata prakṛti upāyam amāni ādikam āgamya ya ācaranti nirmukta bandhāḥ rūpeṇa avasthitam anavacchinna lakṣaṇam ātmānam prāpnuvanti uktāt anyat prakṛti antargatam sattva viṣayam jñānam pravakṣyāmi jñānam prakṛti viṣaya jñānānām uttamam yaj jñānam jñātvā munayaḥ manana śīlāḥ itaḥ bandhāt parām siddhim gatāḥ parām pariśuddha prāpti rūpām siddhim avāptāḥ idam vakṣyamāṇam jñānam upaśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ mad sāmyam prāptāḥ sarge upajāyante sṛji karmatām bhajante pralaye vyathanti saṃhṛti karmatām kṛtsnasya jagataḥ mama yad tasmin garbham dadhāmi aham bhūmiḥ analaḥ vāyuḥ kham buddhiḥ ahaṅkāra iyam me bhinnā aṣṭadhā sarvāsu gandharva yakṣa rākṣasa paśu mṛga pakṣi sarīsṛpa yoniṣu mūrtayaḥ yāḥ saṃbhavanti jāyante tāsām kāraṇam mayā saṃyojita cetana vargā ava sthā kāraṇam aham bīja pradaḥ pitā anuguṇyena cetana vargasya saṃyojakaḥ aham sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi trayaḥ guṇāḥ prakṛteḥ anubandhinaḥ svabhāva viśeṣāḥ nirūpaṇīyāḥ prakṛti avasthāyām anudbhūtāḥ vikāreṣu udbhūtāḥ antaiḥ ārabdha saṃbandhinam dehinam avyayam svataḥ saṃbandhān arham dehe vartamānam nibadhnanti dehe vartamāna upādhinā nibadhnanti sattva rajaḥ tamaḥ sattvasya svarūpam īdṛśam nirmala prakāśakam āvaraṇa svabhāva rahita nirmala janana ekānta svabhāva vastu yātha ātmya avabodhaḥ anāmayam āmaya ākhyam vidyata anāmayam aroga hetuḥ eṣa sattva ākhyaḥ dehinam saṅgena saṅgena badhnāti puruṣasya saṅgam saṅgam janayati sukhayoḥ saṅge jāte sādhaneṣu laukika vaidikeṣu pravartate tataḥ anubhava sādhana bhūtāsu yoniṣu jāyata sattvam saṅga dvāreṇa badhnāti jananam punar tayoḥ saṅga jananam sattvam bhavati rajaḥ rāga ātmakam rāga rāgaḥ yoṣit puruṣayoḥ spṛhā āsaṅga samudbhavam tṛṣṇā saṅgayoḥ udbhava sthānam tṛṣṇā saṅga tṛṣṇā viṣaya spṛhā saṅgaḥ mitra saṃbandhiṣu saṃśleṣa spṛhā rajaḥ dehinam karmasu kriyāsu spṛhā janana dvāreṇa nibadhnāti kriyāsu spṛhayā yāḥ ārabhate dehī puṇya pāpa rūpā anubhava sādhana bhūtāsu yoniṣu hetavaḥ bhavanti ataḥ saṅga dvāreṇa rajaḥ dehinam nibadhnāti rajaḥ rāga tṛṣṇā saṅga hetuḥ saṅga hetuḥ bhavati jñānāt anyat ajñānam abhipretam jñānam vastu yathātmya avabodhaḥ tasmāt anyat viparyaya jñānam tamaḥ vastu yāthātmya via parīta bhavanti sattva mayā aḥ āhārā āyuḥ vivardhanāḥ punar sattvasya vivardhanāḥ sattvam antaḥkaraṇam antaḥkaraṇa jñānam sattva śabdena ucyate sattva at saṃjāyate jñānam sattvasya vivṛddhi hetutvāt āhāraḥ
