yuktāḥ sthirāḥ sthira pariṇāmāḥ hṛdyāḥ ramaṇīya veṣāḥ evaṃvidhāḥ sattva mayā āhārāḥ sāttvikasya puruṣasya priyāḥ kaṭu rasāḥ amla rasāḥ lavaṇotkaṭāḥ uṣṇāḥ ti īkṣaṇāḥ rūkṣāḥ vidāhinaḥ kaṭu amla lavaṇa uṣṇa tīkṣṇa rūkṣa vidāhinaḥ atiśaitya taikṣṇya durupayoga aḥ tīkṣṇāḥ śoṣa karā rūkṣāḥ tāpa karā vidāhinaḥ evaṃvidhā āhārā rāja sasya iṣṭāḥ rajaḥ maya duḥkha śoka āmaya vardhanāḥ rajaḥ vardhanāḥ yātayāmam cira kāla avasthitam gata rasam tyakta svābhāvika rasam pūti durgandha upetam paryuṣitam kāla atipattyā rasa āpannam ucchiṣṭam guru anyeṣām bhukta śiṣṭam amedhyam ayajña arham ayajña śiṣṭam evaṃvidham tamaḥ mayam bhojanam tāmasa priyam bhavati bhujyata āhāra bhojanam punar tamasaḥ vardhanam ataḥ hita eṣibhiḥ sattva vivṛddhaye sāttvika āhāra sevyaḥ ākāṅkṣā rahitaiḥ puruṣaiḥ dravya ādibhiḥ yuktaḥ yaṣṭavyam bhagavat ārādhana svayaṃprayojana yaṣṭavyam samādhāya yaḥ ijyate sāttvikaḥ abhisandhi yuktaiḥ dambha garbhaḥ yaśaḥ phalaḥ yaḥ ijyate tam yajñam rājasam viddhi hīnam brāhmaṇa ukti hīnam sat yuktaiḥ vidvadbhiḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ yajasva ukti hīnam asṛṣṭa annam acodita dravyam hīnam adakṣiṇam śraddhā virahitam yajñam tāmasam paricakṣate dvija guru prājñānām pūjanam śaucam tīrtha snāna ādikam ārjavam vṛttam brahmacaryam yoṣitsu bhogya yukta īkṣaṇa rahita ahiṃsā aprāṇi pīḍā etad tapa ucyate pareṣām anudvega karam satyam hitam yad vākyam svādhyāya abhyasanam etad mayam tapa ucyate prasādaḥ manasaḥ krodha rahita saumya manasaḥ pareṣām abhyudaya prāvaṇyam maunam manasā pravṛtti niyamanam vinigrahaḥ vṛtteḥ dhyeya viṣaye avasthāpanam śuddhiḥ vyatirikta viṣaya cintā rahita etad mānasam tapaḥ aphala ākāṅkṣibhiḥ ākāṅkṣā rahitaiḥ yuktaiḥ parama ārādhana rūpam idam cintā yuktaiḥ naraiḥ parayā śraddhayā yad trividham tapaḥ kāya manobhiḥ taptam sāttvikam paricakṣate manasā ādaraḥ satkāraḥ vācā praśaṃsā mānaḥ śarīraḥ namaskāra pūjā abhisandhi pūrvakam satkāra dambhena hetunā yad tapaḥ kriyate rājasam proktam svarga sādhana asthira tvā at calam adhruvam cala pāta bhayena calana adhruva kṣayiṣṇu mūḍhāḥ avivekinaḥ mūḍha grāheṇa mūḍhaiḥ kṛtena abhiniveśena ādikam aparīkṣya pīḍayā yad tapaḥ kriyate utsādana yad kriyate tāmasam udāhṛtam abhisandhiḥ ahitam dātavyam deśe kāle pātre anupakāriṇe yad dānam dīyate dānam sāttvikam smṛtam pratyupakāra kaṭākṣa garbham uddiśya parikliṣṭam akalyāṇa dravya kam yad dānam dīyate rājasam udāhṛtam adeśa kāle apātrebhyaḥ yad dānam dīyate asatkṛtam prakṣālana gaurava rahitam avajñātam avajñam anupacāra yuktam yad dīyate tāmasam udāhṛtam om sat trividhaḥ ayam nirdeśaḥ brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ brahmaṇaḥ anvayī bhavati vedaḥ veda śabdena vaidikam ucyate vaidikam ādikam ādikam om sat anvitam bhavati om anvayaḥ vaidika prayoga ādau prayujyamāna sat śabdayoḥ anvayaḥ pūjya tvāya vācakatayā tena trividhena śabdena anvitā brāhmaṇāḥ vedān vayinaḥ traivarṇikāḥ vedāḥ yajñāḥ purā vihitāḥ purā mayā nirmitā tasmāt vādinām veda ādinām traivarṇikānām dāna tapaḥ kriyāḥ vidhāna uktāḥ veda vidhāna uktāḥ ādau om udāhṛtya satatam sarvadā pravartante vedāḥ om udāhṛtya ārabhyante vedānām vaidikānām ādīnām karmaṇām om anvayaḥ varṇitaḥ om anvita veda dhāraṇāt anvita karaṇa āt brāhmaṇa nirdiṣṭānām traivarṇikānām om anvayaḥ varṇitaḥ anabhisandhāya veda tapaḥ dāna kriyāḥ kāṅkṣibhiḥ traivarṇikaiḥ yāḥ kriyante prāpti sādhana vācinā śabdena nirdeśyāḥ vaḥ kaḥ kim yad padam anuttamam vācī prasiddhaḥ veda ādīnām sādhana bhūtānām nirdeśya anvaya uktaḥ traivarṇikānām tathāvidha veda adhyaya anuṣṭhānāt anvaya sadbhāve vidyamāna tāyām sādhu kalyāṇa vastuṣu sat etad padam prayujyate vedayoḥ kenacid puruṣeṇa anuṣṭhite laukike praśaste kalyāṇe sat idam sat yujyate prayujyate ataḥ vaidikānām traivarṇikānām yajñe tapasi dāne sthitiḥ kalyāṇa sat ucyate arthīyam traivarṇikā arthīyam dāna ādikam sat abhidhīyate tasmāt vedāḥ vaidikāni karmāṇi brāhmaṇa nirdiṣṭāḥ traivarṇikāḥ om sat anvaya lakṣaṇena avedebhyaḥ vaidikebhyaḥ vyāvṛttā veditavyāḥ aśraddhayā kṛtam śāstrī iyam homa ādikam asad ucyate kutaḥ pretya naḥ mokṣāya sāṃsārikāya phalāya tyāga saṃnyāsau sādhana vihitau karmaṇā prajayā dhanena tyāgena ānaśuḥ su niścita aḥ saṃnyāsa yatayaḥ śuddha sattvāḥ kāle amṛtāt parimucyanti kecana vidvāṃsaḥ kāmyānām karmaṇām nyāsam tyāgam saṃnyāsam viduḥ kecid vicakṣaṇāḥ nityānām naimittikānām kāmyānām karmaṇām tyāga śāstreṣu tyāga prāhuḥ śāstrīya tyāgaḥ kāmya viṣayaḥ viṣaya vivādam pradarśayan ekatra saṃnyāsa tyāga prayuktavān ataḥ tyāga saṃnyāsa śabdayoḥ aṅgīkṛtam jñāyate niścayam śṛṇu me tyāge bharata sattama tyāga śabdena nirṇaya niyatasya saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇaḥ mohāt parityāgaḥ tāmasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ manīṣiṇaḥ kāpilāḥ vaidikāḥ mata anusāriṇaḥ rāga doṣavat bandhaka sarvam ādikam mumukṣuṇā tyājyam prāhuḥ apare paṇḍitāḥ ādikam tyājyam prāhuḥ vādi vipratipanne tyāge tyāga viṣayam niścayam matta ḥ śṛṇu tyāgaḥ kriyamāṇa iṣu vaidikeṣu karmasu viṣaya viṣaya viṣaya mayā trividhaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ mayi karmāṇi saṃnyasya cetasā nirāśīḥ nirmamaḥ bhūtvā yuddhi asva vigata jvaraḥ janyam svarga ādikam mama tyāgaḥ madīya sādhana madīyam idam mamatāyāḥ parityāgaḥ viṣaya ḥ tyāgaḥ īśvare saṃdhānena tyāgaḥ viṣaya ḥ tyāgaḥ dāna tapaḥ prabhṛtīni varṇa āśrama saṃbandhīni karmāṇi manīṣiṇām manana śīlānām pāvanāni mananam upāsanam mumukṣūṇām yāvajjīvam upāsanam kurvatām upāsana niṣpatti virodhi prācīna vināśanā ni yasmān manīṣiṇām dāna tapaḥ prabhṛtīni pāvanāni tasmāt upāsanavat etāni karmāṇi mad ārādhana rūpāṇi saṅgam mamatām phalāni tyaktvā aharahar āprayāṇa at upāsana nivṛttaye mumukṣuṇā kartavyā ani mama niścitam uttamam matam niyatasya naimittikasya mahāyajña ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ saṃnyāsaḥ tyāgaḥ yātrā tena prasiddhyet akarmaṇaḥ yātrāyāḥ yātrā aśanena nirvartyamānā samyak jñānāya prabhavati agham bhuñjate pāpāḥ ayajña agha āpyāyanam manasaḥ viparīta jñānāya bhavati anna mayam somya annena mana āpyāyateāhāra śuddhau sattva śuddhi ḥ sattva śuddhau dhruvā smṛtiḥ lambhe granthīnām vipramokṣaḥ yadi paraṃparayā sādhana duḥkha dravya arjana sādhya bahu āyāsa kāya kleśa kara manasaḥ avasāda karam bhītyā yoga niṣpattaye abhyāsa yatanīya yaḥ mahāyajña āśrama parityajet rājasam rajaḥ mūlam tyāgam kṛtvā ayathā avasthita rūpam rūpam tyāga labhate ayathāvat prajānāti ḥ pārtha rājasī vakṣyate dvāreṇa prasāda hetuḥ bhava gad prasāda dvāreṇa naimittika mahā varṇa āśrama vihitam mad ārādhana svayaṃprayojanam matvā saṅgam mamatām tyaktvā yad kriyate tyāgaḥ sāttvikaḥ mataḥ sattva mūlaḥ avasthita sattvam avasthita vastu jñānam utpādayati sattva at saṃjāyate jñānam vakṣyate pravṛttim nivṛttim akāryam bhaya abhaye bandham mokṣam yā vetti buddhiḥ pārtha sāttvikī sattva samāviṣṭaḥ medhāvī avasthita tattva jñānaḥ tataḥ cchinna saṃśayaḥ saṅga tyāgī dveṣṭy akuśalam śukale anuṣajjate akuśalam kuśalam svarga paśu annādya sarvasmin mamatā rahita tyakta vyatirikta tyakta āc tayoḥ kriyamāṇayoḥ prīti dveṣau karoti pāpam atra prāma ādikam abhipretam virataḥ duścaritān śāntaḥ samāhitaḥ aśa mānasaḥ prajñānena āpnuyāt dehabhṛtā dhriyamāṇa śarīreṇa karmāṇi aśeṣataḥ tyaktum śakyam arthānām pāna ādīnām anubandhinām karmaṇām avarjanīya mahāyajña anuṣṭhānam avarjanīyam yaḥ teṣu mahāyajña karmasu tyāgī tyāgena ānaśuḥ ityādi śāstreṣu tyāgī abhidhīyate tyāgī pradarśana saṅgānām tyāgī trividhaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ prakramāt aniṣṭam naraka iṣṭam svarga miśram saṃbhinnam paśu annādya etad trividham karmaṇaḥ atyāginām amatā tyāga rahitānām pretya bhavati pretya anuṣṭhāna kālam saṃnyāsinām kvacid parityāginām kvacid virodhi bhavati etad bhavati yadi hotra mahā ādīni jīvana adhikārayoḥ iva adhikāre viniyoga pṛthaktvena parihriyate viniyoga ḥ tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇā vividiṣanti yajñena dānena tapasā anāśakena ityādibhiḥ kriyamāṇa iṣu karmasu parityāgaḥ saṃnyāsaḥ tyāga uktaḥ % sāṃkhyā buddhiḥ sāṃkhye kṛtānte avasthita tattva viṣayayā vaidikyā buddhyā anusaṃhite nirṇaye karmaṇām siddhaye utpattaye proktāni etāni kāraṇāni nibodhe me mama sakāśāt anusaṃdhatsva vaidikī buddhiḥ indriya upakaraṇam paramātmānam kartāram avadhārayati ya tiṣṭhan antaraḥ yam veda yasya ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati ta amṛtaḥ antaḥ praviṣṭaḥ śāstā janānām ityādiṣu idam pṛthagvidham vividhā ceṣṭā daivam atra pañcamam manobhiḥ yad prārabhate naraḥ nyāyyam viparītam hetavaḥ nyāyye siddhe viparīte pratiṣiddhe sarvasmin vācike mānase hetavaḥ adhiṣṭhīyate mahābhūta saṃghāta rūpam jīvātmā jñātṛ ata sūtra upapāditam pṛthagvidham pāṇi pañcakam manaskam karmendriyam pṛthagvidham niṣpattau vyāpāram vividhā ceṣṭā ceṣṭā śabdena vāyuḥ abhidhīyate vṛtti vācinā indriya dhāraṇasya apāna bhinnasya vāyoḥ vividhā ceṣṭā vividhā daivam atra pañcamam atra kalāpe daivam pañcamam paramātmā antaryāmī niṣpattau hetuḥ sarvasya aham sanniviṣṭaḥ mattaḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam apohanam vakṣyati īśvaraḥ bhūtānām hṛd deśe arjuna tiṣṭhati bhrāmayan bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā paramātmā āyattam jīvātmanaḥ ityādi upapāditam nanu paramātmā āyatte jīvātmanaḥ tve jīvātmā aniyojyaḥ bhavati niṣedha śāstrāṇi anarthakāni syuḥ idam codyam sūtrakāreṇa parihṛtam vaiya arthyādibhyaḥ etad bhavati parama dattaiḥ ādhāraiḥ karaṇa kalebara ādibhiḥ āhita śaktibhiḥ svayam jīvātmā ādhāra ḥ āhita ḥ san niṣpattaye icchayā karaṇa ākāram prayatnam ārabhate ava sthitaḥ paramātmā anum dānena tam pravartayati jīvasya buddhyā pravṛtti gurutara śilā mahīruha cala pravṛttiṣu bahu sādhyāsu bahūnām niṣedha kartāram ātmānam kevalam yaḥ paśyati akṛtabuddhi tvān paśyati durmatiḥ vastutaḥ paramātma anumati pūrvake jīvātmanaḥ tve kevalam ātmānam kartāram yaḥ paśyati durmatiḥ viparīta matiḥ akṛtabuddhi aniṣpanna avasthita vastu tvān paśyati avasthitam kartāram paśyati yasya ahaṃkṛtaḥ buddhiḥ yasya lipyate hatvā imān lokān hanti nibadhyate parama anusaṃdhānena yasya viṣayaḥ vṛtti viśeṣaḥ ahaṃkṛtaḥ ham abhimāna kṛtaḥ aham karomi jñānam yasya vidyata buddhiḥ yasya lipyate mama etad mayā saṃbadhyate madīyam yasya buddhiḥ jāyata imān lokān yuddhe hatvā tān nihanti kevalam bhīṣma ādīn tataḥ tena yuddha ākhyena karmaṇā nibadhyate anubhavati sarvam idam akartṛ sandhānam sattva vṛddhyā bhavati sattvasya upādeya ājñāpanāya sattva kṛtam vaiṣamyam prapañcayiṣyan codanā prakāram tāvat jñānam jñeyam parijñātā trividhā codanā kāraṇam trividhaḥ saṃgrahaḥ jñānam kartavya viṣayam jñānam jñeyam kartavyam parijñātā boddha trividhā codanā bodha boddha vya boddhṛ yuktaḥ jyotiṣṭoma boddhavya rūpam trividham saṃgṛhyate sādhana dravya ādikam yāga ādikam anuṣṭhātā jñānam tridhā bhedataḥ procyate saṃkhyāne avac śṛṇu kartavya viṣayam jñānam anuṣṭhīyamānam anuṣṭhātā sattva bhedataḥ trividhā procyate saṃkhyāne gaṇane avac śṛṇu guṇataḥ bhinnāni ādīni avac śṛṇu yena ekam avyayam īkṣate avibhaktam vibhakteṣu jñānam viddhi sāttvikam brāhmaṇa kṣatri ya brahmacāri gṛhastha rūpeṇa vibhakteṣu sarveṣu adhikāriṣu yena jñānena ekam ākhyam avibhaktam brāhmaṇa ākāreṣu sita vibhāgavatsu ākāre vibhāga rahitam avyayam vyaya svabhāva iṣu brāhmaṇa śarīreṣu avyayam avikṛtam saṅgān arham velāyām īkṣate jñānam sāttvikam viddhi pṛthaktvena yaj jñānam bhāvān pṛthagvidhān vetti sarveṣu jñānam viddhi rājasam sarveṣu brāhmaṇa brāhmaṇa ākāra pṛthaktvena ākhyān bhāvān bhūtān sita pṛthaktvena pṛthagvidhān saṃyoga yogyān velāyām yaj jñānam vetti jñānam rājasam viddhi yad kṛtsnavat saktam ahetukam atattva alpam tāmasam udāhṛtam yad jñānam kartavye preta gaṇa ārādhana rūpe phale phalavat saktam ahetukam vastu akṛt sna phalavat tathāvidha saṅga rahitam atattva yukta mithyā viṣayam preta ārādhana viṣaya alpam jñānam tāmasam udāhṛtam kartavya viṣaya jñānasya velāyām adhikārī aṃśena guṇataḥ traividhyam uktvā anuṣṭheyasya karmaṇaḥ guṇataḥ traividhyam niyatam saṅga rahitam arāga dveṣataḥ kṛtam aphala prepsunā yad sāttvikam ucyate niyatam varṇa āśrama ucitam saṅga rahitam saṅga rahitam arāga dveṣataḥ kṛtam kīrti rāgāt akīrti dveṣā c kṛtam adambhena kṛtam aphala prepsunā aphala abhisandhinā kṛtam yad sāttvikam ucyate yad īpsunā ahaṅkāreṇa punar kriyate bahula āyāsam rājasam udāhṛtam yad punar īpsunā prepsunā ahaṃkāreṇa ḥ arthe abhimāna yuktena bahula āyāsam yad kriyate rājasam bahula āyāsam idam mayā kriyata evaṃrūpa abhimāna yuktena yad kriyate rājasam anubandham kṣayam hiṃsām anavekṣya pauruṣam mohāt ārabhyate yad tāmasam ucyate kṛte anubadhyamānam duḥkham kṣayaḥ kriyamāṇe vināśaḥ hiṃsā prāṇi pīḍā pauruṣam samāpana sāmarthyam etāni anavekṣya avimṛśya mohāt parama ajñānāt yad ārabhyate tāmasam ucyate saṅgaḥ anahaṃvā ādī dhṛti utsāha samanvitaḥ siddhi asiddhyoḥ nirvikāraḥ sāttvika ucyate saṅgaḥ saṅga rahitaḥ anahaṃvādī abhimāna rahitaḥ dhṛti utsāha samanvitaḥ ārabdhe yāvat samāpti varjanīya duḥkha dhāraṇam dhṛtiḥ utsāhaḥ udyukta tābhyām samanvitaḥ siddhi asiddhyoḥ nirvikāraḥ yuddha ādau upakaraṇa dravya arjana siddhi asiddhyoḥ avikṛta cittaḥ sāttvika ucyate ragī prepsuḥ lubdhaḥ hiṃsā ātmakaḥ aśuciḥ harṣa śoka anvitaḥ rājasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ rāgī yaśaḥ arthī prepsuḥ arthī lubdhaḥ apekṣita dravya vyaya svabhāva rahitaḥ hiṃsā ātmakaḥ parān pīḍayitvā taiḥ kurvāṇaḥ aśuciḥ apekṣita śuddhi rahitaḥ harṣa śoka anvitaḥ yuddha ādau jaya siddhi siddhyoḥ harṣa śoka anvitaḥ rājasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ayuktaḥ prākṛtaḥ stabdhaḥ śaṭhaḥ naikṛti kaḥ alasaḥ viṣa ādī dīrghasūtrī tāmasa ucyate ayuktaḥ śāstrīya yogyaḥ vikarma sthaḥ prākṛtaḥ anadhigata vidyaḥ stabdhaḥ anārambha śīlaḥ śaṭhaḥ abhicāra ruciḥ naikṛtikaḥ vañcana alasaḥ ārabdha iṣu karmasu manda pravṛttiḥ viṣa ādī atimātra avasāda śīlaḥ dīrghasūtrī abhicāra kurvan pareṣu kāla varti anartha paryālocana śīlaḥ evaṃbhūtaḥ yaḥ tāmasaḥ kartavya viṣaya jñāne kartavye anuṣṭhātari guṇataḥ traividhyam idānīm tattva niścaya rūpāyāḥ buddheḥ guṇataḥ traividhyam buddheḥ bhedam iva guṇataḥ trividham śṛṇu procyamānam aśeṣeṇa pṛthaktvena dhanaṃjaya buddhiḥ viveka pūrvakam niścaya rūpam jñānam dhṛtiḥ ārabdhāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ vighna upanipāte dhāraṇam tayoḥ sattva guṇataḥ trividham bhedam pṛthaktvena procyamānam avac śṛṇu pravṛttim nivṛttim akārye bhaya abhaye bandham mokṣam yā vetti buddhiḥ pārtha sāttvikī pravṛttiḥ abhyudaya sādhana bhūtaḥ dharmaḥ nivṛttiḥ sādhana bhūtaḥ tav ubhau avasthitau yā buddhiḥ vetti akārye varṇānām pravṛtti nivṛtti dharmayoḥ niṣṭhānām deśa kāla viśeṣeṣu idam idam akāryam yā vetti bhaya abhaye ativṛttiḥ bhaya sthānam anuvṛttiḥ abhaya sthānam bandham mokṣam yāthātmyam vigamayāthātmyam yā vetti sāttvikī buddhiḥ adharmam ayathāvat prajānāti buddhiḥ pārtha rājasī dvividham viparītam niṣṭhānām deśa kāla yathāvan jānāti rājasī buddhiḥ adharmam yā manyate tamasā āvṛtā arthān viparītān buddhiḥ pārtha tāmasī tāmasī buddhiḥ tamasā āvṛtā satī arthān viparītān manyate adharmam santam asantam asantam santam tattvam aparam aparam tattvam sarvam viparītam manyata dhṛtyā yayā dhārayate indriya kriyāḥ yogena avyabhicāriṇyā dhṛtiḥ pārtha sāttvikī yayā dhṛtyā yogena avyabhicāriṇyā indriyāṇām kriyāḥ puruṣaḥ dhārayate sādhana bhagavat upāsanam yogena bhūtena avyabhicāriṇyā yoga uddeśena pravṛttā aḥ sādhana bhūtāḥ prabhṛtīnām kriyāḥ yayā dhṛtyā dhārayate sāttvikī yayā arthān dhṛtyā dhārayate arjuna prasaṅgena ākāṅkṣī dhṛtiḥ pārtha rājasī ākāṅkṣī puruṣaḥ prakṛṣṭa saṅgena arthān yayā dhṛtyā dhārayate rājasī śabdena sādhana bhūtāḥ indriya lakṣyante ākāṅkṣi atra śabdena rāja satvāt vivakṣitāḥ ataḥ prabhṛtīnām yayā dhṛtyā dhārayate rājasi bhavati yayā svapnam bhayam śokam viṣādam madam vimuñcati durmedhā dhṛtiḥ pārtha tāmasī yayā dhṛtyā svapnam nidrām madam viṣaya anubhava janitam madam madav uddiśya pravṛttā ādīnām kriyāḥ durmedhā vimuñcati dhārayati bhaya śoka viṣāda āḥ bhaya śoka dāyi viṣaya parāḥ sādhana bhūtāḥ yayā dhārayate dhṛtiḥ tāmasī sukham idānīm trividham śṛṇu me bharata ṛṣabha uktāḥ yad cheṣa bhūtāḥ sukham guṇataḥ trividham idānīm śṛṇu ramate duḥkhāntam nigacchati yad agre viṣam iva pariṇāme upamam sukham sāttvikam proktam prasāda jam yasmin sukhe cira kāla niratiśayām ratim prāpnoti duḥkhāntam nigacchati nikhilasya sāṃsārikasya duḥkhasya antam nigacchati viśinaṣṭi yad sukham agre yoga upakrama velāyām bahu āyāsa sādhya vivikta svarūpasya ananubhūta viṣam iva duḥkham iva bhavati pariṇāme upamam pariṇāme vipāke abhyāsa balena vivikta āvirbhāve upamam bhavati prasāda jam viṣayā buddhiḥ buddhiḥ tasyāḥ nivṛtta sakala viṣaya prasādaḥ nivṛtta sakala viṣaya buddhyā vivikta svabhāva anubhava janitam sukham upamam bhavati sukham sāttvikam proktam viṣaya indriya saṃyoga at yad agre upamam pariṇāme viṣam iva sukham rājasam smṛtam agre anubhava velāyām viṣaya indriya saṃyoga at yad amṛtam iva bhavati pariṇāme vipāke viṣayāṇām kṣudh ādau nivṛtte sukhasya niraya viṣam iva pītam bhavati sukham rājasam smṛtam yad agre anubandhe sukham mohanam nidrā ālasya pramāda uttham tāmasam udāhṛtam yad sukham agre anubandhe anubhava velāyām vipāke mohanam moha hetuḥ bhavati mohaḥ atra avasthita vastu abhipretaḥ nidrā ālasya pramāda uttham nidrā ālasya pramāda janitam nidrā anubhava velāyām moha hetavaḥ nidrāyāḥ moha spṛṣṭam ālasyam indriya vyāpāram āndyam indriya vyāpāram āndye jñānam āndyam bhavati pramādaḥ kṛtyān avadhāna jñānam āndyam bhavati tataḥ tayoḥ moha sukham tāmasam udāhṛtam ataḥ mumukṣuṇā rajaḥ tamasī abhibhūya sattvam upādeyam bhavati pṛthivyām divi deveṣu punar sattvam prakṛti jaiḥ muktam yad ebhiḥ tribhiḥ guṇaiḥ pṛthivyām divi deveṣu prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭeṣu sthāvara anteṣu prakṛti jaiḥ ebhiḥ tribhiḥ guṇaiḥ muktam yad sattvam prāṇi jātam tyāgena ānaśuḥ ityādiṣu sādhana nirdiṣṭaḥ tyāgaḥ saṃnyāsa arthāt ananyaḥ kriyamāṇa iṣu karmasu tyāga mūlaḥ karmaṇā ūḥ tyāgaḥ tyāgaḥ parama puruṣe saṃdhānena etad sarvam sattva sattva upādeyata ājñāpanāya sattva rajaḥ tamasām bhedāḥ prapañcitāḥ idānīm evaṃbhūtasya sādhana kriyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥ parama ārādhana veṣatām anuṣṭhitasya karmaṇaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇam pratipādayitum brāhmaṇa adhikāriṇām svabhāva anubandhi sattva bhinnam vṛttyā kartavya svarūpam brāhmaṇa viśām śūdrāṇām paraṃtapa karmāṇi pravibhaktāni svabhāva prabhavaiḥ guṇaiḥ brāhmaṇa viśām svakīyaḥ svabhāvaḥ brāhmaṇa prācīnakarma prabhavāḥ sattva āt ayaḥ guṇāḥ brāhmaṇasya svabhāva prabhavaḥ rajaḥ tamaḥ abhibhavena udbhūtaḥ sattva guṇaḥ kṣatriyasya svabhāva prabhavaḥ tamaḥ sattva abhibhavena udbhūtaḥ rajaḥ guṇaḥ vaiśyasya svabhāva prabhavaḥ sattva rajaḥ abhibhavena udrikta ḥ tamaḥ guṇaḥ śūdrasya svabhāva prabhavaḥ rajaḥ sattva abhibhavena udrikta ḥ tamaḥ guṇaḥ ebhiḥ svabhāva prabhavaiḥ guṇaiḥ pravibhaktāni karmāṇi śāstraiḥ pratipāditāni brāhmaṇa ādaya evaṃguṇakāḥ etāni karmāṇi vṛttayaḥ etāḥ vibhajya pratipādayanti śāstrāṇi śamaḥ damaḥ tapaḥ śaucam kṣāntiḥ ārjavam jñānam vijñānam āstikyam brāhmam svabhāva jam śamaḥ bāhya indriya niyamanam damaḥ antaḥkaraṇa niyamanam tapaḥ niyamana rūpaḥ siddhaḥ kāya kleśaḥ śaucam śāstrī ya yogya kṣāntiḥ paraiḥ pīḍyamānasya avikṛta citta ārjavam pareṣu anurūpam bāhya ceṣṭā prakāśanam jñānam parāvara tattva yāthātmya jñānam vijñānam tattva gata asā viṣayam jñānam āstikyam vaidikasya kṛtsnasya niścayaḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ kena hetunā cālayitum aśakya bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ vāsudevaḥ abhideyaḥ nirasta nikhila gandhaḥ svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya saṅkhyeya kalyāṇa gaṇaḥ nikhila veda vedyaḥ nikhila kāraṇam nikhila ādhāra bhūtaḥ nikhilasya pravartayitā ārādhana vaidikam kṛtsnam taiḥ taiḥ ārādhitaḥ ākhyam prayacchati arthasya niścaya āstikyam vedaiḥ sarvaiḥ aham vedyaḥ aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate mayi sarvam idam protam bhoktāram tapasām jñātvā mām śāntim ṛcchati mattaḥ parataram anyat kiñcid dhanañjaya yataḥ pravṛttiḥ bhūtānām yena sarvam idam tatam karmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mānavaḥ yaḥ mām ajam anādim vetti maheśvaram ucyate etad brāhmaṇasya svabhāva jam śairyam dhṛtiḥ dākṣyam yuddhe apalāyanam dānam īśvara kṣātram svabhāva jam śairyam yuddhe nirbhaya praveśa sāmarthyam paraiḥ anabhibhavanī ya dhṛtiḥ ārabdhe vighna upanipāte samāpana sāmarthyam dākṣyam nirvṛtti sāmarthyam yuddhe apalāyanam yuddhe maraṇa niścaye anirvartanam dānam ātmīyasya dhanasya āpādana paryanta ḥ tyāgaḥ īśvara vyatirikta sakala jana niyamana sāmarthyam etad kṣatriyasya svabhāva jam kṛṣi gorakṣya vāṇijyam vaiśyam svabhāva jam kṛṣiḥ utpādanam karṣaṇam gorakṣyam paśu pālanam vāṇijyam dhana sañcaya kraya vikraya ātmakam etad vaiśyasya svabhāva jam paricaryā ātmakam śūdrasya svabhāva jam varṇa traya paricaryā rūpam śūdrasya svabhāva jam etad caturṇā varṇānām vṛttibhiḥ kartavyānām vihitānām karmaṇām pradarśana varṇānām sādhāraṇāḥ varṇānām mumukṣūṇām sādhāraṇāḥ brāhmaṇasya sattva udrekasya svābhāvika upādānā kṛtvā ādaya svabhāva jam vaiśyayoḥ svataḥ rajaḥ tamaḥ dam duḥkha upādānā kṛtvā brāhmaṇasya yājana adhyāpana pratigrahāḥ kṣatriyasya janapada paripālanam vaiśyasya kṛṣi uktāḥ śūdrasya kartavyam varṇa traya paricaryā sve sve abhirataḥ saṃsiddhim labhate naraḥ nirataḥ siddhim vindati śṛṇu sve sve udite abhirataḥ naraḥ saṃsiddhim parama pada prāptim labhate nirataḥ siddhim vindati parama padam prāpnoti śṛṇu yataḥ pravṛttiḥ bhūtānām yena sarvam idam tatam karmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mānavaḥ yataḥ bhūtānām ādikā pravṛttiḥ yena sarvam idam tatam karmaṇā tam mām indra avasthitam abhyarcya mad prasādān mad prāpti rūpām siddhim vindati mānavaḥ matta sarvam utpadyate mayā sarvam idam tatam aham kṛtsnasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayaḥ mattaḥ parataram anyat kiṃcid dhanañjaya mayā tatam idam sarvam jagad avyakta mūrtinā mayā sūyate sacarācaram aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate ityādiṣu śreyān svadharmaḥ viguṇaḥ dharmāt su anuṣṭhitāt tyakta ādikaḥ mad ārādhana rūpaḥ svadharmaḥ upādātum yogyaḥ dharmaḥ prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭena puruṣeṇa indriya rūpaḥ yoga ātmakaḥ dharmaḥ sukaraḥ bhavati ataḥ yoga ākhyaḥ svadharmaḥ viguṇaḥ dharmāt indriya jaya nipuṇa dharmāj sakala indriya niyamana pramādāt kadācid su anuṣṭhitāt śreyān upapādayati svabhāva niyatam kurvan āpnoti kilbiṣam prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya puruṣasya indriya svabhāvata niyata karmaṇaḥ kurvan kilbiṣam saṃsāram prāpnoti apramāda karmaṇaḥ yogasya sakala indriya niyamana sādhya pramāda niṣṭhaḥ pramādāt kilbiṣam pratipadyeta ataḥ niṣṭhā jyāyasi tṛtīyā adhyāya smārayati sahajam kaunteya doṣam tyajet ārambhā doṣeṇa dhūmena agniḥ iva āvṛtāḥ ataḥ sahaja sukaram apramādam doṣam duḥkham tyajet yoga yogyaḥ kurvīta ārambhāḥ ārambhāḥ ārambhāḥ doṣeṇa duḥkhena dhūmena agniḥ iva āvṛtāḥ iyāṃ viśeṣaḥ sukaraḥ apramādaḥ yoga ḥ viparītaḥ asakta ḥ jita vigata spṛhaḥ naiṣkarmya siddhim paramām saṃnyāsena adhigacchati asakta buddhiḥ jita jita manāḥ parama anusaṃdhānena tve vigata spṛhaḥ tyāgāt nirṇītena saṃnyāsena yuktaḥ kurvan paramām naiṣkarmya siddhim adhigacchati paramām dhyāna niṣṭhām yogasya adhigacchati vakṣyamāṇa dhyāna yoga avāptim indriya uparati rūpām adhigacchati siddhim prāptaḥ āpnoti nibodha me samāsena kaunteya niṣṭhā jñānasya yā parā siddhim prāptaḥ āprayāṇa at hara har anuṣṭhīyamāna yoga niṣpādya dhyāna sidddhim prāptaḥ yena prakāreṇa vartamānaḥ prāpnoti samāsena me nibodha viśeṣyate niṣṭhā jñānasya yā jñānasya dhyāna ātmakasya yā parā niṣṭhā parama prāpyam buddhyā viśuddhayā yuktaḥ dhṛti ātmānam niyamya ādīn viṣayān tyaktvā rāga dveṣau vyudasya vivikta sevī laghu āśī yatavāk kāya mānasaḥ dhyāna yoga vairāgyam samupāśritaḥ ahaṅkāram balam darpam kāmam krodham parigraham vimucya nirmamaḥ śāntaḥ bhūyāya kalpate buddhyā viśuddhayā avasthita tattva viṣayayā yuktaḥ dhṛtyā ātmānam niyamya viṣaya vimukhīkaraṇena yoga yogyam kṛtvā ādīn viṣayān tyaktvā asannihitān kṛtvā nimittau rāga dveṣau vyudasya vivikta sevī sarvaiḥ dhyāna virodhibhiḥ vivikte deśe vartamānaḥ laghu āśī ana śana rahitaḥ yatavāk kāya mānasaḥ dhyāna abhimukhīkṛta kāya dhyāna yoga evaṃbhūta ḥ san prāyāṇa at aharahar dhyāna yoga vairāgyam samupāśritaḥ dhyeya tattva vyatirikta viṣaya avamarśena virāga tām vardhayan ahaṃkāram anātmani abhimānam balam vāsana balam nimittam darpam kāmam krodham parigraham vimucya nirmamaḥ sarveṣu anātmīya iṣu ātmīya rahitaḥ śāntaḥ bhava sukhaḥ evaṃbhūtaḥ dhyāna kurvan bhūyāya kalpate vinirmuktaḥ avasthitam ātmānam anubhavati bhūtaḥ prasanna śocati kāṅkṣati samaḥ sarveṣu mad bhaktim labhate parām bhūtaḥ paricchinna ākāra mat ta svabhāva itaḥ anyām prakṛtim viddhi me parām su śa iṣa uktā prasanna kleśa ādibhiḥ akaluṣa mad vyatiriktam kaṃcana śocati kiṃcana kāṅkṣati mad vyatirikteṣu sarveṣu anādaraṇīya tāyām samaḥ nikhilam vastu jātam tṛṇavan manyamānaḥ mad bhaktim labhate parām mayi īśvare nikhila udbhava pralaya līle nirasta samasta gandhe anavadhika atiśaya saṃkhyeya kalyāṇa gaṇa aika tāne lāvaṇya sāgare śrīmati puṇḍarīka nayane svāmini atyartha anubhava rūpām parām bhaktim labhate bhaktyā mām abhijānāti yāvān yaḥ asmi tattvataḥ tataḥ mām tattvataḥ jñātvā viśate anantaram svarūpataḥ svabhāvataḥ yaḥ aham guṇataḥ vibhūtitaḥ yāvān ḥ aham tam mām evaṃrūpayā bhaktyā tattvataḥ abhijānāti mām tattvataḥ jñātvā anantaram tattva anantaram tataḥ bhaktitaḥ mām viśate praviśati tattvataḥ svabhāva vibhūti darśana kāla bhāvinyā anavadhika atiśaya bhaktyā mām prāpnoti atra tataḥ prāpti nirdiṣṭā bhaktiḥ abhidhīyate bhaktyā ananyayā śakyaḥ tattvataḥ praveśa varṇa ucita naimittika karmaṇām parityakta ādikānām parama ārādhana rūpeṇa anuṣṭhitānām vipāka uktaḥ idānīm kāmyānām karmaṇām uktena prakāreṇa anuṣṭhitānām vipāka karmāṇi sadā kurvāṇaḥ mad mad prasādāt avāpnoti śāśvatam padam avyayam kevalam naimittikāni karmāṇi kāmyāni karmāṇi mad vyāśrayaḥ mayi saṃnyasta ādikaḥ kurvāṇaḥ mad prasādāt chāśvatam padam avyayam avikalam prāpnoti padyate gamyata padam mām prāpnoti yasmāt tasmāt cetasā karmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya mad upāśritya mad citta ḥ satatam bhava cetasā madīya anniyāmya buddhyā mayi karmāṇi saṃnyasya cetasā karmāṇi kartṛkāṇi sārādhyāni mayi saṃnyasya mad aham prāpya anusaṃdhānaḥ karmāṇi kurvan imam upāśritya satatam mad cittaḥ bhava mad cittaḥ durgāṇi mad prasādāt tariṣyasi ahaṃkārān śroṣyasi vinaṅkṣyasi mad cittaḥ karmāṇi kurvan sāṃsārikāṇi durgāṇi mad prasādāt tariṣyasi ahaṃkārāt aham kṛtyā kṛtya viṣayam sarvam jānāmi bhāvān mad śroṣyasi vinaṅkṣyasi vinaṣṭaḥ bhaviṣyasi kaścid mad vyatiriktaḥ kṛtsnasya prāṇi jātasya kṛtyā ākṛtyayoḥ jñātā praśāsitā yadi ahaṅkāram āśritya yotsya manyase mithyā eṣa vyavasāya ḥ tvām niyokṣyati yadi ahaṃkāram hita ahita jñāne svātantrya abhimānam āśritya mad niyogam anādṛtya yotsya manyase eṣa svātantrya vyavasāyaḥ mithyā bhaviṣyati yataḥ tvām yuddhe niyokṣyati mad svātantrya udvignam tvām ajñam niyokṣati upapādayati svabhāva jena kaunteya nibaddhaḥ karmaṇā kartum icchasi yad mohāt kariṣyasi avaśaḥ svabhāva jam kṣatriyasya śauryam svabhāva jena śaurya ākhyena karmaṇā nibaddhaḥ avaśaḥ paraiḥ dharṣaṇam asahamāna ḥ yuddham kariṣyasi yad idānīm mohāt ajñānāt kartum icchasi sarvam jātam īśvareṇa mayā anuguṇyena prakṛti anuvartane niyamitam śṛṇu īśvaraḥ bhūtānām hṛd deśe arjuna tiṣṭhati bhrāmayan bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā īśvaraḥ niyamana śīlaḥ vāsudevaḥ bhūtānām hṛd deśe sakala pravṛtti udaya pradeśe tiṣṭhati katham kim kurvan tiṣṭhati yantra ārūḍhāni bhūtāni māyayā bhrāmayan nirmitam indriya avastham prakṛti ākhyam yantram ārūḍhāni bhūtāni svakīyayā sattva mayyā māyayā anuguṇam pravartayan tiṣṭhati etad sarvasya aham sanniviṣṭaḥ mattaḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam apohanam matta ḥ sarvam pravartate ya tiṣṭhan ādikā śrutiḥ etad nivṛtti hetum tam śaraṇam gaccha bhāvena bhārata prasādāt parām śāntim sthānam prāpsyasi śāśvatam yasmāt tasmāt tam sarvasya praśāsitāram vātsalyena tvad sārathye avasthitam ittham kuru śāsitāram bhāvena śaraṇam gaccha anuvartasva preritena ajñena tvayā yuddha avarjanīyam naṣṭaḥ bhaviṣyasi ataḥ ukta prakāreṇa yuddha ādikam kurv kurvāṇaḥ prasādāt parām śāntim upaśamam śāśvatam sthānam prāpsyasi yad abhidhīyate śataiḥ viṣṇoḥ paramam padam sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ ha nākam mahimānaḥ sacante sādhyāḥ santi devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ prathama jā ye purāṇāḥ nākam nihitam guhāyām yaḥ adhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman yad ataḥ divaḥ dīpyate adhvanaḥ pāram āpnoti viṣṇoḥ paramam padam ityādibhiḥ jñānam ākhyātam guhyāt guhyataram mayā vimṛśya etad aśeṣeṇa icchasi kuru mumukṣubhiḥ adhigantavyam jñānam sarvasmāt guhyāt guhyataram yoga viṣayam yoga viṣayam bhakti yoga viṣayam sarvam ākhyātam etad aśeṣeṇa vimṛśya anurūpam icchasi kuru bhakti yatheṣṭam ātiṣṭha guhyatamam śṛṇu me paramam vacaḥ iṣṭaḥ asi me dṛḍham tataḥ vakṣyāmi hitam sarveṣu eteṣu guhyeṣu bhakti yogasya śraiṣṭhyād guhyatamam idam guhyatamam pravakṣyāmi anasūyave ādau viṣayam paramam me vacaḥ śṛṇu iṣṭaḥ asi me dṛḍham tataḥ hitam vakṣyāmi mad manā bhava mad bhaktaḥ mad yājī mām namaskuru mām eṣyasi satyam pratijāne priyaḥ asi me vedānteṣu veda aham etam mahāntam varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt tam vidvān bhavati panthā vidyate ayanāya ityādiṣu vihitam vedanam dhyāna upāsana vācyam darśana ākāram saṃtānam atyartha priyam mad manā bhava vidhīyate mad bhaktaḥ atyartha mad priyaḥ atyartha mad niratiśaya priyām saṃtatim kuruṣu mad yājī mad bhakta anuṣajyate yajanam pūjanam atyartha mada ārādhana bhava ārādhanam paripūrṇa mām namaskuru namaḥ namanam mayi atimātra prahvībhāvam atyartha priyam kurv vartamānaḥ mām eṣyasi etad satyam pratijāne tava pratijñām karomi upacchandana yataḥ priyaḥ asi me priyaḥ jñāninaḥ atyartham aham mama priyaḥ yasya mayi atimātra prītiḥ vartate mama tasmin atimātrā prītiḥ bhavati viyogam asahamānaḥ aham tam mām prāpayāmi ataḥ satyam pratijñātam mām eṣyasi dharmān parityajya mām ekam śaraṇam vraja aham tvā pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ yoga yoga bhakti yoga rūpān dharmān parama niśśreyasa sādhana bhūtān mad ārādhana atimātra prītyā adhikāram kurvāṇa ukta rītyā parityāgena parityajya mām ekam kartāram ārādhyam prāpyam upāyam saṃdhatsva eṣa dharmāṇām śastrīyaḥ parityāga niścayam śṛṇu me tyāge bharata sattama tyāgaḥ vyāghra trividhaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ ārabhya saṅgam tyaktvā iva tyāga ḥ sāttivikaḥ mataḥ dehabhṛtā śakyam tyaktum karmāṇi aśeṣataḥ yaḥ tyāgī tyāgī abhidhīyate adhyāya ādau su dṛḍham upapāditam aham tvā pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi vartamānam tvām mad prāpti virodhibhyaḥ kāla saṃcita anantā kṛtya karaṇa kṛtya rūpebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ śokam mā kṛthāḥ pāpa vinirmuktā atyartha bhagavat nirvartya bhakti yogasya ārambha virodhi pāpānām ānantyāt prāyaścitta rūpaiḥ dharmaiḥ parimita kāla kṛtaiḥ dustara bhakti yoga ārambhān arhatām ālocya śocataḥ arjunasya śokam apanudan śrī bhagavān uvāca dharmān parityajya mām ekam śaraṇam vraja bhakti yoga ārambha virodhi kāla saṃcita nānāvidha ananta pāpa anuguṇān prāyaścitta rūpān kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa kūśmāṇḍa vaiśvānara vrāta pavitra iṣṭi agniṣṭoma ādikān nānāvidhān anantān tvayā parimita kāla vartinā dūra nuṣṭhānān dharmān parityajya bhakti yoga ārambha siddhaye mām ekam parama kāruṇikam anālocita aśeṣa śaraṇyam vātsalya jaladhim śaraṇam prapadyasva aham tvā pāpebhyaḥ udita bhakti ārambha virodhibhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ idam ātapaskāya bhaktāya kadācana aśuśrūṣave vācyam mām yaḥ abhyasūyati idam paramam guhyam śāstram mayā ākhyātam atapaskāya atapta tapase tvayā vācyam tvayi vaktari mayi bhaktāya kadācana vācyam tapta tapase bhaktāya vācyam aśuśrūṣave bhaktāya aśuśrūṣave vācyam mām yaḥ abhyasūyati mad svarūpe madaiśvarye mad guṇeṣu kathiteṣu yaḥ doṣam āviṣkaroti vācyam asamāna vibhakti nirdeśaḥ atyanta pariharaṇīya ājñāpanāya ya idam paramam guhyam mad bhakteṣu abhidhāsyati bhaktim mayi parām kṛtvā mām eṣyati asaṃśayaḥ idam paramam guhyam mad bhakteṣu yaḥ abhidhāsyati vyākhyāsyati mayi paramām bhaktim kṛtvā mām eṣyati saṃśayaḥ tasmāt manuṣyeṣu kaścid me kṛttamaḥ bhavitā me tasmāt taraḥ bhuvi sarveṣu manuṣyeṣu itaḥ tasmāt manuṣyaḥ me kaścid kṛt tamaḥ abhūt ita uttaram bhavitā ayogyānām prathamam upādānam yogyānām akathanāt kathanasya aniṣṭatama adhyeṣyate ya imam dharmyam saṃvādam āvayoḥ yajñena tena aham iṣṭaḥ syām me matiḥ ya imam āvayoḥ dharmyam saṃvādam adhyeṣyate tena yajñena aham iṣṭaḥ syām me matiḥ yaḥ yajñaḥ abhidhīyate tena aham etad mātreṇa iṣṭaḥ syām śraddhāvān anasūyuḥ śṛṇuyāt yaḥ naraḥ śubhān lokān prāpnuyāt puṇya karmaṇām śraddhāvān anasūyuḥ yaḥ naraḥ śṛṇuyāt tena mātreṇa bhakti virodhi pāpebhyaḥ puṇya karmaṇām mad bhaktānām lokān samūhan prāpnuyāt kaścid etad pārtha tvayā ekāgreṇa cetasā kaccit ajñāna saṃmohaḥ pranaṣṭa ḥ dhanañjaya mayā kathitam etad pārtha tvayā avahitena cetasā kaccit tava saṃmohaḥ kaccit pranaṣṭaḥ yena ajñānena mūḍhaḥ yotsyāmi uktavān arjuna uvāca naṣṭaḥ mohaḥ smṛtiḥ labdhā tvad prasādān mayā acyuta sthitaḥ asmi gata saṃdehaḥ kariṣye vacanam tava mohaḥ viparīta jñānam tvad prasādān mama vinaṣṭam smṛtiḥ avasthita tattva jñānam tvad prasādāt labdham anātmani prakṛtau abhimāna rūpaḥ mohaḥ parama ātmakasya kṛtsnasya cit cit vastunaḥ atadātma abhimāna ḥ naimittika rūpasya karmaṇaḥ parama ārādhana prāpti upāya bandhaka rūpaḥ sarvaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ prakṛti svabhāva rahita jñātṛ svabhāva parama tan niyāmya jñānam nikhila udbhava pralaya aśeṣa pratyanīka kalyāṇa svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya balāi śvarya evaṃrūpa parāvara tattva yāthātmya abhyāsa pūrvakāhara har upacīyamāna parama prīti naimittika ka vedyaḥ parama puruṣaḥ vāsudevaḥ jñānam labdham tataḥ sneha kāruṇya pravṛddha viparīta mūlāt sarvasmāt avasādāt vimuktaḥ gata saṃdehaḥ svasthaḥ sthitaḥ asmi idānīm yuddha kartavya viṣayam tava vacanam kariṣyati yuddha ādikam kariṣyati dhṛtarāṣṭrāya putrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ yuddhe kim kariṣyanti pṛcchate sañjaya uvāca aham vāsudevasya pārthasya mahātmanaḥ saṃvādam imam aśrauṣam adbhutam roma harṣaṇam vāsudevasya vasudeva sūnoḥ pārthasya pitṛṣvasuḥ putrasya mahātmanaḥ mahābuddheḥ pada dvandvam āśritasya imam roma harṣaṇam adbhutam saṃvādam aham aśrauṣam śrutavān aham vyāsa prasāda āt chrutavān etad guhyam aham yogeśvarāt kṛṣṇāt kathayataḥ svayam vyāsa prasādāt vyāsa anugraheṇa divya śrotra lābhāt etad yoga ākhyam guhyam yoga īśva rāj balāi śvarya vīrya tejasām nidheḥ bhagavataḥ kṛṣṇāt svayam kathayataḥ śrutavān aham rājan saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya saṃvādam imam adbhutam keśava arjunayoḥ puṇyam hṛṣyāmi muhur muhur keśava arjunayoḥ imam puṇyam adbhutam saṃvādam chrutam smṛtvā muhur muhur hṛṣyāmi saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya rūpam adbhutam hareḥ vismayaḥ me mahān rājan hṛṣyāmi punar punar arjunāya prakāśitam aiśvaram hareḥ adbhutam rūpam mayā sākṣātkṛtam saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya hṛṣyataḥ me mahān vismayaḥ jāyate punar punar hṛṣyāmi kim atra bahu uktena yogeśvaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ śrīḥ vijayaḥ bhūtiḥ dhruvā nītiḥ matiḥ mama yogeśvaraḥ kṛtsnasya uccāvaca rūpeṇa avasthitasya cetanasya acetanasya vastunaḥ ye ye svabhāva yogāḥ yogānām īśvaraḥ saṃkalpa āyatta samasta vastu pravṛtti bhedaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ vasudeva sūnuḥ pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ pitṛṣvasuḥ putraḥ pada dvandva āśrayaḥ śrīḥ vijayaḥ bhūtiḥ nītiḥ dhruvā niścalā matiḥ mama
